{SaundĀ, 1}
gautamaḥ kapilo nāma munirdharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 1.1]
babhūva tapasi śrāntaḥ kākṣīvāniva gautamaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 1.2]
aśiśriyadyaḥ satataṃ dīptaṃ kāśyapavattapaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 2.1]
āśiśrāya ca tadvṛddhau siddhiṃ kāśyapavat parām | [SaundĀ, 1 2.2]
haviḥṣu yaśca svātmārthaṃ gāmadhukṣad vasiṣṭhavat | [SaundĀ, 1 3.1]
tapaḥśiṣṭeṣu ca śiṣyeṣu gāmadhukṣad vasiṣṭhavat | [SaundĀ, 1 3.2]
māhātmyāddīrghatapaso yo dvitīya ivābhavat | [SaundĀ, 1 4.1]
tṛtīya iva yaścābhūt kāvyāṅgirasayordhiyā | [SaundĀ, 1 4.2]
tasya vistīrṇatapasaḥ pārśve himavataḥ śubhe | [SaundĀ, 1 5.1]
kṣetraṃ cāyatanaṃ caiva tapasāmāśramo 'bhavat | [SaundĀ, 1 5.2]
cāruvīruttaruvanaḥ prasnigdhamṛduśādvalaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 6.1]
havirdhūmavitānena yaḥ sadābhra ivābabhau | [SaundĀ, 1 6.2]
mṛdubhiḥ saikataiḥ snigdhaiḥ kesarāstarapāṇḍubhiḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 7.1]
bhūmibhāgairasaṃkīrṇaiḥ sāṅgarāga ivābhavat | [SaundĀ, 1 7.2]
śucibhistīrthasaṃkhyātaiḥ pāvanairbhāvanairapi | [SaundĀ, 1 8.1]
bandhumāniva yastasthau sarobhiḥ sasaroruhaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 8.2]
paryāptaphalapuṣpābhiḥ sarvato vanarājibhiḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 9.1]
śuśubhe vavṛdhe caiva naraḥ sādhanavāniva | [SaundĀ, 1 9.2]
nīvāraphalasaṃtuṣṭaiḥ svasthaiḥ śāntairanutsukaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 10.1]
ākīrṇo 'pi tapobhṛdbhiḥ śūnyaśūnya ivābhavat | [SaundĀ, 1 10.2]
agnīnāṃ hūyamānānāṃ śikhināṃ kūjatāmapi | [SaundĀ, 1 11.1]
tīrthānāṃ cābhiṣekeṣu śuśruve yatra niḥsvanaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 11.2]
virejurhariṇā yatra suptā medhyāsu vediṣu | [SaundĀ, 1 12.1]
salājairmādhavīpuṣpairupahārāḥ kṛtā iva | [SaundĀ, 1 12.2]
api kṣudramṛgā yatra śāntāśceruḥ samaṃ mṛgaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 13.1]
śaraṇyebhyastapasvibhyo vinayaṃ śikṣitā iva | [SaundĀ, 1 13.2]
saṃdigdhe 'pyapunarbhāve viruddheṣvāgameṣvapi | [SaundĀ, 1 14.1]
pratyakṣiṇa ivākurvaṃstapo yatra tapodhanāḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 14.2]
yatra sma mīyate brahma kaiścit kaiścinna mīyate | [SaundĀ, 1 15.1]
kāle nimīyate somo na cākāle pramīyate | [SaundĀ, 1 15.2]
nirapekṣāḥ śarīreṣu dharme yatra svabuddhayaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 16.1]
saṃhṛṣṭā iva yatnena tāpasāstepire tapaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 16.2]
śrāmyanto munayo yatra svargāyodyuktacetasaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 17.1]
taporāgeṇa dharmasya vilopamiva cakrire | [SaundĀ, 1 17.2]
atha tejasvisadanaṃ tapaḥkṣetraṃ tamāśramam | [SaundĀ, 1 18.1]
kecidikṣvākavo jagmū rājaputrā vivatsavaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 18.2]
suvarṇastambhavarṣmāṇaḥ siṃhoraskā mahābhujāḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 19.1]
pātraṃ śabdasya mahataḥ śriyāṃ ca vinayasya ca | [SaundĀ, 1 19.2]
arharūpā hyanarhasya mahātmānaścalātmanaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 20.1]
prājñāḥ prajñāvimuktasya bhrātṛvyasya yavīyasaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 20.2]
mātṛśulkādupagatāṃ te śriyaṃ ca viṣehire | [SaundĀ, 1 21.1]
rarakṣuśca pituḥ satyaṃ yasmācchiśriyire vanam | [SaundĀ, 1 21.2]
teṣāṃ munirupādhyāyo gautamaḥ kapilo 'bhavat | [SaundĀ, 1 22.1]
gurugotrādataḥ kautsāste bhavanti sma gautamāḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 22.2]
ekapitroryathā bhrātroḥ pṛthagguruparigrahāt | [SaundĀ, 1 23.1]
rāma evābhavad gārgyo vāsubhadro 'pi gautamaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 23.2]
śākavṛkṣapraticchannaṃ vāsaṃ yasmācca cakrire | [SaundĀ, 1 24.1]
tasmādikṣvākuvaṃśyāste bhuvi śākyā iti smṛtāḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 24.2]
sa teṣāṃ gautamaścakre svavaṃśasadṛśīḥ kriyāḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 25.1]
munirūrdhvaṃ kumārasya sagarasyeva bhārgavaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 25.2]
kaṇvaḥ śākuntalasyeva bharatasya tarasvinaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 26.1]
vālmīkiriva dhīmāṃśca dhīmatormaithileyayoḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 26.2]
tadvanaṃ muninā tena taiśca kṣatriyapuṅgavaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 27.1]
śāntāṃ guptāṃ ca yugapad brahmakṣatraśriyaṃ dadhe | [SaundĀ, 1 27.2]
athodakalaśaṃ gṛhya teṣāṃ vṛddhicikīrṣayā | [SaundĀ, 1 28.1]
muniḥ sa viyadutpatya tānuvāca nṛpātmajān | [SaundĀ, 1 28.2]
yā patet kalaśādasmādakṣayyasalilānmahīm | [SaundĀ, 1 29.1]
dhārā tāmanatikramya māmanveta yathākramam | [SaundĀ, 1 29.2]
tataḥ paramamityuktvā śirobhiḥ praṇipatya ca | [SaundĀ, 1 30.1]
rathānāruruhuḥ sarve śīghravāhānalaṃkṛtān | [SaundĀ, 1 30.2]
tataḥ sa tairanugataḥ syandanasthairnabhogataḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 31.1]
tadāśramamahīprāntaṃ paricikṣepa vāriṇā | [SaundĀ, 1 31.2]
aṣṭāpadamivālikhya nimittaiḥ surabhīkṛtam | [SaundĀ, 1 32.1]
tānuvāca muniḥ sthitvā bhūmipālasutānidam | [SaundĀ, 1 32.2]
asmin dhārāparikṣipte nemicihnitalakṣaṇe | [SaundĀ, 1 33.1]
nirmimīdhvaṃ puraṃ yūyaṃ mayi yāte triviṣṭapam | [SaundĀ, 1 33.2]
tataḥ kadācitte vīrāstasmin pratigate munau | [SaundĀ, 1 34.1]
babhramuryauvanoddāmā gajā iva niraṅkuśāḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 34.2]
baddhagodhāṅgulītrāṇā hastaviṣṭhitakārmukāḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 35.1]
śarādhmātamahātūṇā vyāyatābaddhavāsasaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 35.2]
jijñāsamānā nāgeṣu kauśalaṃ śvāpadeṣu ca | [SaundĀ, 1 36.1]
anucakrurvanasthasya dauṣyanterdevakarmaṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 36.2]
tān dṛṣṭvā prakṛtiṃ yātān vṛddhānvyāghraśiśūniva | [SaundĀ, 1 37.1]
tāpasāstadvanaṃ hitvā himavantaṃ siṣevire | [SaundĀ, 1 37.2]
tatastadāśramasthānaṃ śūnyaṃ taiḥ śūnyacetasaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 38.1]
paśyanto manyunā taptā vyālā iva niśaśvasuḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 38.2]
atha te puṇyakarmāṇaḥ pratyupasthitavṛddhayaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 39.1]
tatra tajjñairupākhyātānavāpurmahato nidhīn | [SaundĀ, 1 39.2]
alaṃ dharmārthakāmānāṃ nikhilānāmavāptaye | [SaundĀ, 1 40.1]
nidhayo naikavidhayo bhūrayaste gatārayaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 40.2]
tatastatpratilambhācca pariṇāmācca karmaṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 41.1]
tasmin vāstuni vāstujñāḥ puraṃ śrīmannyaveśayan | [SaundĀ, 1 41.2]
saridvistīrṇaparikhaṃ spaṣṭāñcitamahāpatham | [SaundĀ, 1 42.1]
śailakalpamahāvapraṃ girivrajamivāparam | [SaundĀ, 1 42.2]
pāṇḍurāṭṭālasumukhaṃ suvibhaktāntarāpaṇam | [SaundĀ, 1 43.1]
harmyamālāparikṣiptaṃ kukṣiṃ himagireriva | [SaundĀ, 1 43.2]
vedavedāṅgaviduṣastasthuṣaḥ ṣaṭsu karmasu | [SaundĀ, 1 44.1]
śāntaye vṛddhaye caiva yatra viprānajījapan | [SaundĀ, 1 44.2]
tadbhūmerabhiyoktṝṇāṃ prayuktān vinivṛttaye | [SaundĀ, 1 45.1]
yatra svena prabhāvena bhṛtyadaṇḍānajījapan | [SaundĀ, 1 45.2]
caritradhanasampannān salajjān dīrghadarśinaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 46.1]
arhato 'tiṣṭhipan yatra śūrān dakṣān kuṭumbinaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 46.2]
vyastaistaistairguṇairyuktān mativāgvikramādibhiḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 47.1]
karmasu pratirūpeṣu sacivāṃstānnyayūyujan | [SaundĀ, 1 47.2]
vasumadbhir avibhrāntair alaṃvidyair avismitaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 48.1]
yad babhāse naraiḥ kīrṇaṃ mandaraḥ kinnarairiva | [SaundĀ, 1 48.2]
yatra te hṛṣṭamanasaḥ pauraprīticikīrṣayā | [SaundĀ, 1 49.1]
śrīmantyudyānasaṃjñāni yaśodhāmānyacīkaran | [SaundĀ, 1 49.2]
śivāḥ puṣkariṇīścaiva paramāgryaguṇāmbhasaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 50.1]
nājñayā cetanotkarṣāddikṣu sarvāsvacīkhanan | [SaundĀ, 1 50.2]
manojñāḥ śrīmatīḥ praṣṭhīḥ pathiṣūpavaneṣu ca | [SaundĀ, 1 51.1]
sabhāḥ kūpavatīścaiva samantāt pratyatiṣṭhipan | [SaundĀ, 1 51.2]
hastyaśvarathasaṃkīrṇam asaṃkīrṇam anākulam | [SaundĀ, 1 52.1]
anigūḍhārthivibhavaṃ nigūḍhajñānapauruṣam | [SaundĀ, 1 52.2]
saṃnidhānamivārthānāmādhānamiva tejasām | [SaundĀ, 1 53.1]
niketamiva vidyānāṃ saṃketamiva saṃpadām | [SaundĀ, 1 53.2]
vāsavṛkṣaṃ guṇavatāmāśrayaṃ śaraṇaiṣiṇām | [SaundĀ, 1 54.1]
ānartaṃ kṛtaśāstrāṇāmālānaṃ bāhuśālinām | [SaundĀ, 1 54.2]
samājairutsavairdāyaiḥ kriyāvidhibhireva ca | [SaundĀ, 1 55.1]
alaṃcakruralaṃvīryāste jagaddhāma tatpuram | [SaundĀ, 1 55.2]
yasmādanyāyataste ca kaṃcinnācīkaran karam | [SaundĀ, 1 56.1]
tasmādalpena kālena tattadāpūpuran puram | [SaundĀ, 1 56.2]
kapilasya ca tasyarṣestasminn āśramavāstuni | [SaundĀ, 1 57.1]
yasmātte tatpuraṃ cakrustasmāt kapilavāstu tat | [SaundĀ, 1 57.2]
kakandasya makandasya kuśāmbasyeva cāśrame | [SaundĀ, 1 58.1]
puryo yathā hi śrūyante tathaiva kapilasya tat | [SaundĀ, 1 58.2]
āpuḥ puraṃ tatpuruhūtakalpāste tejasāryeṇa na vismayena | [SaundĀ, 1 59.1]
āpuryaśogandhamataśca śaśvat sutā yayāteriva kīrtimantaḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 59.2]
tannāthavṛttairapi rājaputrairarājakaṃ naiva rarāja rāṣṭram | [SaundĀ, 1 60.1]
tārāsahasrairapi dīpyamānair anutthite candra ivāntarīkṣam | [SaundĀ, 1 60.2]
yo jyāyānatha vayasā guṇaiśca teṣāṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ vṛṣabha ivaujasā vṛṣāṇām | [SaundĀ, 1 61.1]
te tatra priyaguravastamabhyaṣicann ādityā daśaśatalocanaṃ divīva | [SaundĀ, 1 61.2]
ācāravānvinayavānnayavānkriyāvān dharmāya nendriyasukhāya dhṛtātapatraḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 62.1]
tadbhrātṛbhiḥ parivṛtaḥ sa jugopa rāṣṭram saṃkrandano divamivānusṛto marudbhiḥ | [SaundĀ, 1 62.2]
{SaundĀ, 2}
tataḥ kadācitkālena tadavāpa kulakramāt | [SaundĀ, 2 1.1]
rājā śuddhodano nāma śuddhakarmā jitendriyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 1.2]
yaḥ sasañje na kāmeṣu śrīprāptau na visismiye | [SaundĀ, 2 2.1]
nāvamene parānṛddhyā parebhyo nāpi vivyathe | [SaundĀ, 2 2.2]
balīyān sattvasampannaḥ śrutavān buddhimānapi | [SaundĀ, 2 3.1]
vikrānto nayavāṃścaiva dhīraḥ sumukha eva ca | [SaundĀ, 2 3.2]
vapuṣmāṃśca na ca stabdho dakṣiṇo na ca nārjavaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 4.1]
tejasvī na ca na kṣāntaḥ kartā ca na ca vismitaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 4.2]
ākṣiptaḥ śatrubhiḥ saṃkhye suhṛdbhiśca vyapāśritaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 5.1]
abhavad yo na vimukhastejasā ditsayaiva ca | [SaundĀ, 2 5.2]
yaḥ pūrvaiḥ rājabhiryātāṃ yiyāsurdharmapaddhatim | [SaundĀ, 2 6.1]
rājyaṃ dīkṣāmiva vahan vṛttenānvagamat pitṝn | [SaundĀ, 2 6.2]
yasya suvyavahārācca rakṣaṇācca sukhaṃ prajāḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 7.1]
śiśyire vigatodvegāḥ pituraṅkagatā iva | [SaundĀ, 2 7.2]
kṛtaśāstraḥ kṛtāstro vā jāto vā vipule kule | [SaundĀ, 2 8.1]
akṛtārtho na dadṛśe yasya darśanameyivān | [SaundĀ, 2 8.2]
hitaṃ vipriyamapyukto yaḥ śuśrāva na cukṣubhe | [SaundĀ, 2 9.1]
duṣkṛtaṃ bahvapi tyaktvā sasmāra kṛtamaṇvapi | [SaundĀ, 2 9.2]
praṇatānanujagrāha vijagrāha kuladviṣaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 10.1]
āpannān parijagrāha nijagrāhāsthitān pathi | [SaundĀ, 2 10.2]
prāyeṇa viṣaye yasya tacchīlamanuvartinaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 11.1]
arjayanto dadṛśire dhanānīva guṇānapi | [SaundĀ, 2 11.2]
adhyaiṣṭa yaḥ paraṃ brahma na vyaiṣṭa satataṃ dhṛteḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 12.1]
dānānyadita pātrebhyaḥ pāpaṃ nākṛta kiṃcana | [SaundĀ, 2 12.2]
dhṛtyāvākṣīt pratijñāṃ sa sadvājīvodyatāṃ dhuram | [SaundĀ, 2 13.1]
na hyavāñchīccyutaḥ satyānmuhūrtamapi jīvitam | [SaundĀ, 2 13.2]
viduṣaḥ paryupāsiṣṭa vyakāśiṣṭātmavattayā | [SaundĀ, 2 14.1]
vyarociṣṭa ca śiṣṭebhyo māsīṣe candramā iva | [SaundĀ, 2 14.2]
avedīd buddhiśāstrābhyāmiha cāmutra ca kṣamam | [SaundĀ, 2 15.1]
arakṣīddhairyavīryābhyāmindriyāṇyapi ca prajāḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 15.2]
ahārṣīd duḥkhamārtānāṃ dviṣatāṃ corjitaṃ yaśaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 16.1]
acaiṣīcca nayairbhūmiṃ bhūyasā yaśasaiva ca | [SaundĀ, 2 16.2]
apyāsīd duḥkhitān paśyan prakṛtyā karuṇātmakaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 17.1]
nādhauṣīcca yaśo lobhādanyāyādhigatairdhanaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 17.2]
sauhārdadṛḍhabhaktitvānmaitreṣu viguṇeṣvapi | [SaundĀ, 2 18.1]
nādidāsīd aditsīttu saumukhyāt svaṃ svamarthavat | [SaundĀ, 2 18.2]
anivedyāgram arhadbhyo nālikṣat kiṃcid aplutaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 19.1]
gāmadharmeṇa nādhukṣat kṣīratarṣeṇa gāmiva | [SaundĀ, 2 19.2]
nāsṛkṣad balimaprāptaṃ nārukṣanmānamaiśvaram | [SaundĀ, 2 20.1]
āgamairbuddhim ādhikṣaddharmāya na tu kīrtaye | [SaundĀ, 2 20.2]
kleśārhānapi kāṃścittu nākliṣṭa kliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 21.1]
āryabhāvācca nādhukṣad dviṣato 'pi sato guṇān | [SaundĀ, 2 21.2]
ākṛkṣad vapuṣā dṛṣṭīḥ prajānāṃ candramā iva | [SaundĀ, 2 22.1]
parasvaṃ bhuvi nāmṛkṣanmahāviṣamivoragam | [SaundĀ, 2 22.2]
nākrukṣad viṣaye tasya kaścitkaiścit kvacit kṣataḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 23.1]
ādikṣattasya hastasthamārtebhyo hyabhayaṃ dhanuḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 23.2]
kṛtāgaso 'pi praṇatān prāgeva priyakāriṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 24.1]
adarśatsnigdhayā dṛṣṭyā ślakṣṇena vacasāsicat | [SaundĀ, 2 24.2]
bahvīr adhyagamad vidyā viṣayeṣvakutūhalaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 25.1]
sthitaḥ kārtayuge dharme dharmāt kṛcchre 'pi nāsrasat | [SaundĀ, 2 25.2]
avardhiṣṭa guṇaiḥ śaśvadavṛdhanmitrasaṃpadā | [SaundĀ, 2 26.1]
avartiṣṭa ca vṛddheṣu nāvṛtad garhite pathi | [SaundĀ, 2 26.2]
śarairaśīśamacchatrūn guṇairbandhūnarīramat | [SaundĀ, 2 27.1]
randhrairnācūcudad bhṛtyān karair nāpīpiḍat prajāḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 27.2]
rakṣaṇāccaiva śauryācca nikhilāṃ gām avīvapat | [SaundĀ, 2 28.1]
spaṣṭayā daṇḍanītyā ca rātrisattrān avīvapat | [SaundĀ, 2 28.2]
kulaṃ rājarṣivṛttena yaśogandham avīvapat | [SaundĀ, 2 29.1]
dīptyā tama ivādityastejasārīn avīvapat | [SaundĀ, 2 29.2]
apaprathat pitṝṃścaiva satputrasadṛśairguṇaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 30.1]
salileneva cāmbhodo vṛttenājihladat prajāḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 30.2]
dānairajasravipulaiḥ somaṃ viprān asūṣavat | [SaundĀ, 2 31.1]
rājadharmasthitatvācca kāle sasyam asūṣavat | [SaundĀ, 2 31.2]
adharmiṣṭhām acakathanna kathāmakathaṃkathaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 32.1]
cakravartīva ca parān dharmāyābhyudasīṣahat | [SaundĀ, 2 32.2]
rāṣṭramanyatra ca balerna sa kiṃcid adīdapat | [SaundĀ, 2 33.1]
bhṛtyaireva ca sodyogaṃ dviṣaddarpamadīdapat | [SaundĀ, 2 33.2]
svairevādīdapaccāpi bhūyo bhūyo guṇaiḥ kulam | [SaundĀ, 2 34.1]
prajā nādīdapaccaiva sarvadharmavyavasthayā | [SaundĀ, 2 34.2]
aśrāntaḥ samaye yajvā yajñabhūmim amīmapat | [SaundĀ, 2 35.1]
pālanācca dvijān brahma nirudvignān amīmapat | [SaundĀ, 2 35.2]
gurubhirvidhivat kāle saumyaḥ somam amīmapat | [SaundĀ, 2 36.1]
tapasā tejasā caiṣa dviṣatsainyam amīmapat | [SaundĀ, 2 36.2]
prajāḥ paramadharmajñaḥ sūkṣmaṃ dharmam avīvasat | [SaundĀ, 2 37.1]
darśanāccaiva dharmasya kāle svargam avīvasat | [SaundĀ, 2 37.2]
vyaktamapyarthakṛcchreṣu nādharmiṣṭhamatiṣṭhipat | [SaundĀ, 2 38.1]
priya ityeva cāśaktaṃ na saṃrāgādavīvṛdhat | [SaundĀ, 2 38.2]
tejasā ca tviṣā caiva ripūn dṛptān abībhasat | [SaundĀ, 2 39.1]
yaśodīpena dīptena pṛthivīṃ ca vyabībhasat | [SaundĀ, 2 39.2]
ānṛśaṃsyānna yaśase tenādāyi sadārthine | [SaundĀ, 2 40.1]
dravyaṃ mahadapi tyaktvā na caivākīrti kiṃcana | [SaundĀ, 2 40.2]
tenārirapi duḥkhārto nātyāji śaraṇāgataḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 41.1]
jitvā dṛptānapi ripūnna tenākāri vismayaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 41.2]
na tenābhedi maryādā kāmāddveṣādbhayādapi | [SaundĀ, 2 42.1]
tena satsvapi bhogeṣu nāsevīndriyavṛttitā | [SaundĀ, 2 42.2]
na tenādarśi viṣamaṃ kāryaṃ kvacana kiṃcana | [SaundĀ, 2 43.1]
vipriyapriyayoḥ kṛtye na tenāgāmi nikriyāḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 43.2]
tenāpāyi yathākalpaṃ somaśca yaśa eva ca | [SaundĀ, 2 44.1]
vedaścāmnāyi satataṃ vedokto dharma eva ca | [SaundĀ, 2 44.2]
evamādibhiratyakto babhūvāsulabhairguṇaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 45.1]
aśakyaḥ śakyasāmantaḥ śākyarājaḥ sa śakravat | [SaundĀ, 2 45.2]
atha tasmin tathā kāle dharmakāmā divaukasaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 46.1]
vicerurdiśi lokasya dharmacaryāṃ didṛkṣavaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 46.2]
dharmātmānaścarantaste dharmajijñāsayā jagat | [SaundĀ, 2 47.1]
dadṛśustaṃ viśeṣeṇa dharmātmānaṃ narādhipam | [SaundĀ, 2 47.2]
devebhyastuṣitebhyo 'tha bodhisattvaḥ kṣitiṃ vrajan | [SaundĀ, 2 48.1]
upapattiṃ praṇidadhe kule tasya mahīpateḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 48.2]
tasya devī nṛdevasya māyā nāma tadābhavat | [SaundĀ, 2 49.1]
vītakrodhatamomāyā māyeva divi devatā | [SaundĀ, 2 49.2]
svapne 'tha samaye garbhamāviśantaṃ dadarśa sā | [SaundĀ, 2 50.1]
ṣaḍdantaṃ vāraṇaṃ śvetamairāvatamivaujasā | [SaundĀ, 2 50.2]
taṃ vinirdidiśuḥ śrutvā svapnaṃ svapnavido dvijāḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 51.1]
tasya janma kumārasya lakṣmīdharmayaśobhṛtaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 51.2]
tasya sattvaviśeṣasya jātau jātikṣayaiṣiṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 52.1]
sācalā pracacālorvī taraṅgābhihateva nauḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 52.2]
sūryaraśmibhirakliṣṭaṃ puṣpavarṣaṃ papāta khāt | [SaundĀ, 2 53.1]
digvāraṇakarādhūtād vanāccaitrarathādiva | [SaundĀ, 2 53.2]
divi dundubhayo nedurdīvyatāṃ marutāmiva | [SaundĀ, 2 54.1]
didīpe 'bhyadhikaṃ sūryaḥ śivaśca pavano vavau | [SaundĀ, 2 54.2]
tutuṣustuṣitāścaiva śuddhāvāsāśca devatāḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 55.1]
saddharmabahumānena sattvānāṃ cānukampayā | [SaundĀ, 2 55.2]
samāyayau yaśaḥketuṃ śreyaḥketukaraḥ paraḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 56.1]
babhrāje śāntayā lakṣmyā dharmo vigrahavāniva | [SaundĀ, 2 56.2]
devyāmapi yavīyasyāmaraṇyāmiva pāvakaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 57.1]
nando nāma suto jajñe nityānandakaraḥ kule | [SaundĀ, 2 57.2]
dīrghabāhurmahāvakṣāḥ siṃhāṃso vṛṣabhekṣaṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 58.1]
vapuṣāgryeṇa yo nāma sundaropapadaṃ dadhe | [SaundĀ, 2 58.2]
madhumāsa iva prāptaścandro nava ivoditaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 59.1]
aṅgavāniva cānaṅgaḥ sa babhau kāntayā śriyā | [SaundĀ, 2 59.2]
sa tau saṃvardhayāmāsa narendraḥ parayā mudā | [SaundĀ, 2 60.1]
arthaḥ sajjanahastastho dharmakāmau mahāniva | [SaundĀ, 2 60.2]
tasya kālena satputrau vavṛdhāte bhavāya tau | [SaundĀ, 2 61.1]
āryasyārambhamahato dharmārthāviva bhūtaye | [SaundĀ, 2 61.2]
tayoḥ satputrayormadhye śākyarājo rarāja saḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 62.1]
madhyadeśa iva vyakto himavatpāriyātrayoḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 62.2]
tatastayoḥ saṃskṛtayoḥ krameṇa narendrasūnvoḥ kṛtavidyayośca | [SaundĀ, 2 63.1]
kāmeṣvajasraṃ pramamāda nandaḥ sarvārthasiddhastu na saṃrarañja | [SaundĀ, 2 63.2]
sa prekṣyaiva hi jīrṇamāturaṃ ca mṛtaṃ ca vimṛśan jagadanabhijñamārtacittaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 64.1]
hṛdayagataparaghṛṇo na viṣayaratimagamajjananamaraṇabhayamabhito vijighāṃsuḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 64.2]
udvegādapunarbhave manaḥ praṇidhāya sa yayau śayitavarāṅganādanāsthaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 65.1]
niśi nṛpatinilayanād vanagamanakṛtamanāḥ sarasa iva mathitanalināt kalahaṃsaḥ | [SaundĀ, 2 65.2]
{SaundĀ, 3}
tapase tataḥ kapilavāstu hayagajarathaughasaṃkulam | [SaundĀ, 3 1.1]
śrīmadabhayam anuraktajanaṃ sa vihāya niścitamanā vanaṃ yayau | [SaundĀ, 3 1.2]
vividhāgamāṃstapasi tāṃśca vividhaniyamāśrayān munīn | [SaundĀ, 3 2.1]
prekṣya sa viṣayatṛṣākṛpaṇānanavasthitaṃ tapa iti nyavartata | [SaundĀ, 3 2.2]
atha mokṣavādinamarāḍamupaśamamatiṃ tathodrakam | [SaundĀ, 3 3.1]
tattvakṛtamatirupāsya jahāvayamapyamārga iti mārgakovidaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 3.2]
sa vicārayan jagati kiṃ nu paramamiti taṃ tamāgamam | [SaundĀ, 3 4.1]
niścayam anadhigataḥ parataḥ paramaṃ cacāra tapa eva duṣkaram | [SaundĀ, 3 4.2]
atha naiṣa mārga iti vīkṣya tadapi vipulaṃ jahau tapaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 5.1]
dhyānaviṣayamavagamya paraṃ bubhuje varānnam amṛtatvabuddhaye | [SaundĀ, 3 5.2]
sa suvarṇapīnayugabāhurṛṣabhagatirāyatekṣaṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 6.1]
plakṣamavaniruhamabhyagamat paramasya niścayavidherbubhutsayā | [SaundĀ, 3 6.2]
upaviśya tatra kṛtabuddhir acaladhṛtir adrirājavat | [SaundĀ, 3 7.1]
mārabalamajayadugramatho bubudhe padaṃ śivam ahāryam avyayam | [SaundĀ, 3 7.2]
avagamya taṃ ca kṛtakāryamamṛtamanaso divaukasaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 8.1]
harṣamatulamagaman muditā vimukhī tu mārapariṣat pracukṣubhe | [SaundĀ, 3 8.2]
sanagā ca bhūḥ pravicacāla hutavahasakhaḥ śivo vavau | [SaundĀ, 3 9.1]
nedurapi ca suradundubhayaḥ pravavarṣa cāmbudharavarjitaṃ nabhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 9.2]
avabudhya caiva paramārthamajaramanukampayā vibhuḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 10.1]
nityamamṛtamupadarśayituṃ sa varāṇasīparikarāmayāt purīm | [SaundĀ, 3 10.2]
atha dharmacakramṛtanābhi dhṛtimatisamādhinemimat | [SaundĀ, 3 11.1]
tatra vinayaniyamāramṛṣirjagato hitāya pariṣadyavartayat | [SaundĀ, 3 11.2]
iti duḥkhametadiyamasya samudayalatā pravartikā | [SaundĀ, 3 12.1]
śāntiriyamayamupāya iti pravibhāgaśaḥ paramidaṃ catuṣṭayam | [SaundĀ, 3 12.2]
abhidhāya ca triparivartamatulamanivartyamuttamam | [SaundĀ, 3 13.1]
dvādaśaniyatavikalpaṃ ṛṣirvinināya kauṇḍinasagotramāditaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 13.2]
sa hi doṣasāgaramagādhamupadhijalamādhijantukam | [SaundĀ, 3 14.1]
krodhamadabhayataraṅgacalaṃ pratatāra lokamapi ca vyatārayat | [SaundĀ, 3 14.2]
sa vinīya kāśiṣu gayeṣu bahujanamatho girivraje | [SaundĀ, 3 15.1]
pitryamapi paramakāruṇiko nagaraṃ yayāvanujighṛkṣayā tadā | [SaundĀ, 3 15.2]
viṣayātmakasya hi janasya bahuvividhamārgasevinaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 16.1]
sūryasadṛśavapurabhyudito vijahāra sūrya iva gautamastamaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 16.2]
abhitastataḥ kapilavāstu paramaśubhavāstusaṃstutam | [SaundĀ, 3 17.1]
vastumatiśuci śivopavanaṃ sa dadarśa niḥspṛhatayā yathā vanam | [SaundĀ, 3 17.2]
aparigrahaḥ sa hi babhūva niyatamatirātmanīśvaraḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 18.1]
naikavidhabhayakareṣu kimu svajanasvadeśajanamitravastuṣu | [SaundĀ, 3 18.2]
pratipūjayā na sa jaharṣa na ca śucamavajñayāgamat | [SaundĀ, 3 19.1]
niścitamatirasicandanayorna jagāma duḥkhasukhayośca vikriyām | [SaundĀ, 3 19.2]
atha pārthivaḥ samupalabhya sutamupagataṃ tathāgatam | [SaundĀ, 3 20.1]
tūrṇam abahuturagānugataḥ sutadarśanotsukatayābhiniryayau | [SaundĀ, 3 20.2]
sugatastathāgatamavekṣya narapatimadhīramāśayā | [SaundĀ, 3 21.1]
śeṣamapi ca janamaśrumukhaṃ vininīṣayā gaganamutpapāta ha | [SaundĀ, 3 21.2]
sa vicakrame divi bhuvīva punarupaviveśa tasthivān | [SaundĀ, 3 22.1]
niścalamatiraśayiṣṭa punarbahudhābhavat punarabhūttathaikadhā | [SaundĀ, 3 22.2]
salile kṣitāviva cacāra jalamiva viveśa medinīm | [SaundĀ, 3 23.1]
megha iva divi vavarṣa punaḥ punarajvalannava ivodito raviḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 23.2]
yugapajjvalan jvalanavacca jalamavasṛjaṃśca meghavat | [SaundĀ, 3 24.1]
taptakanakasadṛśaprabhayā sa babhau pradīpta iva sandhyayā ghanaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 24.2]
tamudīkṣya hemamaṇijālavalayinamivotthitaṃ dhvajam | [SaundĀ, 3 25.1]
prītimagamadatulāṃ nṛpatirjanatā natāśca bahumānamabhyayuḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 25.2]
atha bhājanīkṛtamavekṣya manujapatimṛddhisaṃpadā | [SaundĀ, 3 26.1]
paurajanamapi ca tatpravaṇaṃ nijagāda dharmavinayaṃ vināyakaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 26.2]
nṛpatistataḥ prathamamāpa phalamamṛtadharmasiddhaye | [SaundĀ, 3 27.1]
dharmamatulamadhigamya munermunaye nanāma sa yato gurāviva | [SaundĀ, 3 27.2]
bahavaḥ prasannamanaso 'tha jananamaraṇārtibhīravaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 28.1]
śākyatanayavṛṣabhāḥ kṛtino vṛṣabhā ivānalabhayāt pravavrajuḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 28.2]
vijahustu ye 'pi na gṛhāṇi tanayapitṛmātrapekṣayā | [SaundĀ, 3 29.1]
te 'pi niyamavidhim āmaraṇājjagṛhuśca yuktamanasaśca dadhrire | [SaundĀ, 3 29.2]
na jihiṃsa sūkṣmamapi jantumapi paravadhopajīvinaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 30.1]
kiṃ bata vipulaguṇaḥ kulajaḥ sadayaḥ sadā kimu munerupāsayā | [SaundĀ, 3 30.2]
akṛśodyamaḥ kṛśadhano 'pi paraparibhavāsaho 'pi san | [SaundĀ, 3 31.1]
nānyadhanamapajahāra tathā bhujagādivānyavibhavāddhi vivyathe | [SaundĀ, 3 31.2]
vibhavānvito 'pi taruṇo 'pi viṣayacapalendriyo 'pi san | [SaundĀ, 3 32.1]
naiva ca parayuvatīragamat paramaṃ hi tā dahanato 'pyamanyata | [SaundĀ, 3 32.2]
anṛtaṃ jagāda na ca kaścidṛtamapi jajalpa nāpriyam | [SaundĀ, 3 33.1]
ślakṣṇamapi ca na jagāvahitaṃ hitamapyuvāca na ca paiśunāya yat | [SaundĀ, 3 33.2]
manasā lulobha na ca jātu paravasuṣu gṛddhamānasaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 34.1]
kāmasukhamasukhato vimṛśan vijahāra tṛpta iva tatra sajjanaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 34.2]
na parasya kaścidapaghātamapi ca saghṛṇo vyacintayat | [SaundĀ, 3 35.1]
mātṛpitṛsutasuhṛtsadṛśaṃ sa dadarśa tatra hi parasparaṃ janaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 35.2]
niyataṃ bhaviṣyati paratra bhavadapi ca bhūtamapyatho | [SaundĀ, 3 36.1]
karmaphalamapi ca lokagatirniyateti darśanamavāpa sādhu ca | [SaundĀ, 3 36.2]
iti karmaṇā daśavidhena paramakuśalena bhūriṇā | [SaundĀ, 3 37.1]
bhraṃśini śithilaguṇo 'pi yuge vijahāra tatra munisaṃśrayājjanaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 37.2]
na ca tatra kaścidupapattisukhamabhilalāṣa tairguṇaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 38.1]
sarvamaśivamavagamya bhavaṃ bhavasaṃkṣayāya vavṛte na janmane | [SaundĀ, 3 38.2]
akathaṃkathā gṛhiṇa eva paramapariśuddhadṛṣṭayaḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 39.1]
srotasi hi vavṛtire bahavo rajasastanutvamapi cakrire pare | [SaundĀ, 3 39.2]
vavṛte 'tra yo 'pi viṣayeṣu vibhavasadṛśeṣu kaścana | [SaundĀ, 3 40.1]
tyāgavinayaniyamābhirato vijahāra so 'pi na cacāla satpathāt | [SaundĀ, 3 40.2]
api ca svato 'pi parato 'pi na bhayamabhavanna daivataḥ | [SaundĀ, 3 41.1]
tatra ca susukhasubhikṣaguṇairjahṛṣuḥ prajāḥ kṛtayuge manoriva | [SaundĀ, 3 41.2]
iti muditamanāmayaṃ nirāpat kururaghupūrupuropamaṃ puraṃ tat | [SaundĀ, 3 42.1]
abhavadabhayadaiśike maharṣau viharati tatra śivāya vītarāge | [SaundĀ, 3 42.2]
{SaundĀ, 4}
munau bruvāṇe 'pi tu tatra dharmaṃ dharmaṃ prati jñātiṣu cādṛteṣu | [SaundĀ, 4 1.1]
prāsādasaṃstho madanaikakāryaḥ priyāsahāyo vijahāra nandaḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 1.2]
sa cakravākyeva hi cakravākastayā sametaḥ priyayā priyārhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 2.1]
nācintayad vaiśramaṇaṃ na śakraṃ tatsthānahetoḥ kuta eva dharmam | [SaundĀ, 4 2.2]
lakṣmyā ca rūpeṇa ca sundarīti stambhena garveṇa ca māninīti | [SaundĀ, 4 3.1]
dīptyā ca mānena ca bhāminīti yāto babhāṣe trividhena nāmnā | [SaundĀ, 4 3.2]
sā hāsahaṃsā nayanadvirephā pīnastanātyunnatapadmakośā | [SaundĀ, 4 4.1]
bhūyo babhāse svakuloditena strīpadminī nandadivākareṇa | [SaundĀ, 4 4.2]
rūpeṇa cātyantamanohareṇa rūpānurūpeṇa ca ceṣṭitena | [SaundĀ, 4 5.1]
manuṣyaloke hi tadā babhūva sā sundarī strīṣu nareṣu nandaḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 5.2]
sā devatā nandanacāriṇīva kulasya nandījananaśca nandaḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 6.1]
atītya martyān anupetya devān sṛṣṭāvabhūtāmiva bhūtadhātrā | [SaundĀ, 4 6.2]
tāṃ sundarīṃ cenna labheta nandaḥ sā vā niṣeveta na taṃ natabhrūḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 7.1]
dvandvaṃ dhruvaṃ tadvikalaṃ na śobhetānyonyahīnāviva rātricandrau | [SaundĀ, 4 7.2]
kandarparatyoriva lakṣyabhūtaṃ pramodanāndyoriva nīḍabhūtam | [SaundĀ, 4 8.1]
praharṣatuṣṭyoriva pātrabhūtaṃ dvandvaṃ sahāraṃsta madāndhabhūtam | [SaundĀ, 4 8.2]
parasparodvīkṣaṇatatparākṣaṃ parasparavyāhṛtasaktacittam | [SaundĀ, 4 9.1]
parasparāśleṣahṛtāṅgarāgaṃ parasparaṃ tanmithunaṃ jahāra | [SaundĀ, 4 9.2]
bhāvānuraktau girinirjharasthau tau kinnarīkiṃpuruṣāvivobhau | [SaundĀ, 4 10.1]
cikrīḍatuścābhivirejatuśca rūpaśriyānyonyamivākṣipantau | [SaundĀ, 4 10.2]
anyonyasaṃrāgavivardhanena taddvandvamanyonyamarīramacca | [SaundĀ, 4 11.1]
klamāntare 'nyonyavinodanena salīlamanyonyam amīmadacca | [SaundĀ, 4 11.2]
vibhūṣayāmāsa tataḥ priyāṃ sa siṣeviṣustāṃ na mṛjāvahārtham | [SaundĀ, 4 12.1]
svenaiva rūpeṇa vibhūṣitā hi vibhūṣaṇānāmapi bhūṣaṇaṃ sā | [SaundĀ, 4 12.2]
dattvātha sā darpaṇamasya haste mamāgrato dhāraya tāvadenam | [SaundĀ, 4 13.1]
viśeṣakaṃ yāvadahaṃ karomītyuvāca kāntaṃ sa ca taṃ babhāra | [SaundĀ, 4 13.2]
bhartustataḥ śmaśru nirīkṣamāṇā viśeṣakaṃ sāpi cakāra tādṛk | [SaundĀ, 4 14.1]
niśvāsavātena ca darpaṇasya cikitsayitvā nijaghāna nandaḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 14.2]
sā tena ceṣṭālalitena bhartuḥ śāṭhyena cāntarmanasā jahāsa | [SaundĀ, 4 15.1]
bhavecca ruṣṭā kila nāma tasmai lalāṭajihmāṃ bhṛkuṭiṃ cakāra | [SaundĀ, 4 15.2]
cikṣepa karṇotpalamasya cāṃse kareṇa savyena madālasena | [SaundĀ, 4 16.1]
patrāṅguliṃ cārdhanimīlitākṣe vaktre 'sya tāmeva vinirdudhāva | [SaundĀ, 4 16.2]
tataścalannūpurayoktritābhyāṃ nakhaprabhodbhāsitarāṅgulibhyām | [SaundĀ, 4 17.1]
padbhyāṃ priyāyā nalinopamābhyāṃ mūrdhnā bhayānnāma nanāma nandaḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 17.2]
sa muktapuṣponmiṣitena mūrdhnā tataḥ priyāyāḥ priyakṛd babhāse | [SaundĀ, 4 18.1]
suvarṇavedyāmanilāvabhagnaḥ puṣpātibhārādiva nāgavṛkṣaḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 18.2]
sā taṃ stanodvartitahārayaṣṭirutthāpayāmāsa nipīḍya dorbhyām | [SaundĀ, 4 19.1]
kathaṃ kṛto 'sīti jahāsa coccairmukhena sācīkṛtakuṇḍalena | [SaundĀ, 4 19.2]
patyustato darpaṇasaktapāṇermuhurmuhurvaktramavekṣamāṇā | [SaundĀ, 4 20.1]
tamālapatrārdratale kapole samāpayāmāsa viśeṣakaṃ tat | [SaundĀ, 4 20.2]
tasyā mukhaṃ tat satamālapatraṃ tāmrādharauṣṭhaṃ cikurāyatākṣam | [SaundĀ, 4 21.1]
raktādhikāgraṃ patitadvirephaṃ saśaivalaṃ padmamivābabhāse | [SaundĀ, 4 21.2]
nandastato darpaṇamādareṇa bibhrat tadāmaṇḍanasākṣibhūtam | [SaundĀ, 4 22.1]
viśeṣakāvekṣaṇakekarākṣo laḍat priyāyā vadanaṃ dadarśa | [SaundĀ, 4 22.2]
tatkuṇḍalādaṣṭaviśeṣakāntaṃ kāraṇḍavakliṣṭamivāravindam | [SaundĀ, 4 23.1]
nandaḥ priyāyā mukhamīkṣamāṇo bhūyaḥ priyānandakaro babhūva | [SaundĀ, 4 23.2]
vimānakalpe sa vimānagarbhe tatastathā caiva nananda nandaḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 24.1]
tathāgataścāgatabhaikṣakālo bhaikṣāya tasya praviveśa veśma | [SaundĀ, 4 24.2]
avāṅmukho niṣpraṇayaśca tasthau bhrāturgṛhe 'nyasya gṛhe yathaiva | [SaundĀ, 4 25.1]
tasmādatho preṣyajanapramādād bhikṣām alabdhvaiva punarjagāma | [SaundĀ, 4 25.2]
kācit pipeṣāṅgavilepanaṃ hi vāso 'ṅganā kācidavāsayacca | [SaundĀ, 4 26.1]
ayojayat snānavidhiṃ tathānyā jagranthuranyāḥ surabhīḥ srajaśca | [SaundĀ, 4 26.2]
tasmin gṛhe bharturataścarantyaḥ krīḍānurūpaṃ lalitaṃ niyogam | [SaundĀ, 4 27.1]
kāścinna buddhaṃ dadṛśuryuvatyo buddhasya vaiṣā niyataṃ manīṣā | [SaundĀ, 4 27.2]
kācit sthitā tatra tu harmyapṛṣṭhe gavākṣapakṣe praṇidhāya cakṣuḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 28.1]
viniṣpatantaṃ sugataṃ dadarśa payodagarbhādiva dīptamarkam | [SaundĀ, 4 28.2]
sā gauravaṃ tatra vicārya bhartuḥ svayā ca bhaktyārhatayārhataśca | [SaundĀ, 4 29.1]
nandasya tasthau purato vivakṣustadājñayā ceti tadācacakṣe | [SaundĀ, 4 29.2]
anugrahāyāsya janasya śaṅke gururgṛhaṃ no bhagavān praviṣṭaḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 30.1]
bhikṣām alabdhvā giramāsanaṃ vā śūnyādaraṇyādiva yāti bhūyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 30.2]
śrutvā maharṣeḥ sa gṛhapraveśaṃ satkārahīnaṃ ca punaḥ prayāṇam | [SaundĀ, 4 31.1]
cacāla citrābharaṇāmbarasrakkalpadrumo dhūta ivānilena | [SaundĀ, 4 31.2]
kṛtvāñjaliṃ mūrdhani padmakalpaṃ tataḥ sa kāntāṃ gamanaṃ yayāce | [SaundĀ, 4 32.1]
kartuṃ gamiṣyāmi gurau praṇāmaṃ māmabhyanujñātumihārhasīti | [SaundĀ, 4 32.2]
sā vepamānā parisasvaje taṃ śālaṃ latā vātasamīriteva | [SaundĀ, 4 33.1]
dadarśa cāśruplutalolanetrā dīrghaṃ ca niśvasya vaco 'bhyuvāca | [SaundĀ, 4 33.2]
nāhaṃ yiyāsorgurudarśanārthamarhāmi kartuṃ tava dharmapīḍām | [SaundĀ, 4 34.1]
gacchāryaputraihi ca śīghrameva viśeṣako yāvadayaṃ na śuṣkaḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 34.2]
sacedbhavestvaṃ khalu dīrghasūtro daṇḍaṃ mahāntaṃ tvayi pātayeyam | [SaundĀ, 4 35.1]
muhurmuhustvāṃ śayitaṃ kucābhyāṃ vibodhayeyaṃ ca na cālapeyam | [SaundĀ, 4 35.2]
athāpyanāśyānaviśeṣakāyāṃ mayyeṣyasi tvaṃ tvaritaṃ tatastvām | [SaundĀ, 4 36.1]
nipīḍayiṣyāmi bhujadvayena nirbhūṣaṇenārdravilepanena | [SaundĀ, 4 36.2]
ityevamuktaśca nipīḍitaśca tayāsavarṇasvanayā jagāda | [SaundĀ, 4 37.1]
evaṃ kariṣyāmi vimuñca caṇḍi yāvad gururdūragato na me saḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 37.2]
tataḥ stanodvartitacandanābhyāṃ mukto bhujābhyāṃ na tu mānasena | [SaundĀ, 4 38.1]
vihāya veṣaṃ madanānurūpaṃ satkārayogyaṃ sa vapurbabhāra | [SaundĀ, 4 38.2]
sā taṃ prayāntaṃ ramaṇaṃ pradadhyau pradhyānaśūnyasthitaniścalākṣī | [SaundĀ, 4 39.1]
sthitoccakarṇā vyapaviddhaśaṣpā bhrāntaṃ mṛgam bhrāntamukhī mṛgīva | [SaundĀ, 4 39.2]
didṛkṣayākṣiptamanā munestu nandaḥ prayāṇaṃ prati tatvare ca | [SaundĀ, 4 40.1]
vivṛttadṛṣṭiśca śanairyayau tāṃ karīva paśyan sa laḍatkareṇum | [SaundĀ, 4 40.2]
chātodarīṃ pīnapayodharoruṃ sa sundarīṃ rukmadarīmivādreḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 41.1]
kākṣeṇa paśyan na tatarpa nandaḥ pibannivaikena jalaṃ kareṇa | [SaundĀ, 4 41.2]
taṃ gauravaṃ buddhagataṃ cakarṣa bhāryānurāgaḥ punarācakarṣa | [SaundĀ, 4 42.1]
so 'niścayānnāpi yayau na tasthau turaṃstaraṃgeṣviva rājahaṃsaḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 42.2]
adarśanaṃ tūpagataśca tasyā harmyāttataścāvatatāra tūrṇam | [SaundĀ, 4 43.1]
śrutvā tato nūpuranisvanaṃ sa punarlalambe hṛdaye gṛhītaḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 43.2]
sa kāmarāgeṇa nigṛhyamāṇo dharmānurāgeṇa ca kṛṣyamāṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 44.1]
jagāma duḥkhena vivartyamānaḥ plavaḥ pratisrota ivāpagāyāḥ | [SaundĀ, 4 44.2]
tataḥ kramairdīrghatamaiḥ pracakrame kathaṃ nu yāto na gururbhavediti | [SaundĀ, 4 45.1]
svajeya tāṃ caiva viśeṣakapriyāṃ kathaṃ priyāmārdraviśeṣakāmiti | [SaundĀ, 4 45.2]
atha sa pathi dadarśa muktamānaṃ pitṛnagare 'pi tathā gatābhimānam | [SaundĀ, 4 46.1]
daśabalamabhito vilambamānaṃ dhvajamanuyāna ivaindramarcyamānam | [SaundĀ, 4 46.2]
{SaundĀ, 5}
athāvatīryāśvarathadvipebhyaḥ śākyā yathāsvarddhigṛhītaveṣāḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 1.1]
mahāpaṇebhyo vyavahāriṇaśca mahāmunau bhaktivaśāt praṇemuḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 1.2]
kecit praṇamyānuyayurmuhūrttaṃ kecit praṇamyārthavaśena jagmuḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 2.1]
kecit svakeṣvāvasatheṣu tasthuḥ kṛtvāñjalīn vīkṣaṇatatparākṣāḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 2.2]
buddhastatastatra narendramārge sroto mahadbhaktimato janasya | [SaundĀ, 5 3.1]
jagāma duḥkhena vigāhamāno jalāgame srota ivāpagāyāḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 3.2]
atho mahadbhiḥ pathi saṃpatadbhiḥ sampūjyamānāya tathāgatāya | [SaundĀ, 5 4.1]
kartuṃ praṇāmaṃ na śaśāka nandastenābhireme tu gurormahimnā | [SaundĀ, 5 4.2]
svaṃ cāvasaṅgaṃ pathi nirmumukṣurbhaktiṃ janasyānyamateśca rakṣan | [SaundĀ, 5 5.1]
nandaṃ ca gehābhimukhaṃ jighṛkṣan mārgaṃ tato 'nyaṃ sugataḥ prapede | [SaundĀ, 5 5.2]
tato viviktaṃ ca viviktacetāḥ sanmārgavin mārgamabhipratasthe | [SaundĀ, 5 6.1]
gatvāgrataścāgryatamāya tasmai nāndīvimuktāya nanāma nandaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 6.2]
śanairvrajanneva sa gauraveṇa paṭāvṛtāṃso vinatārdhakāyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 7.1]
adhonibaddhāñjalirūrdhvanetraḥ sagadgadaṃ vākyamidaṃ babhāṣe | [SaundĀ, 5 7.2]
prāsādasaṃstho bhagavantamantaḥpraviṣṭam aśrauṣam anugrahāya | [SaundĀ, 5 8.1]
atastvarāvānahamabhyupeto gṛhasya kakṣyāmahato 'bhyasūyan | [SaundĀ, 5 8.2]
tatsādhu sādhupriya matpriyārtham tatrāstu bhikṣūttama bhaikṣakālaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 9.1]
asau hi madhyaṃ nabhaso yiyāsuḥ kālaṃ pratismārayatīva sūryaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 9.2]
ityevamuktaḥ praṇatena tena snehābhimānonmukhalocanena | [SaundĀ, 5 10.1]
tādṛṅnimittaṃ sugataścakāra nāhārakṛtyaṃ sa yathā viveda | [SaundĀ, 5 10.2]
tataḥ sa kṛtvā munaye praṇāmaṃ gṛhaprayāṇāya matiṃ cakāra | [SaundĀ, 5 11.1]
anugrahārthaṃ sugatastu tasmai pātraṃ dadau puṣkarapatranetraḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 11.2]
tataḥ sa loke dadataḥ phalārthaṃ pātrasya tasyāpratimasya pātram | [SaundĀ, 5 12.1]
jagrāha cāpagrahaṇakṣamābhyāṃ padmopamābhyāṃ prayataḥ karābhyām | [SaundĀ, 5 12.2]
parāṅmukhas tvanyamanaskam ārād vijñāya nandaḥ sugataṃ gatāstham | [SaundĀ, 5 13.1]
hastasthapātro 'pi gṛhaṃ yiyāsuḥ sasāra mārgānmunimīkṣamāṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 13.2]
bhāryānurāgeṇa yadā gṛhaṃ sa pātraṃ gṛhītvāpi yiyāsureva | [SaundĀ, 5 14.1]
vimohayāmāsa munistatastaṃ rathyāmukhasyāvaraṇena tasya | [SaundĀ, 5 14.2]
nirmokṣabījaṃ hi dadarśa tasya jñānaṃ mṛdu kleśarajaśca tīvram | [SaundĀ, 5 15.1]
kleśānukūlaṃ viṣayātmakaṃ ca nandaṃ yatastaṃ munirācakarṣa | [SaundĀ, 5 15.2]
saṃkleśapakṣo dvividhaśca dṛṣṭastathā dvikalpo vyavadānapakṣaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 16.1]
ātmāśrayo hetubalādhikasya bāhyāśrayaḥ pratyayagauravasya | [SaundĀ, 5 16.2]
ayatnato hetubalādhikastu nirmucyate ghaṭṭitamātra eva | [SaundĀ, 5 17.1]
yatnena tu pratyayaneyabuddhirvimokṣamāpnoti parāśrayeṇa | [SaundĀ, 5 17.2]
nandaḥ sa ca pratyayaneyacetā yaṃ śiśriye tanmayatāmavāpa | [SaundĀ, 5 18.1]
yasmādimaṃ tatra cakāra yatnaṃ taṃ snehapaṅkān munirujjihīrṣan | [SaundĀ, 5 18.2]
nandastu duḥkhena viceṣṭamānaḥ śanairagatyā gurumanvagacchat | [SaundĀ, 5 19.1]
bhāryāmukhaṃ vīkṣaṇalolanetraṃ vicintayannārdraviśeṣakaṃ tat | [SaundĀ, 5 19.2]
tato munistaṃ priyamālyahāraṃ vasantamāsena kṛtābhihāram | [SaundĀ, 5 20.1]
nināya bhagnapramadāvihāraṃ vidyāvihārābhimataṃ vihāram | [SaundĀ, 5 20.2]
dīnaṃ mahākāruṇikastatastaṃ dṛṣṭvā muhūrtaṃ karuṇāyamānaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 21.1]
kareṇa cakrāṅkatalena mūrdhni pasparśa caivedamuvāca cainam | [SaundĀ, 5 21.2]
yāvanna hiṃsraḥ samupaiti kālaḥ śamāya tāvat kuru saumya buddhim | [SaundĀ, 5 22.1]
sarvāsvavasthāsviha vartamānaṃ sarvābhisāreṇa nihanti mṛtyuḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 22.2]
sādhāraṇāt svapnanibhādasārāllolaṃ manaḥ kāmasukhānniyaccha | [SaundĀ, 5 23.1]
havyairivāgneḥ pavaneritasya lokasya kāmairna hi tṛptirasti | [SaundĀ, 5 23.2]
śraddhādhanaṃ śreṣṭhatamaṃ dhanebhyaḥ prajñārasasṛptikaro rasebhyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 24.1]
pradhānamadhyātmasukhaṃ sukhebhyo 'vidyāratirduḥkhatamāratibhyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 24.2]
hitasya vaktā pravaraḥ suhṛdbhyo dharmāya khedo guṇavān śramebhyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 25.1]
jñānāya kṛtyaṃ paramaṃ kriyābhyaḥ kimindriyāṇāmupagamya dāsyam | [SaundĀ, 5 25.2]
tanniścitaṃ bhīklamaśugviyuktaṃ pareṣvanāyattamahāryamanyaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 26.1]
nityaṃ śivaṃ śāntisukhaṃ vṛṇīṣva kim indriyārthārthamanarthamūḍhvā | [SaundĀ, 5 26.2]
jarāsamā nāstyamṛjā prajānāṃ vyādheḥ samo nāsti jagatyanarthaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 27.1]
mṛtyoḥ samaṃ nāsti bhayaṃ pṛthivyāmetattrayaṃ khalvavaśena sevyam | [SaundĀ, 5 27.2]
snehena kaścinna samo 'sti pāśaḥ sroto na tṛṣṇāsamamasti hāri | [SaundĀ, 5 28.1]
rāgāgninā nāsti samastathāgnistaccet trayaṃ nāsti sukhaṃ ca te 'sti | [SaundĀ, 5 28.2]
avaśyabhāvī priyaviprayogastasmācca śoko niyataṃ niṣevyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 29.1]
śokena conmādamupeyivāṃso rājarṣayo 'nye 'pyavaśā viceluḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 29.2]
prajñāmayaṃ varma badhāna tasmānno kṣāntinighnasya hi śokabāṇāḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 30.1]
mahacca dagdhuṃ bhavakakṣajālaṃ saṃdhukṣayālpāgnimivātmatejaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 30.2]
yathauṣadhairhastagataiḥ savidyo na daśyate kaścana pannagena | [SaundĀ, 5 31.1]
tathānapekṣo jitalokamoho na daśyate śokabhujaṃgamena | [SaundĀ, 5 31.2]
āsthāya yogaṃ parigamya tattvaṃ na trāsamāgacchati mṛtyukāle | [SaundĀ, 5 32.1]
ābaddhavarmā sudhanuḥ kṛtāstro jigīṣayā śūra ivāhavasthaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 32.2]
ityevamuktaḥ sa tathāgatena sarveṣu bhūteṣvanukampakena | [SaundĀ, 5 33.1]
dhṛṣṭaṃ girāntarhṛdayena sīdaṃstatheti nandaḥ sugataṃ babhāṣe | [SaundĀ, 5 33.2]
atha pramādācca tamujjihīrṣan matvāgamasyaiva ca pātrabhūtam | [SaundĀ, 5 34.1]
pravrājayānanda śamāya nandamityabravīnmaitramanā maharṣiḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 34.2]
nandaṃ tato 'ntarmanasā rudantamehīti vaidehamunirjagāda | [SaundĀ, 5 35.1]
śanaistatastaṃ samupetya nando na pravrajiṣyāmyahamityuvāca | [SaundĀ, 5 35.2]
śrutvātha nandasya manīṣitaṃ tad buddhāya vaidehamuniḥ śaśaṃsa | [SaundĀ, 5 36.1]
saṃśrutya tasmādapi tasya bhāvaṃ mahāmunirnandamuvāca bhūyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 36.2]
mayyagraje pravrajite 'jitātman bhrātṛṣvanupravrajiteṣu cāsmān | [SaundĀ, 5 37.1]
jñātīṃśca dṛṣṭvā vratino gṛhasthān saṃvinnavitte 'sti na vāsti cetaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 37.2]
rājarṣayaste viditā na nūnaṃ vanāni ye śiśriyire hasantaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 38.1]
niṣṭhīvya kāmānupaśāntikāmāḥ kāmeṣu naivaṃ kṛpaṇeṣu saktāḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 38.2]
bhūyaḥ samālokya gṛheṣu doṣān niśāmya tattyāgakṛtaṃ ca śarma | [SaundĀ, 5 39.1]
naivāsti moktuṃ matirālayaṃ te deśaṃ mumūrṣoriva sopasargam | [SaundĀ, 5 39.2]
saṃsārakāntāraparāyaṇasya śive kathaṃ te pathi nārurukṣā | [SaundĀ, 5 40.1]
āropyamāṇasya tameva mārgaṃ bhraṣṭasya sārthādiva sārthikasya | [SaundĀ, 5 40.2]
yaḥ sarvato veśmani dahyamāne śayīta mohānna tato vyapeyāt | [SaundĀ, 5 41.1]
kālāgninā vyādhijarāśikhena loke pradīpte sa bhavet pramattaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 41.2]
praṇīyamānaśca yathā vadhāya matto hasecca pralapecca vadhyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 42.1]
mṛtyau tathā tiṣṭhati pāśahaste śocyaḥ pramādyan viparītacetāḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 42.2]
yadā narendrāśca kuṭumbinaśca vihāya bandhūṃśca parigrahāṃśca | [SaundĀ, 5 43.1]
yayuśca yāsyanti ca yānti caiva priyeṣvanityeṣu kuto 'nurodhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 43.2]
kiṃcinna paśyāmi ratasya yatra tadanyabhāvena bhavenna duḥkham | [SaundĀ, 5 44.1]
tasmāt kvacinna kṣamate prasaktiryadi kṣamastadvigamānna śokaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 44.2]
tatsaumya lolaṃ parigamya lokaṃ māyopamaṃ citramivendrajālam | [SaundĀ, 5 45.1]
priyābhidhānaṃ tyaja mohajālaṃ chettuṃ matiste yadi duḥkhajālam | [SaundĀ, 5 45.2]
varaṃ hitodarkam aniṣṭamannaṃ na svādu yat syādahitānubaddham | [SaundĀ, 5 46.1]
yasmādahaṃ tvāṃ viniyojayāmi śive śucau vartmani vipriye 'pi | [SaundĀ, 5 46.2]
bālasya dhātrī vinigṛhya loṣṭaṃ yathoddharatyāsyapuṭapraviṣṭam | [SaundĀ, 5 47.1]
tathojjihīrṣuḥ khalu rāgaśalyaṃ tattvāmavocaṃ paruṣaṃ hitāya | [SaundĀ, 5 47.2]
aniṣṭamapyauṣadhamāturāya dadāti vaidyaśca yathā nigṛhya | [SaundĀ, 5 48.1]
tadvanmayoktaṃ pratikūlametattubhyaṃ hitodarkamanugrahāya | [SaundĀ, 5 48.2]
tadyāvadeva kṣaṇasaṃnipāto na mṛtyurāgacchati yāvadeva | [SaundĀ, 5 49.1]
yāvadvayo yogavidhau samarthaṃ buddhiṃ kuru śreyasi tāvadeva | [SaundĀ, 5 49.2]
ityevamuktaḥ sa vināyakena hitaiṣiṇā kāruṇikena nandaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 50.1]
kartāsmi sarvaṃ bhagavan vacaste tathā yathājñāpayasītyuvāca | [SaundĀ, 5 50.2]
ādāya vaidehamunistatastaṃ nināya saṃśliṣya viceṣṭamānam | [SaundĀ, 5 51.1]
vyayojayaccāśrupariplutākṣaṃ keśaśriyaṃ chatranibhasya mūrdhnaḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 51.2]
atho nataṃ tasya mukhaṃ sabāṣpaṃ pravāsyamāneṣu śiroruheṣu | [SaundĀ, 5 52.1]
vakrāgranālaṃ nalinaṃ taḍāge varṣodakaklinnamivābabhāse | [SaundĀ, 5 52.2]
nandastatas tarukaṣāyaviraktavāsāś cintāvaśo navagṛhīta iva dvipendraḥ | [SaundĀ, 5 53.1]
pūrṇaḥ śaśī bahulapakṣagataḥ kṣapānte bālātapena pariṣikta ivābabhāse | [SaundĀ, 5 53.2]
{SaundĀ, 6}
tato hṛte bhartari gauraveṇa prītau hṛtāyāmaratau kṛtāyām | [SaundĀ, 6 1.1]
tatraiva harmyopari vartamānā na sundarī saiva tadā babhāse | [SaundĀ, 6 1.2]
sā bharturabhyāgamanapratīkṣā gavākṣamākramya payodharābhyām | [SaundĀ, 6 2.1]
dvāronmukhī harmyatalāllalambe mukhena tiryaṅnatakuṇḍalena | [SaundĀ, 6 2.2]
vilambahārā calayoktrakā sā tasmād vimānād vinatā cakāśe | [SaundĀ, 6 3.1]
tapaḥkṣayādapsarasāṃ vareva cyutaṃ vimānāt priyamīkṣamāṇā | [SaundĀ, 6 3.2]
sā khedasaṃsvinnalalāṭakena niśvāsaniṣpītaviśeṣakeṇa | [SaundĀ, 6 4.1]
cintācalākṣeṇa mukhena tasthau bharttāramanyatra viśaṅkamānā | [SaundĀ, 6 4.2]
tataścirasthānapariśrameṇa sthitaiva paryaṅkatale papāta | [SaundĀ, 6 5.1]
tiryakca śiśye pravikīrṇahārā sapādukaikārdhavilambapādā | [SaundĀ, 6 5.2]
athātra kācit pramadā sabāṣpāṃ tāṃ duḥkhitāṃ draṣṭum anīpsamānā | [SaundĀ, 6 6.1]
prāsādasopānatalapraṇādaṃ cakāra padbhyāṃ sahasā rudantī | [SaundĀ, 6 6.2]
tasyāśca sopānatalapraṇādaṃ śrutvaiva tūrṇaṃ punarutpapāta | [SaundĀ, 6 7.1]
prītyāṃ prasaktaiva ca saṃjaharṣa priyopayānaṃ pariśaṅkamānā | [SaundĀ, 6 7.2]
sā trāsayantī valabhīpuṭasthān pārāvatān nūpuranisvanena | [SaundĀ, 6 8.1]
sopānakukṣiṃ prasasāra harṣād bhraṣṭaṃ dukūlāntam acintayantī | [SaundĀ, 6 8.2]
tāmaṅganāṃ prekṣya ca vipralabdhā niśvasya bhūyaḥ śayanaṃ prapede | [SaundĀ, 6 9.1]
vivarṇavaktrā na rarāja cāśu vivarṇacandreva himāgame dyauḥ | [SaundĀ, 6 9.2]
sā duḥkhitā bhartturadarśanena kāmena kopena ca dahyamānā | [SaundĀ, 6 10.1]
kṛtvā kare vaktramupopaviṣṭā cintānadīṃ śokajalāṃ tatāra | [SaundĀ, 6 10.2]
tasyāḥ mukhaṃ padmasapatnabhūtaṃ pāṇau sthitaṃ pallavarāgatāmre | [SaundĀ, 6 11.1]
chāyāmayasyāmbhasi paṅkajasya babhau nataṃ padmamivopariṣṭāt | [SaundĀ, 6 11.2]
sā strīsvabhāvena vicintya tattad dṛṣṭānurāge 'bhimukhe 'pi patyau | [SaundĀ, 6 12.1]
dharmāśrite tattvam avindamānā saṃkalpya tattadvilalāpa tattat | [SaundĀ, 6 12.2]
eṣyāmyanāśyānaviśeṣakāyāṃ tvayīti kṛtvā mayi tāṃ pratijñām | [SaundĀ, 6 13.1]
kasmānnu hetordayitapratijñaḥ so 'dya priyo me vitathapratijñaḥ | [SaundĀ, 6 13.2]
āryasya sādhoḥ karuṇātmakasya mannityabhīroratidakṣiṇasya | [SaundĀ, 6 14.1]

ratipriyasya priyavartino me priyasya nūnaṃ hṛdayaṃ viraktam | [SaundĀ, 6 15.1]
tathāpi rāgo yadi tasya hi syān maccittarakṣī na sa nāgataḥ syāt | [SaundĀ, 6 15.2]
rūpeṇa bhāvena ca madviśiṣṭā priyeṇa dṛṣṭā niyataṃ tato 'nyā | [SaundĀ, 6 16.1]
tathā hi kṛtvā mayi moghasāntvaṃ lagnāṃ satīṃ māmāgamad vihāya | [SaundĀ, 6 16.2]
bhaktiṃ sa buddhaṃ prati yām avocattasya prayātuṃ mayi so 'padeśaḥ | [SaundĀ, 6 17.1]
munau prasādo yadi tasya hi syānmṛtyorivogrādanṛtād bibhīyāt | [SaundĀ, 6 17.2]
sevārtham ādarśanam anyacitto vibhūṣayantyā mama dhārayitvā | [SaundĀ, 6 18.1]
bibharti so 'nyasya janasya taṃ cennamo 'stu tasmai calasauhṛdāya | [SaundĀ, 6 18.2]

yastvāṃ priyo nābhyacarat kadācittamanyathā yāsyatikātarāsi | [SaundĀ, 6 21.2]

pragṛhya bāhū virurāva coccairhṛdīva digdhābhihatā kareṇuḥ | [SaundĀ, 6 24.2]
sā rodanāroṣitaraktadṛṣṭiḥ saṃtāpasaṃkṣobhitagātrayaṣṭiḥ | [SaundĀ, 6 25.1]

sā padmarāgaṃ vasanaṃ vasānā padmānanā padmadalāyatākṣī | [SaundĀ, 6 26.1]
padmā vipadmā patiteva lakṣmīḥ śuśoṣa padmasragivātapena | [SaundĀ, 6 26.2]
saṃcintya saṃcintya guṇāṃśca bharturdīrghaṃ niśaśvāsa tatāma caiva | [SaundĀ, 6 27.1]
vibhūṣaṇaśrīnihite prakoṣṭhe tāmre karāgre ca vinirdudhāva | [SaundĀ, 6 27.2]

nirbhūṣaṇā sā patitā cakāśe viśīrṇapuṣpastabakā lateva | [SaundĀ, 6 28.2]
dhṛtaḥ priyeṇāyamabhūnmameti rukmatsaruṃ darpaṇamāliliṅge | [SaundĀ, 6 29.1]
yatnācca vinyastatamālapatrau ruṣṭeva dhṛṣṭaṃ pramamārja gaṇḍau | [SaundĀ, 6 29.2]
sā cakravākīva bhṛśaṃ cukūja śyenāgrapakṣakṣatacakravākā | [SaundĀ, 6 30.1]
vispardhamāneva vimānasaṃsthaiḥ pārāvataiḥ kūjanalolakaṇṭhaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 6 30.2]

rukmāṅgapāde śayane mahārhe na śarma lebhe pariceṣṭamānā | [SaundĀ, 6 31.2]
saṃdṛśya bhartuśca vibhūṣaṇāni vāsāṃsi vīṇāprabhṛtīṃśca līlāḥ | [SaundĀ, 6 32.1]
tamo viveśābhinanāda coccaiḥ paṅkāvatīrṇeva ca saṃsasāda | [SaundĀ, 6 32.2]
sā sundarī śvāsacalodarī hi vajrāgnisaṃbhinnadarīguheva | [SaundĀ, 6 33.1]

antargṛhādāruruhurvimānaṃ trāsena kinnarya ivādripṛṣṭham | [SaundĀ, 6 35.2]

yā tatra tāsāṃ vacasopapannā mānyā ca tasyā vayasādhikā ca | [SaundĀ, 6 38.1]
sā pṛṣṭhatastāṃ tu samāliliṅge pramṛjya cāśrūṇi vacāṃsyuvāca | [SaundĀ, 6 38.2]
rājarṣivadhvāstava nānurūpo dharmāśrite bhartari jātu śokaḥ | [SaundĀ, 6 39.1]
ikṣvākuvaṃśe hyabhikāṅkṣitāni dāyādyabhūtāni tapovanāni | [SaundĀ, 6 39.2]
prāyeṇa mokṣāya viniḥsṛtānāṃ śākyarṣabhāṇāṃ viditāḥ striyaste | [SaundĀ, 6 40.1]
tapovanānīva gṛhāṇi yāsāṃ sādhvīvrataṃ kāmavadāśritānām | [SaundĀ, 6 40.2]
yadyanyayā rūpaguṇādhikatvād bharttā hṛtaste kuru bāṣpamokṣam | [SaundĀ, 6 41.1]
manasvinī rūpavatī guṇāḍhyā hṛdi kṣate kātra hi nāśru muñcet | [SaundĀ, 6 41.2]
athāpi kiṃcid vyasanaṃ prapanno mā caiva tad bhūt sadṛśo 'tra bāṣpaḥ | [SaundĀ, 6 42.1]
ato viśiṣṭaṃ na hi duḥkhamasti kulodgatāyāḥ patidevatāyāḥ | [SaundĀ, 6 42.2]
atha tvidānīṃ laḍitaḥ sukhena svasthaḥ phalastho vyasanānyadṛṣṭvā | [SaundĀ, 6 43.1]
vītaspṛho dharmamanuprapannaḥ kiṃ viklavā rodiṣi harṣakāle | [SaundĀ, 6 43.2]
ityevamuktāpi bahuprakāraṃ snehāttayā naiva dhṛtiṃ cakāra | [SaundĀ, 6 44.1]
athāparā tāṃ manaso 'nukūlaṃ kālopapannaṃ praṇayāduvāca | [SaundĀ, 6 44.2]
bravīmi satyaṃ suviniścitaṃ me prāptaṃ priyaṃ drakṣyasi śīghrameva | [SaundĀ, 6 45.1]
tvayā vinā sthāsyati tatra nāsau sattvāśrayaścetanayeva hīnaḥ | [SaundĀ, 6 45.2]
aṅke 'pi lakṣmyā na sa nirvṛtaḥ syāt tvaṃ tasya pārśve yadi tatra na syāḥ | [SaundĀ, 6 46.1]
āpatsu kṛcchrāsvapi cāgatāsu tvāṃ paśyatastasya bhavenna duḥkham | [SaundĀ, 6 46.2]

{SaundĀ, 7}
liṅgaṃ tataḥ śāstṛvidhipradiṣṭaṃ gātreṇa bibhranna tu cetasā tat | [SaundĀ, 7 1.1]
bhāryāgataireva manovitarkair jehrīyamāṇo na nananda nandaḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 1.2]
sa puṣpamāsasya ca puṣpalakṣmyā sarvābhisāreṇa ca puṣpaketoḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 2.1]
yānīyabhāvena ca yauvanasya vihārasaṃstho na śamaṃ jagāma | [SaundĀ, 7 2.2]
sthitaḥ saḥ dīnaḥ sahakāravīthyām ālīnasaṃmūrchitaṣaṭpadāyām | [SaundĀ, 7 3.1]
bhṛśaṃ jajṛmbhe yugadīrghabāhurdhyātvā priyāṃ cāpamivācakarṣa | [SaundĀ, 7 3.2]
sa pītakakṣodamiva pratīcchan cūtadrumebhyastanupuṣpavarṣam | [SaundĀ, 7 4.1]
dīrghaṃ niśaśvāsa vicintya bhāryāṃ navagraho nāga ivāvaruddhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 4.2]
śokasya hartā śaraṇāgatānāṃ śokasya kartā pratigarvitānām | [SaundĀ, 7 5.1]
aśokamālambya sa jātaśokaḥ priyāṃ priyāśokavanāṃ śuśoca | [SaundĀ, 7 5.2]
priyāṃ priyāyāḥ pratanuṃ priyaṅguṃ niśāmya bhītāmiva niṣpatantīm | [SaundĀ, 7 6.1]
sasmāra tāmaśrumukhīṃ sabāṣpaḥ priyāṃ priyaṅguprasavāvadātām | [SaundĀ, 7 6.2]
puṣpāvanaddhe tilakadrumasya dṛṣṭvānyapuṣṭāṃ śikhare niviṣṭām | [SaundĀ, 7 7.1]
saṃkalpayāmāsa śikhāṃ priyāyāḥ śuklāṃśuke 'ṭṭālamapāśritāyāḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 7.2]
latāṃ praphullāmatimuktakasya cūtasya pārśve parirabhya jātām | [SaundĀ, 7 8.1]

lelihyamānaiśca madhu dvirephaiḥ svanadvanaṃ tasya mano nunoda | [SaundĀ, 7 11.2]
sa tatra bhāryāraṇisaṃbhavena vitarkadhūmena tamaḥśikhena | [SaundĀ, 7 12.1]
kāmāgnināntarhṛdi dahyamāno vihāya dhairyaṃ vilalāpa tattat | [SaundĀ, 7 12.2]
adyāvagacchāmi suduṣkaraṃ te cakruḥ kariṣyanti ca kurvate ca | [SaundĀ, 7 13.1]
tyaktvā priyāmaśrumukhīṃ tapo ye ceruścariṣyanti caranti caiva | [SaundĀ, 7 13.2]
tāvad dṛḍhaṃ bandhanamasti loke na dāravaṃ tāntavamāyasaṃ vā | [SaundĀ, 7 14.1]

chittvā ca bhittvā ca hi yānti tāni svapauruṣāccaiva suhṛdbalācca | [SaundĀ, 7 15.1]

ahaṃ gṛhītvāpi hi bhikṣuliṅgaṃ bhrātṝṣiṇā dvir guruṇānuśiṣṭaḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 17.1]
sarvāsvavasthāsu labhe na śāntiṃ priyāviyogādiva cakravākaḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 17.2]

asmai namo 'stu sthiraniścayāya nivṛttakautūhalavismayāya | [SaundĀ, 7 22.1]

cacāla dhairyānmunir ṛṣyaśṛṅgaḥ śailo mahīkampa ivoccaśṛṅgaḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 34.2]

sa gādhijaścāpahṛto ghṛtācyā samā daśaikaṃ divasaṃ viveda | [SaundĀ, 7 35.2]
tathaiva kandarpaśarābhimṛṣṭo rambhāṃ prati sthūlaśirā mumūrcha | [SaundĀ, 7 36.1]
yaḥ kāmaroṣātmatayānapekṣaḥ śaśāpa tām apratigṛhyamāṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 36.2]
pramadvarāyāṃ ca ruruḥ priyāyāṃ bhujaṅgamenāpahṛtendriyāyām | [SaundĀ, 7 37.1]
saṃdṛśya saṃdṛśya jaghāna sarpān priyaṃ na roṣeṇa tapo rarakṣa | [SaundĀ, 7 37.2]

tathorvaśīmapsarasaṃ vicintya rājarṣirunmādam agacchad aiḍaḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 38.2]
rakto girermūrdhani menakāyāṃ kāmātmakatvācca sa tālajaṅghaḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 39.1]

nāśaṃ gatāyāṃ paramāṅganāyāṃ gaṃgājale 'naṅgaparītacetāḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 40.1]
jahnuśca gaṅgāṃ nṛpatirbhujābhyāṃ rurodha maināka ivācalendraḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 40.2]

kulapradīpaḥ pratipasya sūnuḥ śrīmattanuḥ śantanurasvatantraḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 41.2]

sadvṛttavarmā kila somavarmā babhrāma citodbhavabhinnavarmā | [SaundĀ, 7 42.2]
