balena senāka iti prakāśaḥ senāpatirdeva ivāttasenaḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 43.2]
svargaṃ gate bhartari śantanau ca kālīṃ jihīrṣan janamejayaḥ saḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 44.1]
avāpa bhīṣmāt samavetya mṛtyuṃ na tadgataṃ manmathamutsasarja | [SaundĀ, 7 44.2]
śaptaśca pāṇḍurmadanena nūnaṃ strīsaṃgame mṛtyumavāpsyasīti | [SaundĀ, 7 45.1]
jagāma mādrīṃ na maharṣiśāpādasevyasevī vimamarśa mṛtyum | [SaundĀ, 7 45.2]
evaṃvidhā devanṛparṣisaṅghāḥ strīṇāṃ vaśaṃ kāmavaśena jagmuḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 46.1]
dhiyā ca sāreṇa ca durbalaḥ san priyām apaśyan kimu viklavo 'ham | [SaundĀ, 7 46.2]
yāsyāmi tasmād gṛhameva bhūyaḥ kāmaṃ kariṣye vidhivat sakāmam | [SaundĀ, 7 47.1]
na hyanyacittasya calendriyasya liṅgaṃ kṣamaṃ dharmapathāccyutasya | [SaundĀ, 7 47.2]
pāṇau kapālamavadhārya vidhāya mauṇḍyaṃ mānaṃ nidhāya vikṛtaṃ paridhāya vāsaḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 48.1]
yasyoddhavo na dhṛtirasti na śāntirasti citrapradīpa iva so 'sti ca nāsti caiva | [SaundĀ, 7 48.2]
yo niḥsṛtaśca na ca niḥsṛtakāmarāgaḥ kāṣāyamudvahati yo na ca niṣkaṣāyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 49.1]
pātraṃ bibharti ca guṇairna ca pātrabhūto liṅgaṃ vahannapi sa naiva gṛhī na bhikṣuḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 49.2]
na nyāyyamanvayavataḥ parigṛhya liṅgaṃ bhūyo vimoktumiti yo 'pi hi me vicāraḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 50.1]
so 'pi praṇaśyati vicintya nṛpapravīrāṃstānye tapovanamapāsya gṛhāṇyatīyuḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 50.2]
śālvādhipo hi sasuto 'pi tathāmbarīṣo rāmo 'ndha eva sa ca sāṃskṛtirantidevaḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 51.1]
cīrāṇyapāsya dadhire punaraṃśukāni chittvā jaṭāśca kuṭilā mukuṭāni babhruḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 51.2]
tasmād bhikṣārthaṃ mama gururito yāvadeva prayātastyaktvā kāṣāyaṃ gṛham ahamitas tāvad eva prayāsye | [SaundĀ, 7 52.1]
pūjyaṃ liṅgaṃ hi skhalitamanaso bibhrataḥ kliṣṭabuddhernāmutrārthaḥ syādupahatamaternāpyayaṃ jīvalokaḥ | [SaundĀ, 7 52.2]
{SaundĀ, 8}
atha nandamadhīralocanaṃ gṛhayānotsukamutsukotsukam | [SaundĀ, 8 1.1]
abhigamya śivena cakṣuṣā śramaṇaḥ kaściduvāca maitryā | [SaundĀ, 8 1.2]
kimidaṃ mukhamaśrudurdinaṃ hṛdayasthaṃ vivṛṇoti te tamaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 2.1]
dhṛtimehi niyaccha vikriyāṃ na hi bāṣpaśca śamaśca śobhate | [SaundĀ, 8 2.2]
dvividhā samudeti vedanā niyataṃ cetasi deha eva ca | [SaundĀ, 8 3.1]
śrutavidhyupacārakovidā dvividhā eva tayościkitsakāḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 3.2]
tadiyaṃ yadi kāyikī rujā bhiṣaje tūrṇamanūnamucyatām | [SaundĀ, 8 4.1]
viniguhya hi rogamāturo nacirāttīvramanarthamṛcchati | [SaundĀ, 8 4.2]
atha duḥkhamidaṃ manomayaṃ vada vakṣyāmi yadatra bheṣajam | [SaundĀ, 8 5.1]
manaso hi rajastamasvino bhiṣajo 'dhyātmavidaḥ parīkṣakāḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 5.2]
nikhilena ca satyamucyatāṃ yadi vācyaṃ mayi saumya manyase | [SaundĀ, 8 6.1]
gatayo vividhā hi cetasāṃ bahuguhyāni mahākulāni ca | [SaundĀ, 8 6.2]
iti tena sa coditastadā vyavasāyaṃ pravivakṣur ātmanaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 7.1]
avalambya kare kareṇa taṃ praviveśānyatarad vanāntaram | [SaundĀ, 8 7.2]
atha tatra śucau latāgṛhe kusumodgāriṇi tau niṣedatuḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 8.1]
mṛdubhirmṛdumāruteritairupagūḍhāviva bālapallavaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 8.2]
sa jagāda tataścikīrṣitaṃ ghananiśvāsagṛhītamantarā | [SaundĀ, 8 9.1]
śrutavāgviśadāya bhikṣave viduṣā pravrajitena durvacam | [SaundĀ, 8 9.2]
sadṛśaṃ yadi dharmacāriṇaḥ satataṃ prāṇiṣu maitracetasaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 10.1]
adhṛtau yadi hitaiṣitā mayi te syāt karuṇātmanaḥ sataḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 10.2]
ata eva ca me viśeṣataḥ pravivakṣā kṣamavādini tvayi | [SaundĀ, 8 11.1]
na hi bhāvamimaṃ calātmane kathayeyaṃ bruvate 'pyasādhave | [SaundĀ, 8 11.2]
tadidaṃ śṛṇu me samāsato na rame dharmavidhāvṛte priyām | [SaundĀ, 8 12.1]
girisānuṣu kāminīmṛte kṛtaretā iva kinnaraścaran | [SaundĀ, 8 12.2]
vanavāsasukhāt parāṅmukhaḥ prayiyāsā gṛhameva yena me | [SaundĀ, 8 13.1]
na hi śarma labhe tayā vinā nṛpatirhīna ivottamaśriyā | [SaundĀ, 8 13.2]
atha tasya niśamya tadvacaḥ priyabhāryābhimukhasya śocataḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 14.1]
śramaṇaḥ sa śiraḥ prakampayannijagādātmagataṃ śanairidam | [SaundĀ, 8 14.2]
kṛpaṇaṃ bata yūthalālaso mahato vyādhabhayād viniḥsṛtaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 15.1]
pravivikṣati vāgurāṃ mṛgaścapalo gītaraveṇa vañcitaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 15.2]
vihagaḥ khalu jālasaṃvṛto hitakāmena janena mokṣitaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 16.1]
vicaran phalapuṣpavadvanaṃ pravivikṣuḥ svayameva pañjaram | [SaundĀ, 8 16.2]
kalabhaḥ kariṇā khalūddhṛto bahupaṅkād viṣamānnadītalāt | [SaundĀ, 8 17.1]
jalatarṣavaśena tāṃ punaḥ saritaṃ grāhavatīṃ titīrṣati | [SaundĀ, 8 17.2]
śaraṇe sabhujaṅgame svapan pratibuddhena pareṇa bodhitaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 18.1]
taruṇaḥ khalu jātavibhramaḥ svayamugraṃ bhujagaṃ jighṛkṣati | [SaundĀ, 8 18.2]
mahatā khalu jātavedasā jvalitādutpatito vanadrumāt | [SaundĀ, 8 19.1]
punaricchati nīḍatṛṣṇayā patituṃ tatra gatavyatho dvijaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 19.2]
avaśaḥ khalu kāmamūrcchayā priyayā śyenabhayād vinākṛtaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 20.1]
na dhṛtiṃ samupaiti na hriyaṃ karuṇaṃ jīvati jīvajīvakaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 20.2]
akṛtātmatayā tṛṣānvito ghṛṇayā caiva dhiyā ca varjitaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 21.1]
aśanaṃ khalu vāntamātmanā kṛpaṇaḥ śvā punarattumicchati | [SaundĀ, 8 21.2]
iti manmathaśokakarṣitaṃ tamanudhyāya muhurnirīkṣya ca | [SaundĀ, 8 22.1]
śramaṇaḥ sa hitābhikāṅkṣayā guṇavad vākyamuvāca vipriyam | [SaundĀ, 8 22.2]
avicārayataḥ śubhāśubhaṃ viṣayeṣveva niviṣṭacetasaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 23.1]
upapannamalabdhacakṣuṣo na ratiḥ śreyasi ced bhavettava | [SaundĀ, 8 23.2]
śravaṇe grahaṇe 'tha dhāraṇe paramārthāvagame manaḥśame | [SaundĀ, 8 24.1]
aviṣaktamateś calātmano na hi dharme 'bhiratirvidhīyate | [SaundĀ, 8 24.2]
viṣayeṣu tu doṣadarśinaḥ parituṣṭasya śuceramāninaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 25.1]
śamakarmasu yuktacetasaḥ kṛtabuddhena ratirna vidyate | [SaundĀ, 8 25.2]
ramate tṛṣito dhanaśriyā ramate kāmasukhena bāliśaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 26.1]
ramate praśamena sajjanaḥ paribhogān paribhūya vidyayā | [SaundĀ, 8 26.2]
api ca prathitasya dhīmataḥ kulajasyārcitaliṅgadhāriṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 27.1]
sadṛśī na gṛhāya cetanā praṇatirvāyuvaśād gireriva | [SaundĀ, 8 27.2]
spṛhayet parasaṃśritāya yaḥ paribhūyātmavaśāṃ svatantratām | [SaundĀ, 8 28.1]
upaśāntipathe śive sthitaḥ spṛhayeddoṣavate gṛhāya saḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 28.2]
vyasanābhihato yathā viśet parimuktaḥ punareva bandhanam | [SaundĀ, 8 29.1]
samupetya vanaṃ tathā punargṛhasaṃjñaṃ mṛgayeta bandhanam | [SaundĀ, 8 29.2]
puruṣaśca vihāya yaḥ kaliṃ punaricchet kalimeva sevitum | [SaundĀ, 8 30.1]
sa vihāya bhajeta bāliśaḥ kalibhūtāmajitendriyaḥ priyām | [SaundĀ, 8 30.2]
saviṣā iva saṃśritā latāḥ parimṛṣṭā iva soragā guhāḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 31.1]
vivṛtā iva cāsayo dhṛtā vyasanāntā hi bhavanti yoṣitaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 31.2]
pramadāḥ samadā madapradāḥ pramadā vītamadā bhayapradāḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 32.1]
iti doṣabhayāvahāśca tāḥ kathamarhanti niṣevaṇaṃ nu tāḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 32.2]
svajanaḥ svajanena bhidyate suhṛdaścāpi suhṛjjanena yat | [SaundĀ, 8 33.1]
paradoṣavicakṣaṇāḥ śaṭhāstadanāryāḥ pracaranti yoṣitaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 33.2]
kulajāḥ kṛpaṇībhavanti yadyadayuktaṃ pracaranti sāhasam | [SaundĀ, 8 34.1]
praviśanti ca yaccamūmukhaṃ rabhasāstatra nimittamaṅganāḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 34.2]
vacanena haranti valgunā niśitena praharanti cetasā | [SaundĀ, 8 35.1]
madhu tiṣṭhati vāci yoṣitāṃ hṛdaye hālahalaṃ mahadviṣam | [SaundĀ, 8 35.2]
pradahan dahano 'pi gṛhyate viśarīraḥ pavano 'pi gṛhyate | [SaundĀ, 8 36.1]
kupito bhujago 'pi gṛhyate pramadānāṃ tu mano na gṛhyate | [SaundĀ, 8 36.2]
na vapurvimṛśanti na śriyaṃ na matiṃ nāpi kulaṃ na vikramam | [SaundĀ, 8 37.1]
praharantyaviśeṣataḥ striyaḥ sarito grāhakulākulā iva | [SaundĀ, 8 37.2]
na vaco madhuraṃ na lālanaṃ smarati strī na ca sauhṛdaṃ kvacit | [SaundĀ, 8 38.1]
kalitā vanitaiva cañcalā tadihāriṣviva nāvalambyate | [SaundĀ, 8 38.2]
adadatsu bhavanti narmadāḥ pradadatsu praviśanti vibhramam | [SaundĀ, 8 39.1]
praṇateṣu bhavanti garvitāḥ pramadāstṛptatarāśca māniṣu | [SaundĀ, 8 39.2]
guṇavatsu caranti bhartṛvad guṇahīneṣu caranti putravat | [SaundĀ, 8 40.1]
dhanavatsu caranti tṛṣṇayā dhanahīneṣu carantyavajñayā | [SaundĀ, 8 40.2]
viṣayād viṣayāntaraṃ gatā pracaratyeva yathā hṛtāpi gauḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 41.1]
anavekṣitapūrvasauhṛdā ramate 'nyatra gatā tathāṅganā | [SaundĀ, 8 41.2]
praviśantyapi hi striyaścitāmanubadhnantyapi muktajīvitāḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 42.1]
api bibhrati caiva yantraṇā na tu bhāvena vahanti sauhṛdam | [SaundĀ, 8 42.2]
ramayanti patīn kathañcana pramadā yāḥ patidevatāḥ kvacit | [SaundĀ, 8 43.1]
calacittatayā sahasraśo ramayante hṛdayaṃ svameva tāḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 43.2]
śvapacaṃ kila senajitsutā cakame mīnaripuṃ kumudvatī | [SaundĀ, 8 44.1]
mṛgarājamatho bṛhadrathā pramadānāmagatirna vidyate | [SaundĀ, 8 44.2]
kuruhaihayavṛṣṇivaṃśajā bahumāyākavaco 'tha śambaraḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 45.1]
munirugratapāśca gautamaḥ samavāpurvanitoddhataṃ rajaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 45.2]
akṛtajñamanāryamasthiraṃ vanitānāmidamīdṛśaṃ manaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 46.1]
kathamarhati tāsu paṇḍito hṛdayaṃ sañjayituṃ calātmasu | [SaundĀ, 8 46.2]
atha sūkṣmamatidvayāśivaṃ laghu tāsāṃ hṛdayaṃ na paśyasi | [SaundĀ, 8 47.1]
kimu kāyamasadgṛhaṃ sravad vanitānāmaśuciṃ na paśyasi | [SaundĀ, 8 47.2]
yadahanyahani pradhāvanairvasanaiścābharaṇaiśca saṃskṛtam | [SaundĀ, 8 48.1]
aśubhaṃ tamasāvṛtekṣaṇaḥ śubhato gacchasi nāvagacchasi | [SaundĀ, 8 48.2]
athavā samavaiṣi tattanūmaśubhāṃ tvaṃ na tu saṃvidasti te | [SaundĀ, 8 49.1]
surabhiṃ vidadhāsi hi kriyāmaśucestatprabhavasya śāntaye | [SaundĀ, 8 49.2]
anulepanamañjanaṃ srajo maṇimuktātapanīyamaṃśukam | [SaundĀ, 8 50.1]
yadi sādhu kimatra yoṣitāṃ sahajaṃ tāsu vicīyatāṃ śuci | [SaundĀ, 8 50.2]
malapaṅkadharā digambarā prakṛtisthairnakhadantaromabhiḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 51.1]
yadi sā tava sundarī bhavenniyataṃ te 'dya na sundarī bhavet | [SaundĀ, 8 51.2]
sravatīmaśuciṃ spṛśecca kaḥ saghṛṇo jarjarabhāṇḍavat striyam | [SaundĀ, 8 52.1]
yadi kevalayā tvacāvṛtā na bhavenmakṣikapatramātrayā | [SaundĀ, 8 52.2]
tvacaveṣṭitamasthipañjaraṃ yadi kāyaṃ samavaiṣi yoṣitām | [SaundĀ, 8 53.1]
madanena ca kṛṣyase balādaghṛṇaḥ khalvadhṛtiśca manmathaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 53.2]
śubhatāmaśubheṣu kalpayan nakhadantatvacakeśaromasu | [SaundĀ, 8 54.1]
avicakṣaṇa kiṃ na paśyasi prakṛtiṃ ca prabhavaṃ ca yoṣitām | [SaundĀ, 8 54.2]
tadavetya manaḥśarīrayor vanitā doṣavatīrviśeṣataḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 55.1]
capalaṃ bhavanotsukaṃ manaḥ pratisaṃkhyānabalena vāryatām | [SaundĀ, 8 55.2]
śrutavān matimān kulodgataḥ paramasya praśamasya bhājanam | [SaundĀ, 8 56.1]
upagamya yathā tathā punarna hi bhettuṃ niyamaṃ tvamarhasi | [SaundĀ, 8 56.2]
abhijanamahato manasvinaḥ priyayaśaso bahumānamicchataḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 57.1]
nidhanamapi varaṃ sthirātmanaścyutavinayasya na caiva jīvitam | [SaundĀ, 8 57.2]
baddhvā yathā hi kavacaṃ pragṛhītacāpo nindyo bhavatyapasṛtaḥ samarād rathasthaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 58.1]
bhaikṣākamabhyupagataḥ parigṛhya liṅgaṃ nindyastathā bhavati kāmahṛtendriyāśvaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 58.2]
hāsyo yathā ca paramābharaṇāmbarasrag bhaikṣaṃ caran dhṛtadhanuścalacitramauliḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 59.1]
vairūpyamabhyupagataḥ parapiṇḍabhojī hāsyastathā gṛhasukhābhimukhaḥ satṛṣṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 59.2]
yathā svannaṃ bhuktvā paramaśayanīye 'pi śayito varāho nirmuktaḥ punaraśuci dhāvet paricitam | [SaundĀ, 8 60.1]
tathā śreyaḥ śṛṇvan praśamasukhamāsvādya guṇavad vanaṃ śāntaṃ hitvā gṛhamabhilaṣet kāmatṛṣitaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 60.2]
yatholkā hastasthā dahati pavanapreritaśikhā yathā pādākrānto daśati bhujagaḥ krodharabhasaḥ | [SaundĀ, 8 61.1]
yathā hanti vyāghraḥ śiśurapi gṛhīto gṛhagataḥ tathā strīsaṃsargo bahuvidhamanarthāya bhavati | [SaundĀ, 8 61.2]
tadvijñāya manaḥśarīraniyatānnārīṣu doṣānimān matvā kāmasukhaṃ nadījalacalaṃ kleśāya śokāya ca | [SaundĀ, 8 62.1]
dṛṣṭvā durbalamāmapātrasadṛśaṃ mṛtyūpasṛṣṭaṃ jagannirmokṣāya kuruṣva buddhimatulāmutkaṇṭhituṃ nārhasi | [SaundĀ, 8 62.2]
{SaundĀ, 9}
athaivamukto 'pi sa tena bhikṣuṇā jagāma naivopaśamaṃ priyāṃ prati | [SaundĀ, 9 1.1]
tathā hi tāmeva tadā sa cintayan na tasya śuśrāva visaṃjñavad vacaḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 1.2]
yathā hi vaidyasya cikīrṣataḥ śivaṃ vaco na gṛhṇāti mumūrṣurāturaḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 2.1]
tathaiva matto balarūpayauvanairhitaṃ na jagrāha sa tasya tadvacaḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 2.2]
na cātra citraṃ yadi rāgapāpmanā mano 'bhibhūyeta tamovṛtātmanaḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 3.1]
narasya pāpmā hi tadā nivartate yadā bhavatyantagataṃ tamastanu | [SaundĀ, 9 3.2]
tatastathākṣiptamavekṣya taṃ tadā balena rūpeṇa ca yauvanena ca | [SaundĀ, 9 4.1]
gṛhaprayāṇaṃ prati ca vyavasthitaṃ śaśāsa nandaṃ śramaṇaḥ sa śāntaye | [SaundĀ, 9 4.2]
balaṃ ca rūpaṃ ca navaṃ ca yauvanaṃ tathāvagacchāmi yathāvagacchasi | [SaundĀ, 9 5.1]
ahaṃ tvidaṃ te trayamavyavasthitaṃ yathāvabudhye na tathāvabudhyase | [SaundĀ, 9 5.2]
idaṃ hi rogāyatanaṃ jarāvaśaṃ nadītaṭānokahavaccalācalam | [SaundĀ, 9 6.1]
na vetsi dehaṃ jalaphenadurbalaṃ balasthatāmātmani yena manyase | [SaundĀ, 9 6.2]
yadānnapānāsanayānakarmaṇām asevanād apyatisevanādapi | [SaundĀ, 9 7.1]
śarīramāsannavipatti dṛśyate bale 'bhimānastava kena hetunā | [SaundĀ, 9 7.2]
himātapavyādhijarākṣudādibhir yadāpyanarthair upamīyate jagat | [SaundĀ, 9 8.1]
jalaṃ śucau māsa ivārkaraśmibhiḥ kṣayaṃ vrajan kiṃ baladṛpta manyase | [SaundĀ, 9 8.2]
tvagasthimāṃsakṣatajātmakaṃ yadā śarīramāhāravaśena tiṣṭhati | [SaundĀ, 9 9.1]
ajasramārtaṃ satatapratikriyaṃ balānvito 'smīti kathaṃ vihanyase | [SaundĀ, 9 9.2]
yathā ghaṭaṃ mṛnmayamāmamāśrito narastitīrṣet kṣubhitaṃ mahārṇavam | [SaundĀ, 9 10.1]
samucchrayaṃ tadvadasāram udvahan balaṃ vyavasyed viṣayārthamudyataḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 10.2]
śarīramāmādapi mṛnmayād ghaṭādidaṃ tu niḥsāratamaṃ mataṃ mama | [SaundĀ, 9 11.1]
ciraṃ hi tiṣṭhed vidhivad dhṛto ghaṭaḥ samucchrayo 'yaṃ sudhṛto 'pi bhidyate | [SaundĀ, 9 11.2]
yadāmbubhūvāyvanalāśca dhātavaḥ sadā viruddhā viṣamā ivoragāḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 12.1]
bhavantyanarthāya śarīramāśritāḥ kathaṃ balaṃ rogavidho vyavasyasi | [SaundĀ, 9 12.2]
prayānti mantraiḥ praśamaṃ bhujaṅgamā na mantrasādhyastu bhavanti dhātavaḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 13.1]
kvacicca kaṃcicca daśanti pannagāḥ sadā ca sarvaṃ ca tudanti dhātavaḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 13.2]
idaṃ hi śayyāsanapānabhojanairguṇaiḥ śarīraṃ ciramapyavekṣitam | [SaundĀ, 9 14.1]
na marṣayatyekamapi vyatikramaṃ yato mahāśīviṣavat prakupyati | [SaundĀ, 9 14.2]
yadā himārto jvalanaṃ niṣevate himaṃ nidāghābhihato 'bhikāṅkṣati | [SaundĀ, 9 15.1]
kṣudhānvito 'nnaṃ salilaṃ tṛṣānvito balaṃ kutaḥ kiṃ ca kathaṃ ca kasya ca | [SaundĀ, 9 15.2]
tadevamājñāya śarīramāturaṃ balānvito 'smīti na mantumarhasi | [SaundĀ, 9 16.1]
asāram asvantam aniścitaṃ jagajjagatyanitye balamavyavasthitam | [SaundĀ, 9 16.2]
kva kārtavīryasya balābhimāninaḥ sahasrabāhor balamarjunasya tat | [SaundĀ, 9 17.1]
cakarta bāhūn yudhi yasya bhārgavaḥ mahānti śṛṅgāṇyaśanir gireriva | [SaundĀ, 9 17.2]
kva tad balaṃ kaṃsavikarṣiṇo haresturaṅgarājasya puṭāvabhedinaḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 18.1]
yamekabāṇena nijaghnivān jarāḥ kramāgatā rūpamivottamaṃ jarā | [SaundĀ, 9 18.2]
diteḥ sutasyāmararoṣakāriṇaścamūrucervā namuceḥ kva tad balam | [SaundĀ, 9 19.1]
yamāhave kruddhamivāntakaṃ sthitaṃ jaghāna phenāvayavena vāsavaḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 19.2]
balaṃ kurūṇāṃ kva ca tattadābhavad yudhi jvalitvā tarasaujasā ca ye | [SaundĀ, 9 20.1]
samitsamiddhā jvalanā ivādhvare hatāsavo bhasmani paryavasthitāḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 20.2]
ato viditvā balavīryamānināṃ balānvitānāmavamarditaṃ balam | [SaundĀ, 9 21.1]
jagajjarāmṛtyuvaśaṃ vicārayan bale 'bhimānaṃ na vidhātumarhasi | [SaundĀ, 9 21.2]
balaṃ mahad yadi vā na manyase kuruṣva yuddhaṃ saha tāvadindriyaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 22.1]
jayaśca te 'trāsti mahacca te balaṃ parājayaśced vitathaṃ ca te balam | [SaundĀ, 9 22.2]
tathā hi vīrāḥ puruṣā na te matā jayanti ye sāśvarathadvipānarīn | [SaundĀ, 9 23.1]
yathā matā vīratarā manīṣiṇo jayanti lolāni ṣaḍindriyāṇi ye | [SaundĀ, 9 23.2]
ahaṃ vapuṣmāniti yacca manyase vicakṣaṇaṃ naitadidaṃ ca gṛhyatām | [SaundĀ, 9 24.1]
kva tadvapuḥ sā ca vapuṣmatī tanurgadasya śāmbasya ca sāraṇasya ca | [SaundĀ, 9 24.2]
yathā mayūraścalacitracandrako bibharti rūpaṃ guṇavat svabhāvataḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 25.1]
śarīrasaṃskāraguṇādṛte tathā bibharti rūpaṃ yadi rūpavānasi | [SaundĀ, 9 25.2]
yadi pratīpaṃ vṛṇuyānna vāsasā na śaucakāle yadi saṃspṛśedapaḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 26.1]
mṛjāviśeṣaṃ yadi nādadīta vā vapurvapuṣman vada kīdṛśaṃ bhavet | [SaundĀ, 9 26.2]
navaṃ vayaścātmagataṃ niśāmya yadgṛhonmukhaṃ te viṣayāptaye manaḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 27.1]
niyaccha tacchailanadīrayopamaṃ drutaṃ hi gacchatyanivarti yauvanam | [SaundĀ, 9 27.2]
ṛturvyatītaḥ parivartate punaḥ kṣayaṃ prayātaḥ punareti candramāḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 28.1]
gataṃ gataṃ naiva tu saṃnivartate jalaṃ nadīnāṃ ca nṛṇāṃ ca yauvanam | [SaundĀ, 9 28.2]
vivarṇitaśmaśru valīvikuñcitaṃ viśīrṇadantaṃ śithilabhru niṣprabham | [SaundĀ, 9 29.1]
yadā mukhaṃ drakṣyasi jarjaraṃ tadā jarābhibhūto vimado bhaviṣyasi | [SaundĀ, 9 29.2]
niṣevya pānaṃ madanīyamuttamaṃ niśāvivāseṣu cirād vimādyati | [SaundĀ, 9 30.1]
narastu matto balarūpayauvanairna kaścid aprāpya jarāṃ vimādyati | [SaundĀ, 9 30.2]
yathekṣuratyantarasaprapīḍito bhuvi praviddho dahanāya śuṣyate | [SaundĀ, 9 31.1]
tathā jarāyantranipīḍitā tanurnipītasārā maraṇāya tiṣṭhati | [SaundĀ, 9 31.2]
yathā hi nṛbhyāṃ karapatramīritaṃ samucchritaṃ dāru bhinattyanekadhā | [SaundĀ, 9 32.1]
tathocchritāṃ pātayati prajāmimāmaharniśābhyāmupasaṃhitā jarā | [SaundĀ, 9 32.2]
smṛteḥ pramoṣo vapuṣaḥ parābhavo rateḥ kṣayo vākchruticakṣuṣāṃ grahaḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 33.1]
śramasya yonirbalavīryayorvadho jarāsamo nāsti śarīriṇāṃ ripuḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 33.2]
idaṃ viditvā nidhanasya daiśikaṃ jarābhidhānaṃ jagato mahadbhayam | [SaundĀ, 9 34.1]
ahaṃ vapuṣmān balavān yuveti vā na mānamāroḍhumanāryamarhasi | [SaundĀ, 9 34.2]
ahaṃ mametyeva ca raktacetasāṃ śarīrasaṃjñā tava yaḥ kalau grahaḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 35.1]
tamutsṛjaivaṃ yadi śāmyatā bhaved bhayaṃ hyahaṃ ceti mameti cārchati | [SaundĀ, 9 35.2]
yadā śarīre na vaśo 'sti kasyacinnirasyamāne vividhairupaplavaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 36.1]
kathaṃ kṣamaṃ vettumahaṃ mameti vā śarīrasaṃjñaṃ gṛhamāpadāmidam | [SaundĀ, 9 36.2]
sapannage yaḥ kugṛhe sadāśucau rameta nityaṃ pratisaṃskṛte 'bale | [SaundĀ, 9 37.1]
sa duṣṭadhātāvaśucau calācale rameta kāye viparītadarśanaḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 37.2]
yathā prajābhyaḥ kunṛpo balād balīn haratyaśeṣaṃ ca na cābhirakṣati | [SaundĀ, 9 38.1]
tathaiva kāyo vasanādisādhanaṃ haratyaśeṣaṃ ca na cānuvartate | [SaundĀ, 9 38.2]
yathā prarohanti tṛṇānyayatnataḥ kṣitau prayatnāt tu bhavanti śālayaḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 39.1]
tathaiva duḥkhāni bhavantyayatnataḥ sukhāni yatnena bhavanti vā na vā | [SaundĀ, 9 39.2]
śarīramārtaṃ parikarṣataścalaṃ na cāsti kiṃcit paramārthataḥ sukham | [SaundĀ, 9 40.1]
sukhaṃ hi duḥkhapratikārasevayā sthite ca duḥkhe tanuni vyavasyati | [SaundĀ, 9 40.2]
yathānapekṣyāgryam apīpsitaṃ sukhaṃ prabādhate duḥkhamupetamaṇvapi | [SaundĀ, 9 41.1]
tathānapekṣyātmani duḥkhamāgataṃ na vidyate kiṃcana kasyacit sukhaṃ | [SaundĀ, 9 41.2]
śarīramīdṛg bahuduḥkhādhruvaṃ phalānurodhādatha nāvagacchasi | [SaundĀ, 9 42.1]
dravatphalebhyo dhṛtiraśmibhirmano nigṛhyatāṃ gauriva śasyalālasā | [SaundĀ, 9 42.2]
na kāmabhogā hi bhavanti tṛptaye havīṃṣi dīptasya vibhāvasoriva | [SaundĀ, 9 43.1]
yathā yathā kāmasukheṣu vartate tathā tathecchā viṣayeṣu vardhate | [SaundĀ, 9 43.2]
yathā ca kuṣṭhavyasanena duḥkhitaḥ pratāpanānnaiva śamaṃ nigacchati | [SaundĀ, 9 44.1]
tathendriyārtheṣvajitendriyaścaranna kāmabhogairupaśāntimṛcchati | [SaundĀ, 9 44.2]
yathā hi bhaiṣajyasukhābhikāṅkṣayā bhajeta rogānna bhajeta tatkṣamam | [SaundĀ, 9 45.1]
tathā śarīre bahuduḥkhabhājane rameta mohād viṣayābhikāṅkṣayā | [SaundĀ, 9 45.2]
anarthakāmaḥ puruṣasya yo janaḥ sa tasya śatruḥ kila tena karmaṇā | [SaundĀ, 9 46.1]
anarthamūlā viṣayāśca kevalā nanu praheyā viṣamā yathārayaḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 46.2]
ihaiva bhūtvā ripavo vadhātmakāḥ prayānti kāle puruṣasya mitratāṃ | [SaundĀ, 9 47.1]
paratra caiveha ca duḥkhahetavo bhavanti kāmā na tu kasyacicchivāḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 47.2]
yathopayuktaṃ rasavarṇagandhavad vadhāya kimpākaphalaṃ na puṣṭaye | [SaundĀ, 9 48.1]
niṣevyamāṇā viṣayāścalātmano bhavantyanarthāya tathā na bhūtaye | [SaundĀ, 9 48.2]
tadetadājñāya vipāpmanātmanā vimokṣadharmādyupasaṃhitaṃ hitam | [SaundĀ, 9 49.1]
juṣasva me sajjanasaṃmataṃ mataṃ pracakṣva vā niścayamudgiran giram | [SaundĀ, 9 49.2]
iti hitamapi bahvapīdamuktaḥ śrutamahatā śramaṇena tena nandaḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 50.1]
na dhṛtimupayayau na śarma lebhe dvirada ivātimado madāndhacetāḥ | [SaundĀ, 9 50.2]
nandasya bhāvamavagamya tataḥ sa bhikṣuḥ pāriplavaṃ gṛhasukhābhimukhaṃ na dharme | [SaundĀ, 9 51.1]
sattvāśayānuśayabhāvaparīkṣakāya buddhāya tattvaviduṣe kathayāṃcakāra | [SaundĀ, 9 51.2]
{SaundĀ, 10}
śrutvā tataḥ sadvratamutsisṛkṣuṃ bhāryāṃ didṛkṣuṃ bhavanaṃ vivikṣum | [SaundĀ, 10 1.1]
nandaṃ nirānandamapetadhairyam abhyujjihīrṣurmunirājuhāva | [SaundĀ, 10 1.2]
taṃ prāptamaprāptavimokṣamārgaṃ papraccha cittaskhalitaṃ sucittaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 2.1]
sa hrīmate hrīvinato jagāda svaṃ niścayaṃ niścayakovidāya | [SaundĀ, 10 2.2]
nandaṃ viditvā sugatastatastaṃ bhāryābhidhāne tamasi bhramantam | [SaundĀ, 10 3.1]
pāṇau gṛhītvā viyadutpapāta malaṃ jale sādhurivojjihīrṣuḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 3.2]
kāṣāyavastrau kanakāvadātau virejatustau nabhasi prasanne | [SaundĀ, 10 4.1]
anyonyasaṃśliṣṭavikīrṇapakṣau saraḥprakīrṇāviva cakravākau | [SaundĀ, 10 4.2]
tau devadārūttamagandhavantaṃ nadīsaraḥprasravaṇaughavantam | [SaundĀ, 10 5.1]
ājagmatuḥ kāñcanadhātumantaṃ devarṣimantaṃ himavantamāśu | [SaundĀ, 10 5.2]
tasmin girau cāraṇasiddhajuṣṭe śive havirdhūmakṛtottarīye | [SaundĀ, 10 6.1]
agamyapārasya nirāśrayasya tau tasthaturdvīpa ivāmbarasya | [SaundĀ, 10 6.2]
śāntendriye tatra munau sthite tu savismayaṃ dikṣu dadarśa nandaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 7.1]
darīśca kuñjāṃśca vanaukasaśca vibhūṣaṇaṃ rakṣaṇameva cādreḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 7.2]
bahvāyate tatra site hi śṛṅge saṃkṣiptabarhaḥ śayito mayūraḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 8.1]
bhuje balasyāyatapīnabāhorvaiḍūryakeyūra ivābabhāse | [SaundĀ, 10 8.2]
manaḥśilādhātuśilāśrayeṇa pītākṛtāṃso virarāja siṃhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 9.1]
saṃtaptacāmīkarabhakticitraṃ rūpyāṅgadaṃ śīrṇamivāmbikasya | [SaundĀ, 10 9.2]
vyāghraḥ klamavyāyatakhelagāmī lāṅgūlacakreṇa kṛtāpasavyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 10.1]
babhau gireḥ prasravaṇaṃ pipāsurditsan pitṛbhyo 'mbha ivāvatīrṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 10.2]
calatkadambe himavannitambe tarau pralambe camaro lalambe | [SaundĀ, 10 11.1]
chettuṃ vilagnaṃ na śaśāka bālaṃ kulodgatāṃ prītimivāryavṛttaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 11.2]
suvarṇagaurāśca kirātasaṃghā mayūrapattrojjvalagātralekhāḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 12.1]
śārdūlapātapratimā guhābhyo niṣpeturudgāra ivācalasya | [SaundĀ, 10 12.2]
darīcarīṇāmatisundarīṇāṃ manoharaśroṇikucodarīṇām | [SaundĀ, 10 13.1]
vṛndāni rejurdiśi kinnarīṇāṃ puṣpotkacānāmiva vallarīṇām | [SaundĀ, 10 13.2]
nagānnagasyopari devadārūnāyāsayantaḥ kapayo viceruḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 14.1]
tebhyaḥ phalaṃ nāpurato 'pajagmurmoghaprasādebhya iveśvarebhyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 14.2]
tasmāttu yūthādapasāryamāṇāṃ niṣpīḍitālaktakaraktavaktrām | [SaundĀ, 10 15.1]
śākhāmṛgīm ekavipannadṛṣṭiṃ dṛṣṭvā munirnandamidaṃ babhāṣe | [SaundĀ, 10 15.2]
kā nanda rūpeṇa ca ceṣṭayā ca saṃpaśyataścārutarā matā te | [SaundĀ, 10 16.1]
eṣā mṛgī vaikavipannadṛṣṭiḥ sa vā jano yatra gatā taveṣṭiḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 16.2]
ityevamuktaḥ sugatena nandaḥ kṛtvā smitaṃ kiṃcididaṃ jagāda | [SaundĀ, 10 17.1]
kva cottamastrī bhagavan vadhūste mṛgī nagakleśakarī kva caiṣā | [SaundĀ, 10 17.2]
tato munistasya niśamya vākyaṃ hetvantaraṃ kiṃcidavekṣamāṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 18.1]
ālambya nandaṃ prayayau tathaiva krīḍāvanaṃ vajradharasya rājñaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 18.2]
ṛtāvṛtāvākṛtimeka eke kṣaṇe kṣaṇe bibhrati yatra vṛkṣāḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 19.1]
citrāṃ samastāmapi kecidanye ṣaṇṇāmṛtūnāṃ śriyamudvahanti | [SaundĀ, 10 19.2]
puṣyanti kecit surabhīrudārā mālāḥ srajaśca granthitā vicitrāḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 20.1]
karṇānukūlānavataṃsakāṃśca pratyarthibhūtāniva kuṇḍalānām | [SaundĀ, 10 20.2]
raktāni phullāḥ kamalāni yatra pradīpavṛkṣā iva bhānti vṛkṣāḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 21.1]
praphullanīlotpalarohiṇo 'nye sonmīlitākṣā eva bhānti vṛkṣāḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 21.2]
nānāvirāgāṇyatha pāṇḍarāṇi suvarṇabhaktivyavabhāsitāni | [SaundĀ, 10 22.1]
atāntavānyekaghanāni yatra sūkṣmāṇi vāsāṃsi phalanti vṛkṣāḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 22.2]
hārān maṇīn uttamakuṇḍalāni keyūravaryāṇyatha nūpurāṇi | [SaundĀ, 10 23.1]
evaṃvidhānyābharaṇāni yatra svargānurūpāṇi phalanti vṛkṣāḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 23.2]
vaiḍūryanālāni ca kāñcanāni padmāni vajrāṅkurakesarāṇi | [SaundĀ, 10 24.1]
sparśakṣamāṇyuttamagandhavanti rohanti niṣkampatalā nalinyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 24.2]
yatrāyatāṃścaiva tatāṃśca tāṃstān vādyasya hetūn suṣirān ghanāṃśca | [SaundĀ, 10 25.1]
phalanti vṛkṣā maṇihemacitrāḥ krīḍāsahāyās tridaśālayānām | [SaundĀ, 10 25.2]
mandāravṛkṣāṃśca kuśeśayāṃśca puṣpānatān kokanadāṃśca vṛkṣān | [SaundĀ, 10 26.1]
ākramya māhātmyaguṇairvirājan rājāyate yatra sa pārijātaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 26.2]
kṛṣṭe tapaḥśīlahalair akhinnais triviṣṭapakṣetratale prasūtāḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 27.1]
evaṃvidhā yatra sadānuvṛttā divaukasāṃ bhogavidhānavṛkṣāḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 27.2]
manaḥśilābhairvadanairvihaṃgā yatrākṣibhiḥ sphāṭikasaṃnibhaiśca | [SaundĀ, 10 28.1]
śāvaiśca pakṣair abhilohitāntair māñjiṣṭhakairardhasitaiśca pādaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 28.2]
citraiḥ suvarṇacchadanaistathānye vaiḍūryanīlair nayanaiḥ prasannaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 29.1]
vihaṃgamāḥ śiñjirikābhidhānā rutairmanaḥśrotraharairbhramanti | [SaundĀ, 10 29.2]
raktābhiragreṣu ca vallarībhirmadhyeṣu cāmīkarapiñjarābhiḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 30.1]
vaiḍūryavarṇābhirupāntamadhyeṣvalaṃkṛtā yatra khagāścaranti | [SaundĀ, 10 30.2]
rociṣṇavo nāma patatriṇo 'nye dīptāgnivarṇā jvalitairivāsyaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 31.1]
bhramanti dṛṣṭīrvapuṣākṣipantaḥ svanaiḥ śubhairapsaraso harantaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 31.2]
yatreṣṭaceṣṭāḥ satataprahṛṣṭā nirartayo nirjaraso viśokāḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 32.1]
svaiḥ karmabhirhīnaviśiṣṭamadhyāḥ svayaṃprabhāḥ puṇyakṛto ramante | [SaundĀ, 10 32.2]
pūrvaṃ tapomūlyaparigraheṇa svargakrayārthaṃ kṛtaniścayānām | [SaundĀ, 10 33.1]
manāṃsi khinnāni tapodhanānāṃ haranti yatrāpsaraso laḍantyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 33.2]
nityotsavaṃ taṃ ca niśāmya lokaṃ nistandrinidrāratiśokarogam | [SaundĀ, 10 34.1]
nando jarāmṛtyuvaśaṃ sadārtaṃ mene śmaśānapratimaṃ nṛlokam | [SaundĀ, 10 34.2]
aindraṃ vanaṃ tacca dadarśa nandaḥ samantato vismayaphulladṛṣṭiḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 35.1]
harṣānvitāścāpsarasaḥ parīyuḥ sagarvamanyonyamavekṣamāṇāḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 35.2]
sadā yuvatyo madanaikakāryāḥ sādhāraṇāḥ puṇyakṛtāṃ vihārāḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 36.1]
divyāśca nirdoṣaparigrahāśca tapaḥphalasyāśrayaṇaṃ surāṇām | [SaundĀ, 10 36.2]
tāsāṃ jagurdhīramudāttamanyāḥ padmāni kāścillalitaṃ babhañjuḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 37.1]
anyonyaharṣān nanṛtustathānyāś citrāṅgahārāḥ stanabhinnahārāḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 37.2]
kāsāṃcidāsāṃ vadanāni rejurvanāntarebhyaścalakuṇḍalāni | [SaundĀ, 10 38.1]
vyāviddhaparṇebhya ivākarebhyaḥ padmāni kāraṇḍavaghaṭṭitāni | [SaundĀ, 10 38.2]
tāḥ niḥsṛtāḥ prekṣya vanāntarebhyastaḍitpatākā iva toyadebhyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 39.1]
nandasya rāgeṇa tanur vivepe jale cale candramasaḥ prabheva | [SaundĀ, 10 39.2]
vapuśca divyaṃ lalitāśca ceṣṭāstataḥ sa tāsāṃ manasā jahāra | [SaundĀ, 10 40.1]
kautūhalāvarjitayā ca dṛṣṭyā saṃśleṣatarṣādiva jātarāgaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 40.2]
sa jātatarṣo 'psarasaḥ pipāsustatprāptaye 'dhiṣṭhitaviklavārtaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 41.1]
lolendriyāśvena manorathena jehrīyamāṇo na dhṛtiṃ cakāra | [SaundĀ, 10 41.2]
yathā manuṣyo malinaṃ hi vāsaḥ kṣāreṇa bhūyo malinīkaroti | [SaundĀ, 10 42.1]
malakṣayārthaṃ na malodbhavārthaṃ rajastathāsmai munirācakarṣa | [SaundĀ, 10 42.2]
doṣāṃśca kāyād bhiṣagujjihīrṣurbhūyo yathā kleśayituṃ yateta | [SaundĀ, 10 43.1]
rāgaṃ tathā tasya munirjighāṃsurbhūyastaraṃ rāgamupānināya | [SaundĀ, 10 43.2]
dīpaprabhāṃ hanti yathāndhakāre sahasraraśmeruditasya dīptiḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 44.1]
manuṣyaloke dyutimaṅganānām antardadhātyapsarasāṃ tathā śrīḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 44.2]
mahacca rūpaṃ svaṇu hanti rūpaṃ śabdo mahān hanti ca śabdamalpam | [SaundĀ, 10 45.1]
gurvī rujā hanti rujāṃ ca mṛdvīṃ sarvo mahān heturaṇorvadhāya | [SaundĀ, 10 45.2]
muneḥ prabhāvācca śaśāka nandastaddarśanaṃ soḍhumasahyamanyaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 46.1]
avītarāgasya hi durbalasya mano dahedapsarasāṃ vapuḥśrīḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 46.2]
matvā tato nandamudīrṇarāgaṃ bhāryānurodhād apavṛttarāgam | [SaundĀ, 10 47.1]
rāgeṇa rāgaṃ pratihantukāmo munirvirāgo giramityuvāca | [SaundĀ, 10 47.2]
etāḥ striyaḥ paśya divaukasastvaṃ nirīkṣya ca brūhi yathārthatattvam | [SaundĀ, 10 48.1]
etāḥ kathaṃ rūpaguṇairmatāste sa vā jano yatra gataṃ manaste | [SaundĀ, 10 48.2]
athāpsaraḥsveva niviṣṭadṛṣṭī rāgāgnināntarhṛdaye pradīptaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 49.1]
sagadgadaṃ kāmaviṣaktacetāḥ kṛtāñjalirvākyamuvāca nandaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 49.2]
haryaṅganāsau muṣitaikadṛṣṭiryadantare syāttava nātha vadhvāḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 50.1]
tadantare 'sau kṛpaṇā vadhūste vapuṣmatīrapsarasaḥ pratītya | [SaundĀ, 10 50.2]
āsthā yathā pūrvamabhūnna kācidanyāsu me strīṣu niśāmya bhāryām | [SaundĀ, 10 51.1]
tasyāṃ tataḥsamprati kācidāsthā na me niśāmyaiva hi rūpamāsām | [SaundĀ, 10 51.2]
yathā pratapto mṛdunātapena dahyeta kaścin mahatānalena | [SaundĀ, 10 52.1]
rāgeṇa pūrvaṃ mṛdunābhitapto rāgāgninānena tathābhidahye | [SaundĀ, 10 52.2]
vāgvāriṇāṃ māṃ pariṣiñca tasmādyāvanna dahye sa ivābjaśatruḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 53.1]
rāgāgniradyaiva hi māṃ didhakṣuḥ kakṣaṃ savṛkṣāgramivotthito 'gniḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 53.2]
prasīda sīdāmi vimuñca mā mune vasundharādhairya na dhairyamasti me | [SaundĀ, 10 54.1]
asūn vimokṣyāmi vimuktamānasa prayaccha vā vāgamṛtaṃ mumūrṣave | [SaundĀ, 10 54.2]
anarthabhogena vighātadṛṣṭinā pramādadaṃṣṭreṇa tamoviṣāgninā | [SaundĀ, 10 55.1]
ahaṃ hi daṣṭo hṛdi manmathāhinā vidhatsva tasmādagadaṃ mahābhiṣak | [SaundĀ, 10 55.2]
anena daṣṭo madanāhinā hi nā na kaścidātmanyanavasthitaḥ sthitaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 56.1]
mumoha bodhyorhyacalātmano mano babhūva dhīmāṃśca sa śantanustanuḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 56.2]
sthite viśiṣṭe tvayi saṃśraye śraye yathā na yāmīha vasan diśaṃ diśam | [SaundĀ, 10 57.1]
yathā ca labdhvā vyasanakṣayaṃ kṣayaṃ vrajāmi tanme kuru śaṃsataḥ sataḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 57.2]
tato jighāṃsurhṛdi tasya tattamastamonudo naktamivotthitaṃ tamaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 58.1]
maharṣicandro jagatastamonudastamaḥprahīṇo nijagāda gautamaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 58.2]
dhṛtiṃ pariṣvajya vidhūya vikriyāṃ nigṛhya tāvacchrutacetasī śṛṇu | [SaundĀ, 10 59.1]
imā yadi prārthayase tvamaṅganā vidhatsva śuklārthamihottamaṃ tapaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 59.2]
imā hi śakyā na balānna sevayā na saṃpradānena na rūpavattayā | [SaundĀ, 10 60.1]
imā hriyante khalu dharmacaryayā sacet praharṣaścara dharmamādṛtaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 60.2]
ihādhivāso divi daivataiḥ samaṃ vanāni ramyāṇyajarāśca yoṣitaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 61.1]
idaṃ phalaṃ svasya śubhasya karmaṇo na dattamanyena na cāpyahetutaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 61.2]
kṣitau manuṣyo dhanurādibhiḥ śramaiḥ striyaḥ kadāciddhi labheta vā na vā | [SaundĀ, 10 62.1]
asaṃśayaṃ yattviha dharmacaryayā bhaveyuretā divi puṇyakarmaṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 62.2]
tadapramatto niyame samudyato ramasva yadyapsaraso 'bhilipsase | [SaundĀ, 10 63.1]
ahaṃ ca te 'tra pratibhūḥ sthire vrate yathā tvamābhirniyataṃ sameṣyasi | [SaundĀ, 10 63.2]
ataḥparaṃ paramamiti vyavasthitaḥ parāṃ dhṛtiṃ paramamunau cakāra saḥ | [SaundĀ, 10 64.1]
tato muniḥ pavana ivāmbarāt patan pragṛhya taṃ punaragamanmahītalam | [SaundĀ, 10 64.2]
{SaundĀ, 11}
tatastā yoṣito dṛṣṭvā nando nandanacāriṇīḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 1.1]
babandha niyamastambhe durdamaṃ capalaṃ manaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 1.2]
so 'niṣṭanaiṣkramyaraso mlānatāmarasopamaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 2.1]
cacāra viraso dharmaṃ niveśyāpsaraso hṛdi | [SaundĀ, 11 2.2]
tathā lolendriyo bhūtvā dayitendriyagocaraḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 3.1]
indriyārthavaśādeva babhūva niyatendriyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 3.2]
kāmacaryāsu kuśalo bhikṣucaryāsu viklavaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 4.1]
paramācāryaviṣṭabdho brahmacaryaṃ cacāra saḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 4.2]
saṃvṛtena ca śāntena tīvreṇa madanena ca | [SaundĀ, 11 5.1]
jalāgneriva saṃsargācchaśāma ca śuśoṣa ca | [SaundĀ, 11 5.2]
svabhāvadarśanīyo 'pi vairūpyamagamat param | [SaundĀ, 11 6.1]
cintayāpsarasāṃ caiva niyamenāyatena ca | [SaundĀ, 11 6.2]
prastāveṣvapi bhāryāyāṃ priyabhāryastathāpi saḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 7.1]
vītarāga ivātasthau na jaharṣa na cukṣubhe | [SaundĀ, 11 7.2]
taṃ vyavasthitamājñāya bhāryārāgāt parāṅmukham | [SaundĀ, 11 8.1]
abhigamyābravīnnandamānandaḥ praṇayādidam | [SaundĀ, 11 8.2]
aho sadṛśamārabdhaṃ śrutamasyābhijanasya ca | [SaundĀ, 11 9.1]
nigṛhītendriyaḥ svastho niyame yadi saṃsthitaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 9.2]
abhiṣvaktasya kāmeṣu rāgiṇo viṣayātmanaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 10.1]
yadiyaṃ saṃvidutpannā neyamalpena hetunā | [SaundĀ, 11 10.2]
vyādhiralpena yatnena mṛduḥ pratinivāryate | [SaundĀ, 11 11.1]
prabalaḥ prabalaireva yatnairnaśyati vā na vā | [SaundĀ, 11 11.2]
durharo mānaso vyādhirbalavāṃśca tavābhavat | [SaundĀ, 11 12.1]
vinivṛtto yadi ca te sarvathā dhṛtimānasi | [SaundĀ, 11 12.2]
duṣkaraṃ sādhvanāryeṇa māninā caiva mārdavam | [SaundĀ, 11 13.1]
atisargaśca lubdhena brahmacaryaṃ ca rāgiṇā | [SaundĀ, 11 13.2]
ekastu mama saṃdehastavāsyāṃ niyame dhṛtau | [SaundĀ, 11 14.1]
atrānunayamicchāmi vaktavyaṃ yadi manyase | [SaundĀ, 11 14.2]
ārjavābhihitaṃ vākyaṃ na ca mantavyamanyathā | [SaundĀ, 11 15.1]
rūkṣamapyāśaye śuddhe rūkṣato naiti sajjanaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 15.2]
apriyaṃ hi hitaṃ snigdhamasnigdhamahitaṃ priyam | [SaundĀ, 11 16.1]
durlabhaṃ tu priyahitaṃ svādu pathyamivauṣadham | [SaundĀ, 11 16.2]
viśvāsaścārthacaryā ca sāmānyaṃ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 17.1]
marṣaṇaṃ praṇayaścaiva mitravṛttiriyaṃ satām | [SaundĀ, 11 17.2]
tadidaṃ tvāṃ vivakṣāmi praṇayānna jighāṃsayā | [SaundĀ, 11 18.1]
tvacchreyo hi vivakṣā me yato nārhāmyupekṣitum | [SaundĀ, 11 18.2]
apsarobhṛtako dharmaṃ carasītyabhidhīyase | [SaundĀ, 11 19.1]
kimidaṃ bhūtamāhosvit parihāso 'yamīdṛśaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 19.2]
yadi tāvadidaṃ satyaṃ vakṣyāmyatra yadauṣadham | [SaundĀ, 11 20.1]
auddhatyamatha vaktṝṇāmabhidhāsyāmi tadrajaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 20.2]
ślakṣṇapūrvamatho tena hṛdi so 'bhihatastadā | [SaundĀ, 11 21.1]
dhyātvā dīrghaṃ niśaśvāsa kiṃciccāvāṅmukho 'bhavat | [SaundĀ, 11 21.2]
tatastasyeṅgitaṃ jñātvā manaḥsaṃkalpasūcakam | [SaundĀ, 11 22.1]
babhāṣe vākyamānando madhurodarkamapriyam | [SaundĀ, 11 22.2]
ākāreṇāvagacchāmi tava dharmaprayojanam | [SaundĀ, 11 23.1]
yajjñātvā tvayi jātaṃ me hāsyaṃ kāruṇyameva ca | [SaundĀ, 11 23.2]
yathāsanārthaṃ skandhena kaścid gurvīṃ śilāṃ vahet | [SaundĀ, 11 24.1]
tadvattvamapi kāmārthaṃ niyamaṃ voḍhumudyataḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 24.2]
titāḍayiṣayāsṛpto yathā meṣo 'pasarpati | [SaundĀ, 11 25.1]
tadvad abrahmacaryāya brahmacaryamidaṃ tava | [SaundĀ, 11 25.2]
cikrīṣanti yathā paṇyaṃ vaṇijo lābhalipsayā | [SaundĀ, 11 26.1]
dharmacaryā tava tathā paṇyabhūtā na śāntaye | [SaundĀ, 11 26.2]
yathā phalaviśeṣārthaṃ bījaṃ vapati kārṣakaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 27.1]
tadvad viṣayakārpaṇyād viṣayāṃstyaktavānasi | [SaundĀ, 11 27.2]
ākāṅkṣecca yathā rogaṃ pratīkārasukhepsayā | [SaundĀ, 11 28.1]
duḥkhamanvicchati bhavāṃstathā viṣayatṛṣṇayā | [SaundĀ, 11 28.2]
yathā paśyati madhveva na prapātamavekṣate | [SaundĀ, 11 29.1]
paśyasyapsarasastadvad bhraṃśamante na paśyasi | [SaundĀ, 11 29.2]
hṛdi kāmāgninā dīpte kāyena vahato vratam | [SaundĀ, 11 30.1]
kimidaṃ brahmacaryaṃ te manasābrahmacāriṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 30.2]
saṃsāre vartamānena yadā cāpsarasastvayā | [SaundĀ, 11 31.1]
prāptāstyaktāśca śataśastābhyaḥ kimiti te spṛhā | [SaundĀ, 11 31.2]
tṛptirnāstīndhanairagnernāmbhasā lavaṇāmbhasaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 32.1]
nāpi kāmaiḥ satṛṣṇasya tasmāt kāmā na tṛptaye | [SaundĀ, 11 32.2]
atṛptau sa kutaḥ śāntiraśāntau ca kutaḥ sukham | [SaundĀ, 11 33.1]
asukhe ca kutaḥ prītiraprītau ca kuto ratiḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 33.2]
riraṃsā yadi te tasmādadhyātme dhīyatāṃ manaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 34.1]
praśāntā cānavadyā ca nāstyadhyātmasamā ratiḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 34.2]
na tatra kāryaṃ tūryaiste na strībhirna vibhūṣaṇaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 35.1]
ekastvaṃ yatra tatrasthastayā ratyābhiraṃsyase | [SaundĀ, 11 35.2]
mānasaṃ balavad duḥkhaṃ tarṣe tiṣṭhati tiṣṭhati | [SaundĀ, 11 36.1]
taṃ tarṣaṃ chinddhi duḥkhaṃ hi tṛṣṇā cāsti ca nāsti ca | [SaundĀ, 11 36.2]
saṃpattau vā vipattau vā divā vā naktameva vā | [SaundĀ, 11 37.1]
kāmeṣu hi satṛṣṇasya na śāntirupapadyate | [SaundĀ, 11 37.2]
kāmānāṃ prārthanā duḥkhā prāptau tṛptirna vidyate | [SaundĀ, 11 38.1]
viyogānniyataḥ śoko viyogaśca dhruvo divi | [SaundĀ, 11 38.2]
kṛtvāpi duṣkaraṃ karma svargaṃ labdhvāpi durlabham | [SaundĀ, 11 39.1]
nṛlokaṃ punarevaiti pravāsāt svagṛhaṃ yathā | [SaundĀ, 11 39.2]
yadā bhraṣṭasya kuśalaṃ śiṣṭaṃ kiṃcinna vidyate | [SaundĀ, 11 40.1]
tiryakṣu pitṛloke vā narake copapadyate | [SaundĀ, 11 40.2]
tasya bhuktavataḥ svarge viṣayānuttamānapi | [SaundĀ, 11 41.1]
bhraṣṭasyārtasya duḥkhena kimāsvādaḥ karoti saḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 41.2]
śyenāya prāṇivātsalyāt svamāṃsānyapi dattavān | [SaundĀ, 11 42.1]
śibiḥ svargāt paribhraṣṭastādṛk kṛtvāpi duṣkaram | [SaundĀ, 11 42.2]
śakrasyārdhāsanaṃ gatvā pūrvapārthiva eva yaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 43.1]
sa devatvaṃ gataḥ kāle māndhātādhaḥ punaryayau | [SaundĀ, 11 43.2]
rājyaṃ kṛtvāpi devānāṃ papāta nahuṣo bhuvi | [SaundĀ, 11 44.1]
prāptaḥ kila bhujaṃgatvaṃ nādyāpi parimucyate | [SaundĀ, 11 44.2]
tathaivelivilo rājā rājavṛttena saṃskṛtaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 45.1]
svargaṃ gatvā punarbhraṣṭaḥ kūrmībhūtaḥ kilārṇave | [SaundĀ, 11 45.2]
bhūridyumno yayātiśca te cānye ca nṛparṣabhāḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 46.1]
karmabhirdyām abhikrīya tatkṣayāt punaratyajan | [SaundĀ, 11 46.2]
asurāḥ pūrvadevāstu surairapahṛtaśriyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 47.1]
śriyaṃ samanuśocantaḥ pātālaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 47.2]
kiṃca rājarṣibhistāvadasurairvā surādibhiḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 48.1]
mahendrāḥ śataśaḥ peturmāhātmyamapi na sthiram | [SaundĀ, 11 48.2]
saṃsadaṃ śobhayitvaindrīm upendraścendravikramaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 49.1]
kṣīṇakarmā papātorvīṃ madhyādapsarasāṃ rasan | [SaundĀ, 11 49.2]
hā caitraratha hā vāpi hā mandākini hā priye | [SaundĀ, 11 50.1]
ityārtā vilapanto 'pi gāṃ patanti divaukasaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 50.2]
tīvraṃ hyutpadyate duḥkhamiha tāvanmumūrṣatām | [SaundĀ, 11 51.1]
kiṃ punaḥ patatāṃ svargādevānte sukhasevinām | [SaundĀ, 11 51.2]
rajo gṛhṇanti vāsāṃsi mlāyanti paramāḥ srajaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 52.1]
gātrebhyo jāyate svedo ratirbhavati nāsane | [SaundĀ, 11 52.2]
etānyādau nimittāni cyutau svargād divaukasām | [SaundĀ, 11 53.1]
aniṣṭānīva martyānāmariṣṭāni mumūrṣatām | [SaundĀ, 11 53.2]
sukhamutpadyate yacca divi kāmānupāśnatām | [SaundĀ, 11 54.1]
yacca duḥkhaṃ nipatatāṃ duḥkhameva viśiṣyate | [SaundĀ, 11 54.2]
tasmād asvantam atrāṇam aviśvāsyam atarpakam | [SaundĀ, 11 55.1]
vijñāya kṣayiṇaṃ svargamapavarge matiṃ kuru | [SaundĀ, 11 55.2]
aśarīraṃ bhavāgraṃ hi gatvāpi munirudrakaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 56.1]
karmaṇo 'nte cyutastasmāt tiryagyoniṃ prapatsyate | [SaundĀ, 11 56.2]
maitryā saptavārṣikyā brahmalokamito gataḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 57.1]
sunetraḥ punarāvṛtto garbhavāsamupeyivān | [SaundĀ, 11 57.2]
yadā caiśvaryavanto 'pi kṣayiṇaḥ svargavāsinaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 58.1]
ko nāma svargavāsāya kṣeṣṇave spṛhayed budhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 58.2]
sūtreṇa baddho hi yathā vihaṃgo vyāvartate dūragato 'pi bhūyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 59.1]
ajñānasūtreṇa tathāvabaddho gato 'pi dūraṃ punareti lokaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 59.2]
kṛtvā kālavilakṣaṇaṃ pratibhuvā mukto yathā bandhanād bhuktvā veśmasukhānyatītya samayaṃ bhūyo viśed bandhanaṃ | [SaundĀ, 11 60.1]
tadvad dyāṃ pratibhūvadātmaniyamairdhyānādibhiḥ prāptavān kāle karmasu teṣu bhuktaviṣayeṣvākṛṣyate gāṃ punaḥ | [SaundĀ, 11 60.2]
antarjālagatāḥ pramattamanaso mīnāstaḍāge yathā jānanti vyasanaṃ na rodhajanitaṃ svasthāścarantyambhasi | [SaundĀ, 11 61.1]
antarlokagatāḥ kṛtārthamatayastadvaddivi dhyāyino manyante śivamacyutaṃ dhruvamiti svaṃ sthānamāvartakam | [SaundĀ, 11 61.2]
tajjanmavyādhimṛtyuvyasanaparigataṃ matvā jagadidaṃ saṃsāre bhrāmyamāṇaṃ divi nṛṣu narake tiryakpitṛṣu ca | [SaundĀ, 11 62.1]
yattrāṇaṃ nirbhayaṃ yacchivamamarajaraṃ niḥśokamamṛtaṃ taddhetorbrahmacaryaṃ cara jahi hi calaṃ svargaṃ prati rucim | [SaundĀ, 11 62.2]
{SaundĀ, 12}
apsarobhṛtako dharmaṃ carasītyatha coditaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 1.1]
ānandena tadā nandaḥ paraṃ vrīḍamupāgamat | [SaundĀ, 12 1.2]
tasya vrīḍena mahatā pramodo hṛdi nābhavat | [SaundĀ, 12 2.1]
aprāmodyena vimukhaṃ nāvatasthe vrate manaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 2.2]
kāmarāgapradhāno 'pi parihāsasamo 'pi san | [SaundĀ, 12 3.1]
paripākagate hetau na sa tanmamṛṣe vacaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 3.2]
aparīkṣakabhāvācca pūrvaṃ matvā divaṃ dhruvam | [SaundĀ, 12 4.1]
tasmāt kṣeṣṇuṃ pariśrutya bhṛśaṃ saṃvegameyivān | [SaundĀ, 12 4.2]
tasya svargānnivavṛte saṃkalpāśvo manorathaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 5.1]
mahāratha ivonmārgādapramattasya sāratheḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 5.2]
svargatarṣānnivṛttaśca sadyaḥ svastha ivābhavat | [SaundĀ, 12 6.1]
mṛṣṭādapathyād virato jijīviṣurivāturaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 6.2]
visasmāra priyāṃ bhāryāmapsarodarśanād yathā | [SaundĀ, 12 7.1]
tathānityatayodvignastatyājāpsaraso 'pi saḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 7.2]
mahatāmapi bhūtānāmāvṛttiriti cintayan | [SaundĀ, 12 8.1]
saṃvegācca sarāgo 'pi vītarāga ivābhavat | [SaundĀ, 12 8.2]
babhūva sa hi saṃvegaḥ śreyasastasya vṛddhaye | [SaundĀ, 12 9.1]
dhātur edhir ivākhyāte paṭhito 'kṣaracintakaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 9.2]
na tu kāmānmanastasya kenacijjagṛhe dhṛtiḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 10.1]
triṣu kāleṣu sarveṣu nipāto 'stiriva smṛtaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 10.2]
khelagāmī mahābāhur gajendra iva nirmadaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 11.1]
so 'bhyagacchad guruṃ kāle vivakṣurbhāvamātmanaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 11.2]
praṇamya ca gurau mūrdhnā bāṣpavyākulalocanaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 12.1]
kṛtvāñjalimuvācedaṃ hriyā kiṃcidavāṅmukhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 12.2]
apsaraḥprāptaye yanme bhagavan pratibhūrasi | [SaundĀ, 12 13.1]
nāpsarobhirmamārtho 'sti pratibhūtvaṃ tyajāmyaham | [SaundĀ, 12 13.2]
śrutvā hyāvartakaṃ svargaṃ saṃsārasya ca citratām | [SaundĀ, 12 14.1]
na martyeṣu na deveṣu pravṛttirmama rocate | [SaundĀ, 12 14.2]
yadi prāpya divaṃ yatnānniyamena damena ca | [SaundĀ, 12 15.1]
avitṛptāḥ patantyante svargāya tyāgine namaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 15.2]
ataśca nikhilaṃ lokaṃ viditvā sacarācaram | [SaundĀ, 12 16.1]
sarvaduḥkhakṣayakare tvaddharme parame rame | [SaundĀ, 12 16.2]
tasmād vyāsasamāsābhyāṃ tanme vyākhyātumarhasi | [SaundĀ, 12 17.1]
yacchrutvā śṛṇvatāṃ śreṣṭha paramaṃ prāpnuyāṃ padam | [SaundĀ, 12 17.2]
tatastasyāśayaṃ jñātvā vipakṣāṇīndriyāṇi ca | [SaundĀ, 12 18.1]
śreyaścaivāmukhībhūtaṃ nijagāda tathāgataḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 18.2]
aho pratyavamarśo 'yaṃ śreyasaste purojavaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 19.1]
araṇyāṃ mathyamānāyāmagnerdhūma ivotthitaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 19.2]
ciramunmārgavihṛto lolairindriyavājibhiḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 20.1]
avatīrṇo 'si panthānaṃ diṣṭyā dṛṣṭyāvimūḍhayā | [SaundĀ, 12 20.2]
adya te saphalaṃ janma lābho 'dya sumahāṃstava | [SaundĀ, 12 21.1]
yasya kāmarasajñasya naiṣkramyāyotsukaṃ manaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 21.2]
loke 'sminnālayārāme nivṛttau durlabhā ratiḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 22.1]
vyathante hyapunarbhāvāt prapātādiva bāliśāḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 22.2]
duḥkhaṃ na syāt sukhaṃ me syāditi prayatate janaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 23.1]
atyantaduḥkhoparamaṃ sukhaṃ tacca na budhyate | [SaundĀ, 12 23.2]
aribhūteṣvanityeṣu satataṃ duḥkhahetuṣu | [SaundĀ, 12 24.1]
kāmādiṣu jagat saktaṃ na vetti sukhamavyayam | [SaundĀ, 12 24.2]
sarvaduḥkhāpahaṃ tattu hastasthamamṛtaṃ tava | [SaundĀ, 12 25.1]
viṣaṃ pītvā yadagadaṃ samaye pātumicchasi | [SaundĀ, 12 25.2]
anarhasaṃsārabhayaṃ mānārhaṃ te cikīrṣitam | [SaundĀ, 12 26.1]
rāgāgnistādṛśo yasya dharmonmukha parāṅmukhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 26.2]
rāgoddāmena manasā sarvathā duṣkarā dhṛtiḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 27.1]
sadoṣaṃ salilaṃ dṛṣṭvā pathineva pipāsunā | [SaundĀ, 12 27.2]
īdṛśī nāma buddhiste viruddhā rajasābhavat | [SaundĀ, 12 28.1]
rajasā caṇḍavātena vivasvata iva prabhā | [SaundĀ, 12 28.2]
sā jighāṃsustamo hārdaṃ yā saṃprati vijṛmbhate | [SaundĀ, 12 29.1]
tamo naiśaṃ prabhā saurī vinirgīrṇeva meruṇā | [SaundĀ, 12 29.2]
yuktarūpamidaṃ caiva śuddhasattvasya cetasaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 30.1]
yatte syānnaiṣṭhike sūkṣme śreyasi śraddadhānatā | [SaundĀ, 12 30.2]
dharmacchandamimaṃ tasmādvivardhayitumarhasi | [SaundĀ, 12 31.1]
sarvadharmā hi dharmajña niyamācchandahetavaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 31.2]
satyāṃ gamanabuddhau hi gamanāya pravartate | [SaundĀ, 12 32.1]
śayyābuddhau ca śayanaṃ sthānabuddhau tathā sthitiḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 32.2]
antarbhūmigataṃ hyambhaḥ śraddadhāti naro yadā | [SaundĀ, 12 33.1]
arthitve sati yatnena tadā khanati gāmimām | [SaundĀ, 12 33.2]
nārthī yadyagninā vā syācchraddadhyāttaṃ na vāraṇau | [SaundĀ, 12 34.1]
mathnīyānnāraṇiṃ kaścit tadbhāve sati mathyate | [SaundĀ, 12 34.2]
sasyotpattiṃ yadi na vā śraddadhyāt kārṣakaḥ kṣitau | [SaundĀ, 12 35.1]
arthī sasyena vā na syād bījāni na vaped bhuvi | [SaundĀ, 12 35.2]
ataśca hasta ityuktā mayā śraddhā viśeṣataḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 36.1]
yasmād gṛhṇāti saddharmaṃ dāyaṃ hasta ivākṣataḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 36.2]
prādhānyādindriyamiti sthiratvād balamityataḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 37.1]
guṇadāridryaśamanād dhanamityabhivarṇitā | [SaundĀ, 12 37.2]
rakṣaṇārthena dharmasya tatheṣīketyudāhṛtā | [SaundĀ, 12 38.1]
loke 'smin durlabhatvācca ratnamityabhibhāṣitā | [SaundĀ, 12 38.2]
punaśca bījamityuktā nimittaṃ śreyaso yadā | [SaundĀ, 12 39.1]
pāvanārthena pāpasya nadītyabhihitā punaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 39.2]
yasmāddharmasya cotpattau śraddhā kāraṇamuttamam | [SaundĀ, 12 40.1]
mayoktā kāryatastasmāttatra tatra tathā tathā | [SaundĀ, 12 40.2]
śraddhāṅkuramimaṃ tasmāt saṃvardhayitumarhasi | [SaundĀ, 12 41.1]
tadvṛddhau vardhate dharmo mūlavṛddhau yathā drumaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 41.2]
vyākulaṃ darśanaṃ yasya durbalo yasya niścayaḥ | [SaundĀ, 12 42.1]
tasya pāriplavā śraddhā na hi kṛtyāya vartate | [SaundĀ, 12 42.2]
yāvattattvaṃ na bhavati hi dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ vā tāvacchraddhā na bhavati balasthā sthirā vā | [SaundĀ, 12 43.1]
dṛṣṭe tattve niyamaparibhūtendriyasya śraddhāvṛkṣo bhavati saphalaścāśrayaśca | [SaundĀ, 12 43.2]
{SaundĀ, 13}
atha saṃrādhito nandaḥ śraddhāṃ prati maharṣiṇā | [SaundĀ, 13 1.1]
pariṣikto 'mṛteneva yuyuje parayā mudā | [SaundĀ, 13 1.2]
kṛtārthamiva taṃ mene saṃbuddhaḥ śraddhayā tayā | [SaundĀ, 13 2.1]
mene prāptamiva śreyaḥ sa ca buddhena saṃskṛtaḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 2.2]
ślakṣṇena vacasā kāṃścit kāṃścit paruṣayā girā | [SaundĀ, 13 3.1]
kāṃścidābhyāmupāyābhyāṃ sa vininye vināyakaḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 3.2]
pāṃsubhyaḥ kāñcanaṃ jātaṃ viśuddhaṃ nirmalaṃ śuci | [SaundĀ, 13 4.1]
sthitaṃ pāṃsuṣvapi yathā pāṃsudoṣairna lipyate | [SaundĀ, 13 4.2]
padmaparṇaṃ yathā caiva jale jātaṃ jale sthitam | [SaundĀ, 13 5.1]
upariṣṭādadhastādvā na jalenopalipyate | [SaundĀ, 13 5.2]
tadvalloke munirjāto lokasyānugrahaṃ caran | [SaundĀ, 13 6.1]
kṛtitvānnirmalatvācca lokadharmairna lipyate | [SaundĀ, 13 6.2]
śleṣaṃ tyāgaṃ priyaṃ rūkṣaṃ kathāṃ ca dhyānameva ca | [SaundĀ, 13 7.1]
mantukāle cikitsārthaṃ cakre nātmānuvṛttaye | [SaundĀ, 13 7.2]
ataśca saṃdadhe kāyaṃ mahākaruṇayā tayā | [SaundĀ, 13 8.1]
mocayeyaṃ kathaṃ duḥkhāt sattvānītyanukampakaḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 8.2]
atha saṃharṣaṇānnandaṃ viditvā bhājanīkṛtam | [SaundĀ, 13 9.1]
abravīd bruvatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ kramajñaḥ śreyasāṃ kramam | [SaundĀ, 13 9.2]
ataḥ prabhṛti bhūyastvaṃ śraddhendriyapuraḥsaraḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 10.1]
amṛtasyāptaye saumya vṛttaṃ rakṣitumarhasi | [SaundĀ, 13 10.2]
prayogaḥ kāyavacasoḥ śuddho bhavati te yathā | [SaundĀ, 13 11.1]
uttāno vivṛto gupto 'navacchidrastathā kuru | [SaundĀ, 13 11.2]
uttāno bhāvakaraṇād vivṛtaścāpy agūhanāt | [SaundĀ, 13 12.1]
gupto rakṣaṇatātparyādacchidraścānavadyataḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 12.2]
śarīravacasoḥ śuddhau saptāṅge cāpi karmaṇi | [SaundĀ, 13 13.1]
ājīvasamudācāraṃ śaucāt saṃskartumarhasi | [SaundĀ, 13 13.2]
doṣāṇāṃ kuhanādīnāṃ pañcānām aniṣevaṇāt | [SaundĀ, 13 14.1]
tyāgācca jyotiṣādīnāṃ caturṇāṃ vṛttighātinām | [SaundĀ, 13 14.2]
prāṇidhānyadhanādīnāṃ varjyānām apratigrahāt | [SaundĀ, 13 15.1]
bhaikṣāṅgānāṃ nisṛṣṭānāṃ niyatānāṃ pratigrahāt | [SaundĀ, 13 15.2]
parituṣṭaḥ śucirmañjuścaukṣayā jīvasaṃpadā | [SaundĀ, 13 16.1]
kuryā duḥkhapratīkāraṃ yāvadeva vimuktaye | [SaundĀ, 13 16.2]
karmaṇo hi yathādṛṣṭāt kāyavākprabhavādapi | [SaundĀ, 13 17.1]
ājīvaḥ pṛthagevokto duḥśodhatvādayaṃ mayā | [SaundĀ, 13 17.2]
gṛhasthena hi duḥśodhā dṛṣṭirvividhadṛṣṭinā | [SaundĀ, 13 18.1]
ājīvo bhikṣuṇā caiva pareṣvāyattavṛttinā | [SaundĀ, 13 18.2]
etāvacchīlamityuktamācāro 'yaṃ samāsataḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 19.1]
asya nāśena naiva syāt pravrajyā na gṛhasthatā | [SaundĀ, 13 19.2]
tasmāccāritrasampanno brahmacaryamidaṃ cara | [SaundĀ, 13 20.1]
aṇumātreṣvavadyeṣu bhayadarśī dṛḍhavrataḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 20.2]
śīlamāsthāya vartante sarvā hi śreyasi kriyāḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 21.1]
sthānādyānīva kāryāṇi pratiṣṭhāya vasundharām | [SaundĀ, 13 21.2]
mokṣasyopaniṣat saumya vairāgyamiti gṛhyatām | [SaundĀ, 13 22.1]
vairāgyasyāpi saṃvedaḥ saṃvido jñānadarśanam | [SaundĀ, 13 22.2]
jñānasyopaniṣaccaiva samādhirupadhāryatām | [SaundĀ, 13 23.1]
samādherapyupaniṣat sukhaṃ śārīramānasam | [SaundĀ, 13 23.2]
praśrabdhiḥ kāyamanasaḥ sukhasyopaniṣat parā | [SaundĀ, 13 24.1]
praśrabdherapyupaniṣat prītirapyavagamyatām | [SaundĀ, 13 24.2]
tathā prīterupaniṣat prāmodyaṃ paramaṃ matam | [SaundĀ, 13 25.1]
prāmodyasyāpyahṛllekhaḥ kukṛteṣvakṛteṣu vā | [SaundĀ, 13 25.2]
ahṛllekhasya manasaḥ śīlaṃ tūpaniṣacchuci | [SaundĀ, 13 26.1]
ataḥ śīlaṃ nayatyagryamiti śīlaṃ viśodhaya | [SaundĀ, 13 26.2]
śīlanācchīlamityuktaṃ śīlanaṃ sevanādapi | [SaundĀ, 13 27.1]
sevanaṃ tannideśācca nideśaśca tadāśrayāt | [SaundĀ, 13 27.2]
śīlaṃ hi śaraṇaṃ saumya kāntāra iva daiśikaḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 28.1]
mitraṃ bandhuśca rakṣā ca dhanaṃ ca balameva ca | [SaundĀ, 13 28.2]
yataḥ śīlamataḥ saumya śīlaṃ saṃskartumarhasi | [SaundĀ, 13 29.1]
etatsthānamathānye ca mokṣārambheṣu yoginām | [SaundĀ, 13 29.2]
tataḥ smṛtimadhiṣṭhāya capalāni svabhāvataḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 30.1]
indriyāṇīndriyārthebhyo nivārayitumarhasi | [SaundĀ, 13 30.2]
bhetavyaṃ na tathā śatrornāgnernāherna cāśaneḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 31.1]
indriyebhyo yathā svebhyastairajasraṃ hi hanyate | [SaundĀ, 13 31.2]
dviṣadbhiḥ śatrubhiḥ kaścit kadācit pīḍyate na vā | [SaundĀ, 13 32.1]
indriyairbādhyate sarvaḥ sarvatra ca sadaiva ca | [SaundĀ, 13 32.2]
na ca prayāti narakaṃ śatruprabhṛtibhirhataḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 33.1]
kṛṣyate tatra nighnastu capalairindriyairhataḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 33.2]
hanyamānasya tairduḥkhaṃ hārdaṃ bhavati vā na vā | [SaundĀ, 13 34.1]
indriyairbādhyamānasya hārdaṃ śārīrameva ca | [SaundĀ, 13 34.2]
saṃkalpaviṣadigdhā hi pañcendriyamayāḥ śarāḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 35.1]
cintāpuṅkhā ratiphalā viṣayākāśagocarāḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 35.2]
manuṣyahariṇān ghnanti kāmavyādheritā hṛdi | [SaundĀ, 13 36.1]
vihanyante yadi na te tataḥ patanti taiḥ kṣatāḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 36.2]
niyamājirasaṃsthena dhairyakārmukadhāriṇā | [SaundĀ, 13 37.1]
nipatanto nivāryāste mahatā smṛtivarmaṇā | [SaundĀ, 13 37.2]
indriyāṇāmupaśamādarīṇāṃ nigrahādiva | [SaundĀ, 13 38.1]
sukhaṃ svapiti vāste vā yatra tatra gatoddhavaḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 38.2]
teṣāṃ hi satataṃ loke viṣayānabhikāṅkṣatām | [SaundĀ, 13 39.1]
saṃvinnaivāsti kārpaṇyācchunāmāśāvatāmiva | [SaundĀ, 13 39.2]
viṣayairindriyagrāmo na tṛptimadhigacchati | [SaundĀ, 13 40.1]
ajasraṃ pūryamāṇo 'pi samudraḥ salilairiva | [SaundĀ, 13 40.2]
avaśyaṃ gocare sve sve vartitavyamihendriyaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 41.1]
nimittaṃ tatra na grāhyamanuvyañjanameva ca | [SaundĀ, 13 41.2]
ālokya cakṣuṣā rūpaṃ dhātumātre vyavasthitaḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 42.1]
strī veti puruṣo veti na kalpayitumarhasi | [SaundĀ, 13 42.2]
sacet strīpuruṣagrāhaḥ kvacid vidyeta kaścana | [SaundĀ, 13 43.1]
śubhataḥ keśadantādīn nānuprasthātumarhasi | [SaundĀ, 13 43.2]
nāpaneyaṃ tataḥ kiṃcit prakṣepyaṃ nāpi kiṃcana | [SaundĀ, 13 44.1]
draṣṭavyaṃ bhūtato bhūtaṃ yādṛśaṃ ca yathā ca yat | [SaundĀ, 13 44.2]
evaṃ te paśyatastattvaṃ śaśvadindriyagocaram | [SaundĀ, 13 45.1]
bhaviṣyati padasthānaṃ nābhidhyādaurmanasyayoḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 45.2]
abhidhyā priyarūpeṇa hanti kāmātmakaṃ jagat | [SaundĀ, 13 46.1]
arirmitramukheneva priyavākkaluṣāśayaḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 46.2]
daurmanasyābhidhānastu pratigho viṣayāśritaḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 47.1]
mohādyenānuvṛttena paratreha ca hanyate | [SaundĀ, 13 47.2]
anurodhavirodhābhyāṃ śītoṣṇābhyām ivārditaḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 48.1]
śarma nāpnoti na śreyaścalendriyamato jagat | [SaundĀ, 13 48.2]
nendriyaṃ viṣaye tāvat pravṛttamapi sajjate | [SaundĀ, 13 49.1]
yāvanna manasastatra parikalpaḥ pravartate | [SaundĀ, 13 49.2]
indhane sati vāyau ca yathā jvalati pāvakaḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 50.1]
viṣayāt parikalpācca kleśāgnirjāyate tathā | [SaundĀ, 13 50.2]
abhūtaparikalpena viṣayasya hi vadhyate | [SaundĀ, 13 51.1]
tameva viṣayaṃ paśyan bhūtataḥ parimucyate | [SaundĀ, 13 51.2]
dṛṣṭvaikaṃ rūpamanyo hi rajyate 'nyaḥ praduṣyati | [SaundĀ, 13 52.1]
kaścid bhavati madhyasthastatraivānyo ghṛṇāyate | [SaundĀ, 13 52.2]
ato na viṣayo heturbandhāya na vimuktaye | [SaundĀ, 13 53.1]
parikalpaviśeṣeṇa saṃgo bhavati vā na vā | [SaundĀ, 13 53.2]
kāryaḥ paramayatnena tasmādindriyasaṃvaraḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 54.1]
indriyāṇi hyaguptāni duḥkhāya ca bhavāya ca | [SaundĀ, 13 54.2]
kāmabhogabhogavadbhirātmadṛṣṭidṛṣṭibhiḥ pramādanaikamūrdhabhiḥ praharṣalolajihvakaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 13 55.1]
indriyoragair manobilāśrayaiḥ spṛhāviṣaiḥ śamāgadādṛte na dṛṣṭamasti yaccikitset | [SaundĀ, 13 55.2]
tasmādeṣāmakuśalakarāṇāmarīṇāṃ cakṣurghrāṇaśravaṇarasanasparśanānām | [SaundĀ, 13 56.1]
sarvāvasthaṃ bhava viniyamād apramatto māsminnarthe kṣaṇamapi kṛthāstvaṃ pramādam | [SaundĀ, 13 56.2]
{SaundĀ, 14}
atha smṛtikavāṭena pidhāyendriyasaṃvaram | [SaundĀ, 14 1.1]
bhojane bhava mātrājño dhyānāyānāmayāya ca | [SaundĀ, 14 1.2]
prāṇāpānau nigṛhṇāti glāninidre prayacchati | [SaundĀ, 14 2.1]
kṛto hyatyarthamāhāro vihanti ca parākramam | [SaundĀ, 14 2.2]
yathā cātyarthamāhāraḥ kṛto 'narthāya kalpate | [SaundĀ, 14 3.1]
upayuktastathātyalpo na sāmarthyāya kalpate | [SaundĀ, 14 3.2]
ācayaṃ dyutimutsāhaṃ prayogaṃ balameva ca | [SaundĀ, 14 4.1]
bhojanaṃ kṛtamatyalpaṃ śarīrasyāpakarṣati | [SaundĀ, 14 4.2]
yathā bhāreṇa namate laghunonnamate tulā | [SaundĀ, 14 5.1]
samā tiṣṭhati yuktena bhojyeneyaṃ tathā tanuḥ | [SaundĀ, 14 5.2]
tasmād abhyavahartavyaṃ svaśaktimanupaśyatā | [SaundĀ, 14 6.1]
nātimātraṃ na cātyalpaṃ meyaṃ mānavaśādapi | [SaundĀ, 14 6.2]
atyākrānto hi kāyāgnirguruṇānnena śāmyati | [SaundĀ, 14 7.1]
avacchanna ivālpo 'gniḥ sahasā mahatendhasā | [SaundĀ, 14 7.2]
atyantamapi saṃhāro nāhārasya praśasyate | [SaundĀ, 14 8.1]
anāhāro hi nirvāti nirindhana ivānalaḥ | [SaundĀ, 14 8.2]
yasmānnāsti vināhārāt sarvaprāṇabhṛtāṃ sthitiḥ | [SaundĀ, 14 9.1]
tasmād duṣyati nāhāro vikalpo 'tra tu vāryate | [SaundĀ, 14 9.2]
na hyekaviṣaye 'nyatra sajyante prāṇinastathā | [SaundĀ, 14 10.1]
avijñāte yathāhāre boddhavyaṃ tatra kāraṇam | [SaundĀ, 14 10.2]
cikitsārthaṃ yathā dhatte vraṇasyālepanaṃ vraṇī | [SaundĀ, 14 11.1]
kṣudvighātārthamāhārastadvat sevyo mumukṣuṇā | [SaundĀ, 14 11.2]
bhārasyodvahanārthaṃ ca rathākṣo 'bhyajyate yathā | [SaundĀ, 14 12.1]
bhojanaṃ prāṇayātrārthaṃ tadvad vidvānniṣevate | [SaundĀ, 14 12.2]
samatikramaṇārthaṃ ca kāntārasya yathādhvagau | [SaundĀ, 14 13.1]
putramāṃsāni khādetāṃ dampatī bhṛśaduḥkhitau | [SaundĀ, 14 13.2]
evamabhyavahartavyaṃ bhojanaṃ pratisaṃkhyayā | [SaundĀ, 14 14.1]
na bhūṣārthaṃ na vapuṣe na madāya na dṛptaye | [SaundĀ, 14 14.2]
dhāraṇārthaṃ śarīrasya bhojanaṃ hi vidhīyate | [SaundĀ, 14 15.1]
upastambhaḥ pipatiṣor durbalasyeva veśmanaḥ | [SaundĀ, 14 15.2]
plavaṃ yatnād yathā kaścid badhnīyād dhārayedapi | [SaundĀ, 14 16.1]
na tatsnehena yāvattu mahaughasyottitīrṣayā | [SaundĀ, 14 16.2]
tathopakaraṇaiḥ kāyaṃ dhārayanti parīkṣakāḥ | [SaundĀ, 14 17.1]
na tatsnehena yāvattu duḥkhaughasya titīrṣayā | [SaundĀ, 14 17.2]
śocatā pīḍyamānena dīyate śatrave yathā | [SaundĀ, 14 18.1]
na bhaktyā nāpi tarṣeṇa kevalaṃ prāṇaguptaye | [SaundĀ, 14 18.2]
yogācārastathāhāraṃ śarīrāya prayacchati | [SaundĀ, 14 19.1]
kevalaṃ kṣudvighātārthaṃ na rāgeṇa na bhaktaye | [SaundĀ, 14 19.2]
manodhāraṇayā caiva pariṇāmyātmavānahaḥ | [SaundĀ, 14 20.1]
vidhūya nidrāṃ yogena niśāmapyatināmayet | [SaundĀ, 14 20.2]
hṛdi yatsaṃjñinaścaiva nidrā prādurbhavettava | [SaundĀ, 14 21.1]

{SaundĀ, 16}
evaṃ manodhāraṇayā krameṇa vyapohya kiṃcit samupohya kiṃcit | [SaundĀ, 16 1.1]
dhyānāni catvāryadhigamya yogī prāpnotyabhijñā niyamena pañca | [SaundĀ, 16 1.2]
ṛddhipravekaṃ ca bahuprakāraṃ parasya cetaścaritāvabodham | [SaundĀ, 16 2.1]
atītajanmasmaraṇaṃ ca dīrghaṃ divye viśuddhe śruticakṣuṣī ca | [SaundĀ, 16 2.2]
ataḥ paraṃ tattvaparīkṣaṇena mano dadhātyāsravasaṃkṣayāya | [SaundĀ, 16 3.1]
tato hi duḥkhaprabhṛtīni samyak catvāri satyāni padānyavaiti | [SaundĀ, 16 3.2]
bādhātmakaṃ duḥkhamidaṃ prasaktaṃ duḥkhasya hetuḥ prabhavātmako 'yam | [SaundĀ, 16 4.1]

ityāryasatyānyavabudhya buddhyā catvāri samyak pratividhya caiva | [SaundĀ, 16 5.1]
sarvāsravān bhāvanayābhibhūya na jāyate śāntimavāpya bhūyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 5.2]

loke tathā tiryaguparyadho vā duḥkhāya sarvaṃ na sukhāya janma | [SaundĀ, 16 9.2]

pravātsu ghoreṣvapi māruteṣu na hyaprasūtāstaravaścalanti | [SaundĀ, 16 10.2]
ākāśayoniḥ pavano yathā hi yathā śamīgarbhaśayo hutāśaḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 11.1]
āpo yathāntarvasudhāśayāśca duḥkhaṃ tathā cittaśarīrayoniḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 11.2]
apāṃ dravatvaṃ kaṭhinatvamurvyā vāyoścalatvaṃ dhruvamauṣṇyamagneḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 12.1]
yathā svabhāvo hi tathā svabhāvo duḥkhaṃ śarīrasya ca cetasaśca | [SaundĀ, 16 12.2]

yathā ca tadduḥkhamidaṃ ca duḥkhaṃ duḥkhaṃ tathānāgatamapyavehi | [SaundĀ, 16 14.2]

diśaṃ na kāṃcid vidiśaṃ na kāṃcit snehakṣayāt kevalameti śāntim | [SaundĀ, 16 28.2]

diśaṃ na kāṃcid vidiśaṃ na kāṃcit kleśakṣayāt kevalameti śāntim | [SaundĀ, 16 29.2]

vākkarma samyak sahakāyakarma yathāvadājīvanayaśca śuddhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 31.1]
idaṃ trayaṃ vṛttavidhau pravṛttaṃ śīlāśrayaṃ karmaparigrahāya | [SaundĀ, 16 31.2]

kimatra citraṃ yadi vītamoho vanaṃ gataḥ svasthamanā na muhyet | [SaundĀ, 16 84.1]
