tadāryasatyādhigamāya pūrvaṃ viśodhayānena nayena mārgam | [SaundĀ, 16 85.1]
yātrāgataḥ śatruvinigrahārthaṃ rājeva lakṣmīmajitāṃ jigīṣan | [SaundĀ, 16 85.2]
etānyaraṇyānyabhitaḥ śivāni yogānukūlānyajaneritāni | [SaundĀ, 16 86.1]
kāyasya kṛtvā pravivekamātraṃ kleśaprahāṇāya bhajasva mārgam | [SaundĀ, 16 86.2]
kauṇḍinyanandakṛmilāniruddhāstiṣyopasenau vimalo 'tha rādhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 87.1]
bāṣpottarau dhautakimoharājau kātyāyanadravyapilindavatsāḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 87.2]
bhaddālibhadrāyaṇasarpadāsasubhūtigodattasujātavatsāḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 88.1]
saṃgrāmajid bhadrajid aśvajicca śroṇaśca śoṇaśca ca koṭikarṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 88.2]
kṣemājito nandakanandamātā vupālivāgīśayaśoyaśodāḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 89.1]
mahāhvayo valkalirāṣṭrapālau sudarśanasvāgatamedhikāśca | [SaundĀ, 16 89.2]
sa kapphinaḥ kāśyapa auruvilvo mahāmahākāśyapatiṣyanandāḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 90.1]
pūrṇaśca pūrṇaśca sa pūrṇakaśca śonāparāntaśca sa pūrṇa eva | [SaundĀ, 16 90.2]
śāradvatīputrasubāhucundāḥ kondeyakāpyabhṛgukuṇṭhadhānāḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 91.1]
saśaivalau revatakauṣṭhilau ca maudgalyagotraśca gavāṃpatiśca | [SaundĀ, 16 91.2]
yaṃ vikramaṃ yogavidhāvakurvaṃstameva śīghraṃ vidhivat kuruṣva | [SaundĀ, 16 92.1]
tataḥ padaṃ prāpsyasi tairavāptaṃ sukhāvṛtaistvaṃ niyataṃ yaśaśca | [SaundĀ, 16 92.2]
dravyaṃ yathā syāt kaṭukaṃ rasena taccopayuktaṃ madhuraṃ vipāke | [SaundĀ, 16 93.1]
tathaiva vīryaṃ kaṭukaṃ śrameṇa tasyārthasiddhyai madhuro vipākaḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 93.2]
vīryaṃ paraṃ kāryakṛtau hi mūlaṃ vīryādṛte kācana nāsti siddhiḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 94.1]
udeti vīryādiha sarvasaṃpannirvīryatā cet sakalaśca pāpmā | [SaundĀ, 16 94.2]
alabdhasyālābho niyatamupalabdhasya vigamastathaivātmāvajñā kṛpaṇamadhikebhyaḥ paribhavaḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 95.1]
tamo nistejastvaṃ śrutiniyamatuṣṭivyuparamo nṛṇāṃ nirvīryāṇāṃ bhavati vinipātaśca bhavati | [SaundĀ, 16 95.2]
nayaṃ śrutvā śakto yadayamabhivṛddhiṃ na labhate paraṃ dharmaṃ jñātvā yadupari nivāsaṃ na labhate | [SaundĀ, 16 96.1]
gṛhaṃ tyaktvā muktau yadayamupaśāntiṃ na labhate | [SaundĀ, 16 96.2]
nimittaṃ kausīdyaṃ bhavati puruṣasyātra na ripuḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 96.3]
anikṣiptotsāho yadi khanati gāṃ vāri labhate | [SaundĀ, 16 97.1]
prasaktaṃ vyāmathnan jvalanamaraṇibhyāṃ janayati | [SaundĀ, 16 97.2]
prayuktā yoge tu dhruvamupalabhante śramaphalaṃ drutaṃ nityaṃ yāntyo girimapi hi bhindanti saritaḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 97.3]
kṛṣṭvā gāṃ paripālya ca śramaśatairaśnoti sasyaśriyaṃ yatnena pravigāhya sāgarajalaṃ ratnaśriyā krīḍati | [SaundĀ, 16 98.1]
śatrūṇāmavadhūya vīryamiṣubhirbhuṅkte narendraśriyaṃ tadvīryaṃ kuru śāntaye viniyataṃ vīrye hi sarvarddhayaḥ | [SaundĀ, 16 98.2]
{SaundĀ, 17}
athaivamādeśitatattvamārgo nandastadā prāptavimokṣamārgaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 1.1]
sarveṇa bhāvena gurau praṇamya kleśaprahāṇāya vanaṃ jagāma | [SaundĀ, 17 1.2]
tatrāvakāśaṃ mṛdunīlaśaṣpaṃ dadarśa śāntaṃ taruṣaṇḍavantam | [SaundĀ, 17 2.1]
niḥśabdayā nimnagayopagūḍhaṃ vaiḍūryanīlodakayā vahantyā | [SaundĀ, 17 2.2]
sa pādayostatra vidhāya śaucaṃ śucau śive śrīmati vṛkṣamūle | [SaundĀ, 17 3.1]
mokṣāya baddhvā vyavasāyakakṣāṃ paryaṅkamaṅkāvahitaṃ babandha | [SaundĀ, 17 3.2]
ṛjuṃ samagraṃ praṇidhāya kāyaṃ kāye smṛtiṃ cābhimukhīṃ vidhāya | [SaundĀ, 17 4.1]
sarvendriyāṇyātmani saṃnidhāya sa tatra yogaṃ prayataḥ prapede | [SaundĀ, 17 4.2]
tataḥ sa tattvaṃ nikhilaṃ cikīrṣurmokṣānukūlāṃśca vidhīṃścikīrṣan | [SaundĀ, 17 5.1]
jñānena śīlena śamena caiva cacāra cetaḥ parikarmabhūmau | [SaundĀ, 17 5.2]
saṃdhāya dhairyaṃ praṇidhāya vīryaṃ vyapohya saktiṃ parigṛhya śaktim | [SaundĀ, 17 6.1]
praśāntacetā niyamasthacetāḥ svasthastato 'bhūd viṣayeṣvanāsthaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 6.2]
ātaptabuddheḥ prahitātmano 'pi svabhyastabhāvādatha kāmasaṃjñā | [SaundĀ, 17 7.1]
paryākulaṃ tasya manaścakāra prāvṛṭsu vidyujjalamāgateva | [SaundĀ, 17 7.2]
sa paryavasthānamavetya sadyaścikṣepa tāṃ dharmavighātakartrīm | [SaundĀ, 17 8.1]
priyāmapi krodhaparītacetā nārīmivodvṛttaguṇāṃ manasvī | [SaundĀ, 17 8.2]
ārabdhavīryasya manaḥśamāya bhūyastu tasyākuśalo vitarkaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 9.1]
vyādhipraṇāśāya niviṣṭabuddher upadravo ghora ivājagāma | [SaundĀ, 17 9.2]
sa tadvighātāya nimittamanyad yogānukūlaṃ kuśalaṃ prapede | [SaundĀ, 17 10.1]
ārtāyanaṃ kṣīṇabalo balasthaṃ nirasyamāno balināriṇeva | [SaundĀ, 17 10.2]
puraṃ vidhāyānuvidhāya daṇḍaṃ mitrāṇi saṃgṛhya ripūn vigṛhya | [SaundĀ, 17 11.1]
rājā yathāpnoti hi gāmapūrvāṃ nītirmumukṣorapi saiva yoge | [SaundĀ, 17 11.2]
vimokṣakāmasya hi yogino 'pi manaḥ puraṃ jñānavidhiśca daṇḍaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 12.1]
guṇāśca mitrāṇyarayaśca doṣā bhūmirvimuktiryatate yadartham | [SaundĀ, 17 12.2]
sa duḥkhajālānmahato mumukṣurvimokṣamārgādhigame vivikṣuḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 13.1]
panthānamāryaṃ paramaṃ didṛkṣuḥ śamaṃ yayau kiṃcidupāttacakṣuḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 13.2]
yaḥ syānniketastamaso 'niketaḥ śrutvāpi tattvaṃ sa bhavet pramattaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 14.1]
yasmāttu mokṣāya sa pātrabhūtastasmānmanaḥ svātmani saṃjahāra | [SaundĀ, 17 14.2]
sambhārataḥ pratyayataḥ svabhāvādāsvādato doṣaviśeṣataśca | [SaundĀ, 17 15.1]
athātmavānniḥsaraṇātmataśca dharmeṣu cakre vidhivat parīkṣām | [SaundĀ, 17 15.2]
sa rūpiṇaṃ kṛtsnamarūpiṇaṃ ca sāraṃ didṛkṣurvicikāya kāyam | [SaundĀ, 17 16.1]
athāśuciṃ duḥkhamanityamasvaṃ nirātmakaṃ caiva cikāya kāyam | [SaundĀ, 17 16.2]
anityatastatra hi śūnyataśca nirātmato duḥkhata eva cāpi | [SaundĀ, 17 17.1]
mārgapravekeṇa sa laukikena kleśadrumaṃ saṃcalayāṃcakāra | [SaundĀ, 17 17.2]
yasmād abhūtvā bhavatīha sarvaṃ bhūtvā ca bhūyo na bhavatyavaśyam | [SaundĀ, 17 18.1]
sahetukaṃ ca kṣayi hetumacca tasmādanityaṃ jagadityavindat | [SaundĀ, 17 18.2]
yataḥ prasūtasya ca karmayogaḥ prasajyate bandhavighātahetuḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 19.1]
duḥkhapratīkāravidhau sukhākhye tato bhavaṃ duḥkhamiti vyapaśyat | [SaundĀ, 17 19.2]
yataśca saṃskāragataṃ viviktaṃ na kārakaḥ kaścana vedako vā | [SaundĀ, 17 20.1]
sāmagryataḥ sambhavati pravṛttiḥ śūnyaṃ tato lokamimaṃ dadarśa | [SaundĀ, 17 20.2]
yasmānnirīhaṃ jagadasvatantraṃ naiśvaryamekaḥ kurute kriyāsu | [SaundĀ, 17 21.1]
tattatpratītya prabhavanti bhāvā nirātmakaṃ tena viveda lokam | [SaundĀ, 17 21.2]
tataḥ sa vātaṃ vyajanādivoṣṇe kāṣṭhāśritaṃ nirmathanādivāgnim | [SaundĀ, 17 22.1]
antaḥkṣitisthaṃ khananādivāmbho lokottaraṃ vartma durāpamāpa | [SaundĀ, 17 22.2]
sajjñānacāpaḥ smṛtivarma baddhvā viśuddhaśīlavratavāhanasthaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 23.1]
kleśāribhiścittaraṇājirasthaiḥ sārdhaṃ yuyutsurvijayāya tasthau | [SaundĀ, 17 23.2]
tataḥ sa bodhyaṅgaśitāttaśastraḥ samyakpradhānottamavāhanasthaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 24.1]
mārgāṅgamātaṅgavatā balena śanaiḥ śanaiḥ kleśacamūṃ jagāhe | [SaundĀ, 17 24.2]
sa smṛtyupasthānamayaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ śatrūn viparyāsamayān kṣaṇena | [SaundĀ, 17 25.1]
duḥkhasya hetūṃścaturaścaturbhiḥ svaiḥ svaiḥ pracārāyatanairdadāra | [SaundĀ, 17 25.2]
āryairbalaiḥ pañcabhireva pañca cetaḥkhilānyapratimairbabhañja | [SaundĀ, 17 26.1]
mithyāṅganāgāṃśca tathāṅganāgairvinirdudhāvāṣṭabhireva so 'ṣṭau | [SaundĀ, 17 26.2]
athātmadṛṣṭiṃ sakalāṃ vidhūya caturṣu satyeṣvakathaṃkathaḥ san | [SaundĀ, 17 27.1]
viśuddhaśīlavratadṛṣṭadharmā dharmasya pūrvāṃ phalabhūmimāpa | [SaundĀ, 17 27.2]
sa darśanādāryacatuṣṭayasya kleśaikadeśasya ca viprayogāt | [SaundĀ, 17 28.1]
pratyātmikāccāpi viśeṣalābhāt pratyakṣato jñānisukhasya caiva | [SaundĀ, 17 28.2]
dārḍhyāt prasādasya dhṛteḥ sthiratvāt satyeṣvasaṃmūḍhatayā caturṣu | [SaundĀ, 17 29.1]
śīlasya cācchidratayottamasya niḥsaṃśayo dharmavidhau babhūva | [SaundĀ, 17 29.2]
kudṛṣṭijālena sa viprayukto lokaṃ tathābhūtamavekṣamāṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 30.1]
jñānāśrayāṃ prītimupājagāma bhūyaḥ prasādaṃ ca gurāviyāya | [SaundĀ, 17 30.2]
yo hi pravṛttiṃ niyatāmavaiti naivānyahetoriha nāpyahetoḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 31.1]
pratītya tattatsamavaiti tattatsa naiṣṭhikaṃ paśyati dharmamāryam | [SaundĀ, 17 31.2]
śāntaṃ śivaṃ nirjarasaṃ virāgaṃ niḥśreyasaṃ paśyati yaśca dharmam | [SaundĀ, 17 32.1]
tasyopadeṣṭāramathāryavaryaṃ sa prekṣate buddhamavāptacakṣuḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 32.2]
yathopadeśena śivena mukto rogādarogo bhiṣajaṃ kṛtajñaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 33.1]
anusmaran paśyati cittadṛṣṭyā maitryā ca śāstrajñatayā ca tuṣṭaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 33.2]
āryeṇa mārgeṇa tathaiva muktastathāgataṃ tattvavid āryatattvaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 34.1]
anusmaran paśyati kāyasākṣī maitryā ca sarvajñatayā ca tuṣṭaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 34.2]
sa nāśakairdṛṣṭigatairvimuktaḥ paryantamālokya punarbhavasya | [SaundĀ, 17 35.1]
bhaktvā ghṛṇāṃ kleśavijṛmbhiteṣu mṛtyorna tatrāsa na durgatibhyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 35.2]
tvaksnāyumedorudhirāsthimāṃsakeśādināmedhyagaṇena pūrṇam | [SaundĀ, 17 36.1]
tataḥ sa kāyaṃ samavekṣamāṇaḥ sāraṃ vicintyāṇvapi nopalebhe | [SaundĀ, 17 36.2]
sa kāmarāgapratighau sthirātmā tenaiva yogena tanū cakāra | [SaundĀ, 17 37.1]
kṛtvā mahoraskatanustanū tau prāpa dvitīyaṃ phalamāryadharme | [SaundĀ, 17 37.2]
sa lobhacāpaṃ parikalpabāṇaṃ rāgaṃ mahāvairiṇamalpaśeṣam | [SaundĀ, 17 38.1]
kāyasvabhāvādhigatair bibheda yogāyudhāstrair aśubhāpṛṣatkaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 38.2]
dveṣāyudhaṃ krodhavikīrṇabāṇaṃ vyāpādamantaḥprasavaṃ sapatnam | [SaundĀ, 17 39.1]
maitrīpṛṣatkairdhṛtitūṇasaṃsthaiḥ kṣamādhanurjyāvisṛtairjaghāna | [SaundĀ, 17 39.2]
mūlānyatha trīṇyaśubhasya vīrastribhirvimokṣāyatanaiścakarta | [SaundĀ, 17 40.1]
camūmukhasthān dhṛtakārmukāṃstrīnarīnivāristribhirāyasāgraiḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 40.2]
sa kāmadhātoḥ samatikramāya pārṣṇigrahāṃstānabhibhūya śatrūn | [SaundĀ, 17 41.1]
yogādanāgāmiphalaṃ prapadya dvārīva nirvāṇapurasya tasthau | [SaundĀ, 17 41.2]
kāmairviviktaṃ malinaiśca dharmairvitarkavaccāpi vicāravacca | [SaundĀ, 17 42.1]
vivekajaṃ prītisukhopapannaṃ dhyānaṃ tataḥ sa prathamaṃ prapede | [SaundĀ, 17 42.2]
kāmāgnidāhena sa vipramukto hlādaṃ paraṃ dhyānasukhādavāpa | [SaundĀ, 17 43.1]
sukhaṃ vigāhyāpsviva dharmakhinnaḥ prāpyeva cārthaṃ vipulaṃ daridraḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 43.2]
tatrāpi taddharmagatān vitarkān guṇāguṇe ca prasṛtān vicārān | [SaundĀ, 17 44.1]
buddhvā manaḥkṣobhakarānaśāntāṃstadviprayogāya matiṃ cakāra | [SaundĀ, 17 44.2]
kṣobhaṃ prakurvanti yathormayo hi dhīraprasannāmbuvahasya sindhoḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 45.1]
ekāgrabhūtasya tathormibhūtāścittāmbhasaḥ kṣobhakarā vitarkāḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 45.2]
khinnasya suptasya ca nirvṛtasya bādhaṃ yathā saṃjanayanti śabdāḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 46.1]
adhyātmam aikāgryamupāgatasya bhavanti bādhāya tathā vitarkāḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 46.2]
athāvitarkaṃ kramaśo 'vicāram ekāgrabhāvānmanasaḥ prasannam | [SaundĀ, 17 47.1]
samādhijaṃ prītisukhaṃ dvitīyaṃ dhyānaṃ tadādhyātmaśivaṃ sa dadhyau | [SaundĀ, 17 47.2]
taddhyānamāgamya ca cittamaunaṃ lebhe parāṃ prītim alabdhapūrvām | [SaundĀ, 17 48.1]
prītau tu tatrāpi sa doṣadarśī yathā vitarkeṣvabhavattathaiva | [SaundĀ, 17 48.2]
prītiḥ parā vastuni yatra yasya viparyayāttasya hi tatra duḥkham | [SaundĀ, 17 49.1]
prītāvataḥ prekṣya sa tatra doṣān prītikṣaye yogamupāruroha | [SaundĀ, 17 49.2]
prītervirāgāt sukhamāryajuṣṭaṃ kāyena vindannatha samprajānan | [SaundĀ, 17 50.1]
upekṣakaḥ sa smṛtimān vyahārṣīddhyānaṃ tṛtīyaṃ pratilabhya dhīraḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 50.2]
yasmāt paraṃ tatra sukhaṃ sukhebhyastataḥ paraṃ nāsti sukhapravṛttiḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 51.1]
tasmād babhāṣe śubhakṛtsnabhūmiḥ parāparajñaḥ parameti maitryā | [SaundĀ, 17 51.2]
dhyāne 'pi tatrātha dadarśa doṣaṃ mene paraṃ śāntam aniñjam eva | [SaundĀ, 17 52.1]
ābhogato 'pīñjayati sma tasya cittaṃ pravṛttaṃ sukhamityasram | [SaundĀ, 17 52.2]
yatreñjitaṃ spanditamasti tatra yatrāsti ca spanditamasti duḥkham | [SaundĀ, 17 53.1]
yasmādatastatsukham iñjakatvāt praśāntikāmā yatayastyajanti | [SaundĀ, 17 53.2]
atha prahāṇāt sukhaduḥkhayośca manovikārasya ca pūrvameva | [SaundĀ, 17 54.1]
dadhyāvupekṣāsmṛtimad viśuddhaṃ dhyānaṃ tathāduḥkhasukhaṃ caturtham | [SaundĀ, 17 54.2]
yasmāttu tasminna sukhaṃ na duḥkhaṃ jñānaṃ ca tatrāsti tadarthacāri | [SaundĀ, 17 55.1]
tasmād upekṣāsmṛtipāriśuddhir nirucyate dhyānavidhau caturthe | [SaundĀ, 17 55.2]
dhyānaṃ sa niśritya tataścaturthamarhattvalābhāya matiṃ cakāra | [SaundĀ, 17 56.1]
saṃdhāya mitraṃ balavantamāryaṃ rājeva deśānajitān jigīṣuḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 56.2]
cicheda kārtsnyena tataḥ sa pañca prajñāsinā bhāvanayeritena | [SaundĀ, 17 57.1]
ūrdhvaṃgamānyuttamabandhanāni saṃyojanānyuttamabandhanāni | [SaundĀ, 17 57.2]
bodhyaṅganāgairapi saptabhiḥ sa saptaiva cittānuśayān mamarda | [SaundĀ, 17 58.1]
dvipānivopasthitavipraṇāśān kālo grahaiḥ saptabhireva sapta | [SaundĀ, 17 58.2]
agnidrumājyāmbuṣu yā hi vṛttiḥ kabandhavāyvagnidivākarāṇām | [SaundĀ, 17 59.1]
doṣeṣu tāṃ vṛttimiyāya nando nirvāpaṇotpāṭanadāhaśoṣaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 59.2]
iti trivegaṃ trijhaṣaṃ trivīcam ekāmbhasaṃ pañcarayaṃ dvikūlam | [SaundĀ, 17 60.1]
dvigrāhamaṣṭāṅgavatā plavena duḥkhārṇavaṃ dustaramuttatāra | [SaundĀ, 17 60.2]
arhattvamāsādya sa satkriyārho nirutsuko niṣpraṇayo nirāśaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 61.1]
vibhīr viśug vītamado virāgaḥ sa eva dhṛtyānya ivābabhāse | [SaundĀ, 17 61.2]
bhrātuśca śāstuśca tayānuśiṣṭyā nandastataḥ svena ca vikrameṇa | [SaundĀ, 17 62.1]
praśāntacetāḥ paripūrṇakāryo vāṇīmimāmātmagatāṃ jagāda | [SaundĀ, 17 62.2]
namo 'stu tasmai sugatāya yena hitaiṣiṇā me karuṇātmakena | [SaundĀ, 17 63.1]
bahūni duḥkhānyapavartitāni sukhāni bhūyāṃsyupasaṃhṛtāni | [SaundĀ, 17 63.2]
ahaṃ hyanāryeṇa śarīrajena duḥkhātmake vartmani kṛṣyamāṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 64.1]
nivartitastadvacanāṅkuśena darpānvito nāga ivāṅkuśena | [SaundĀ, 17 64.2]
tasyājñayā kāruṇikasya śāsturhṛdisthamutpāṭya hi rāgaśalyam | [SaundĀ, 17 65.1]
adyaiva tāvat sumahat sukhaṃ me sarvakṣaye kiṃ bata nirvṛtasya | [SaundĀ, 17 65.2]
nirvāpya kāmāgnimahaṃ hi dīptaṃ dhṛtyambunā pāvakamambuneva | [SaundĀ, 17 66.1]
hlādaṃ paraṃ sāṃpratamāgato 'smi śītaṃ hradaṃ gharma ivāvatīrṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 66.2]
na me priyaṃ kiṃcana nāpriyaṃ me na me 'nurodho 'sti kuto virodhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 67.1]
tayorabhāvāt sukhito 'smi sadyo himātapābhyāmiva vipramuktaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 67.2]
mahābhayāt kṣemamivopalabhya mahāvarodhādiva vipramokṣam | [SaundĀ, 17 68.1]
mahārṇavāt pāramivāplavaḥ san bhīmāndhakārādiva ca prakāśam | [SaundĀ, 17 68.2]
rogādivārogyam asahyarūpād ṛṇādivānṛṇyam anantasaṃkhyāt | [SaundĀ, 17 69.1]
dviṣatsakāśādiva cāpayānaṃ durbhikṣayogācca yathā subhikṣam | [SaundĀ, 17 69.2]
tadvatparāṃ śāntimupāgato 'haṃ yasyānubhāvena vināyakasya | [SaundĀ, 17 70.1]
karomi bhūyaḥ punaruktamasmai namo namo 'rhāya tathāgatāya | [SaundĀ, 17 70.2]
yenāhaṃ girimupanīya rukmaśṛṅgaṃ svargaṃ ca plavagavadhūnidarśanena | [SaundĀ, 17 71.1]
kāmātmā tridivacarībhiraṅganābhirniṣkṛṣṭo yuvatimaye kalau nimagnaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 71.2]
tasmācca vyasanaparādanarthapaṅkādutkṛṣya kramaśithilaḥ karīva paṅkāt | [SaundĀ, 17 72.1]
śānte 'smin virajasi vijvare viśoke saddharme vitamasi naiṣṭhike vimuktaḥ | [SaundĀ, 17 72.2]
taṃ vande paramanukampakaṃ maharṣiṃ mūrdhnāhaṃ prakṛtiguṇajñamāśayajñam | [SaundĀ, 17 73.1]
saṃbuddhaṃ daśabalinaṃ bhiṣakpradhānaṃ trātāraṃ punarapi cāsmi saṃnatastam | [SaundĀ, 17 73.2]
{SaundĀ, 18}
atha dvijo bāla ivāptavedaḥ kṣipraṃ vaṇik prāpta ivāptalābhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 1.1]
jitvā ca rājanya ivārisainyaṃ nandaḥ kṛtārtho gurumabhyagacchat | [SaundĀ, 18 1.2]
draṣṭuṃ sukhaṃ jñānasamāptikāle gururhi śiṣyasya gurośca śiṣyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 2.1]
pariśramaste saphalo mayīti yato didṛkṣāsya munau babhūva | [SaundĀ, 18 2.2]
yato hi yenādhigato viśeṣastasyottamāṅge 'rhati kartumīḍyām | [SaundĀ, 18 3.1]
āryaḥ sarāgo 'pi kṛtajñabhāvāt prakṣīṇamānaḥ kimu vītarāgaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 3.2]
yasyārthakāmaprabhavā hi bhaktistato 'sya sā tiṣṭhati rūḍhamūlā | [SaundĀ, 18 4.1]
dharmānvayo yasya tu bhaktirāgastasya prasādo hṛdayāvagāḍhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 4.2]
kāṣāyavāsāḥ kanakāvadātastataḥ sa mūrdhnā gurave praṇeme | [SaundĀ, 18 5.1]
vāteritaḥ pallavatāmrarāgaḥ puṣpojjvalaśrīriva karṇikāraḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 5.2]
athātmanaḥ śiṣyaguṇasya caiva mahāmuneḥ śāstṛguṇasya caiva | [SaundĀ, 18 6.1]
saṃdarśanārthaṃ sa na mānahetoḥ svāṃ kāryasiddhiṃ kathayāṃbabhūva | [SaundĀ, 18 6.2]
yo dṛṣṭiśalyo hṛdayāvagāḍhaḥ prabho bhṛśaṃ māmatudat sutīkṣṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 7.1]
tvadvākyasaṃdaṃśamukhena me sa samuddhṛtaḥ śalyahṛteva śalyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 7.2]
kathaṃkathābhāvagato 'smi yena chinnaḥ sa niḥsaṃśaya saṃśayo me | [SaundĀ, 18 8.1]
tvacchāsanāt satpathamāgato 'smi sudeśikasyeva pathi pranaṣṭaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 8.2]
yatpītamāsvādavaśendriyeṇa darpeṇa kandarpaviṣaṃ mayāsīt | [SaundĀ, 18 9.1]
tanme hataṃ tvadvacanāgadena viṣaṃ vināśīva mahāgadena | [SaundĀ, 18 9.2]
kṣayaṃ gataṃ janma nirastajanman saddharmacaryāmuṣito 'smi samyak | [SaundĀ, 18 10.1]
kṛtsnaṃ kṛtaṃ me kṛtakārya kāryaṃ lokeṣu bhūto 'smi na lokadharmā | [SaundĀ, 18 10.2]
maitrīstanīṃ vyañjanacārusāsnāṃ saddharmadugdhāṃ pratibhānaśṛṅgām | [SaundĀ, 18 11.1]
tavāsmi gāṃ sādhu nipīya tṛptastṛṣeva gām uttamavatsavarṇaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 11.2]
yatpaśyataścādhigamo mamāyaṃ tanme samāsena mune nibodha | [SaundĀ, 18 12.1]
sarvajña kāmaṃ viditaṃ tavaitat svaṃ tūpacāraṃ pravivakṣurasmi | [SaundĀ, 18 12.2]
anye 'pi santo vimumukṣavo hi śrutvā vimokṣāya nayaṃ parasya | [SaundĀ, 18 13.1]
muktasya rogādiva rogavantastenaiva mārgeṇa sukhaṃ ghaṭante | [SaundĀ, 18 13.2]
urvyādikān janmani vedmi dhātūn nātmānamurvyādiṣu teṣu kiṃcit | [SaundĀ, 18 14.1]
yasmādatasteṣu na me 'sti saktirbahiśca kāyena samā matirme | [SaundĀ, 18 14.2]
skandhāṃśca rūpaprabhṛtīn daśārdhān paśyāmi yasmāccapalānasārān | [SaundĀ, 18 15.1]
anātmakāṃścaiva vadhātmakāṃśca tasmād vimukto 'smyaśivebhya ebhyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 15.2]
yasmācca paśyāmyudayaṃ vyayaṃ ca sarvāsvavasthāsvahamindriyāṇām | [SaundĀ, 18 16.1]
tasmādanityeṣu nirātmakeṣu duḥkheṣu me teṣvapi nāsti saṃgaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 16.2]
yataśca lokaṃ samajanmaniṣṭhaṃ paśyāmi niḥsāramasacca sarvam | [SaundĀ, 18 17.1]
ato dhiyā me manasā vibaddhamasmīti me neñjitamasti yena | [SaundĀ, 18 17.2]
caturvidhe naikavidhaprasaṅge yato 'hamāhāravidhāvasaktaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 18.1]
amūrchitaścāgrathitaśca tatra tribhyo vimukto 'smi tato bhavebhyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 18.2]
aniścitaścāpratibaddhacitto dṛṣṭaśrutādau vyavahāradharme | [SaundĀ, 18 19.1]
yasmāt samātmānugataśca tatra tasmād visaṃyogagato 'smi muktaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 19.2]
ityevamuktvā gurubāhumānyāt sarveṇa kāyena sa gāṃ nipannaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 20.1]
praverito lohitacandanākto haimo mahāstambha ivābabhāse | [SaundĀ, 18 20.2]
tataḥ pramādāt prasṛtasya pūrvaṃ śrutvā dhṛtiṃ vyākaraṇaṃ ca tasya | [SaundĀ, 18 21.1]
dharmānvayaṃ cānugataṃ prasādaṃ meghasvarastaṃ munirābabhāṣe | [SaundĀ, 18 21.2]
uttiṣṭha dharme sthita śiṣyajuṣṭe kiṃ pādayorme patito 'si mūrdhnā | [SaundĀ, 18 22.1]
abhyarcanaṃ me na tathā praṇāmo dharme yathaiṣā pratipattireva | [SaundĀ, 18 22.2]
adyāsi supravrajito jitātmannaiśvaryamapyātmani yena labdham | [SaundĀ, 18 23.1]
jitātmanaḥ pravrajanaṃ hi sādhu calātmano na tvajitendriyasya | [SaundĀ, 18 23.2]
adyāsi śaucena pareṇa yukto vākkāyacetāṃsi śucīni yatte | [SaundĀ, 18 24.1]
ataḥ punaścāprayatām asaumyāṃ yatsaumya no vekṣyasi garbhaśayyām | [SaundĀ, 18 24.2]
adyārthavatte śrutavacchrutaṃ tacchrutānurūpaṃ pratipadya dharmam | [SaundĀ, 18 25.1]
kṛtaśruto vipratipadyamāno nindyo hi nirvīrya ivāttaśastraḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 25.2]
aho dhṛtiste 'viṣayātmakasya yattvaṃ matiṃ mokṣavidhāvakārṣīḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 26.1]
yāsyāmi niṣṭhāmiti bāliśo hi janmakṣayāt trāsamihābhyupaiti | [SaundĀ, 18 26.2]
diṣṭyā durāpaḥ kṣaṇasaṃnipāto nāyaṃ kṛto mohavaśena moghaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 27.1]
udeti duḥkhena gato hyadhastāt kūrmo yugacchidra ivārṇavasthaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 27.2]
nirjitya māraṃ yudhi durnivāramadyāsi loke raṇaśīrṣaśūraḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 28.1]
śūro 'pyaśūraḥ sa hi veditavyo doṣairamitrairiva hanyate yaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 28.2]
nirvāpya rāgāgnimudīrṇamadya diṣṭyā sukhaṃ svapsyasi vītadāhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 29.1]
duḥkhaṃ hi śete śayane 'pyudāre kleśāgninā cetasi dahyamānaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 29.2]
abhyucchrito dravyamadena pūrvamadyāsi tṛṣṇoparamāt samṛddhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 30.1]
yāvat satarṣaḥ puruṣo hi loke tāvat samṛddho 'pi sadā daridraḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 30.2]
adyāpadeṣṭuṃ tava yuktarūpaṃ śuddhodano me nṛpatiḥ piteti | [SaundĀ, 18 31.1]
bhraṣṭasya dharmāt pitṛbhirnipātād aślāghanīyo hi kulāpadeśaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 31.2]
diṣṭyāsi śāntiṃ paramāmupeto nistīrṇakāntāra ivāptasāraḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 32.1]
sarvo hi saṃsāragato bhayārto yathaiva kāntāragatastathaiva | [SaundĀ, 18 32.2]
āraṇyakaṃ bhaikṣacaraṃ vinītaṃ drakṣyāmi nandaṃ nibhṛtaṃ kadeti | [SaundĀ, 18 33.1]
āsīt purastāttvayi me didṛkṣā tathāsi diṣṭyā mama darśanīyaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 33.2]
bhavatyarūpo 'pi hi darśanīyaḥ svalaṃkṛtaḥ śreṣṭhatamairguṇaiḥ svaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 34.1]
doṣaiḥ parīto malinīkaraistu sudarśanīyo 'pi virūpa eva | [SaundĀ, 18 34.2]
adya prakṛṣṭā tava buddhimattā kṛtsnaṃ yayā te kṛtamātmakāryam | [SaundĀ, 18 35.1]
śrutonnatasyāpi hi nāsti buddhirnotpadyate śreyasi yasya buddhiḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 35.2]
unmīlitasyāpi janasya madhye nimīlitasyāpi tathaiva cakṣuḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 36.1]
prajñāmayaṃ yasya hi nāsti cakṣuścakṣurna tasyāsti sacakṣuṣo 'pi | [SaundĀ, 18 36.2]
duḥkhapratīkāranimittamārtaḥ kṛṣyādibhiḥ khedamupaiti lokaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 37.1]
ajasramāgacchati tacca bhūyo jñānena yasyādya kṛtastvayāntaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 37.2]
duḥkhaṃ na me syāt sukhameva me syāditi pravṛttaḥ satataṃ hi lokaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 38.1]
na vetti taccaiva tathā yathā syāt prāptaṃ tvayādyāsulabhaṃ yathāvat | [SaundĀ, 18 38.2]
ityevamādi sthirabuddhicittastathāgatenābhihito hitāya | [SaundĀ, 18 39.1]
staveṣu nindāsu ca nirvyapekṣaḥ kṛtāñjalirvākyamuvāca nandaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 39.2]
aho viśeṣeṇa viśeṣadarśin tvayānukampā mayi darśiteyaṃ | [SaundĀ, 18 40.1]
yatkāmapaṅke bhagavannimagnastrāto 'smi saṃsārabhayādakāmaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 40.2]
bhrātrā tvayā śreyasi daiśikena pitrā phalasthena tathaiva mātrā | [SaundĀ, 18 41.1]
hato 'bhaviṣyaṃ yadi na vyamokṣyaṃ sārthāt paribhraṣṭa ivākṛtārthaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 41.2]
śāntasya tuṣṭasya sukho viveko vijñātatattvasya parīkṣakasya | [SaundĀ, 18 42.1]
prahīṇamānasya ca nirmadasya sukhaṃ virāgatvamasaktabuddheḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 42.2]
atho hi tattvaṃ parigamya samyaṅnirdhūya doṣānadhigamya śāntim | [SaundĀ, 18 43.1]
svaṃ nāśrayaṃ samprati cintayāmi na taṃ janaṃ nāpsaraso na devān | [SaundĀ, 18 43.2]
idaṃ hi bhuktvā śuci śāmikaṃ sukhaṃ na me manaḥ kāṅkṣati kāmajaṃ sukham | [SaundĀ, 18 44.1]
mahārhamapyannam adaivatāhṛtaṃ divaukaso bhuktavataḥ sudhāmiva | [SaundĀ, 18 44.2]
aho 'ndhavijñānanimīlitaṃ jagat paṭāntare paśyati nottamaṃ sukham | [SaundĀ, 18 45.1]
sudhīram adhyātmasukhaṃ vyapāsya hi śramaṃ tathā kāmasukhārthamṛcchati | [SaundĀ, 18 45.2]
yathā hi ratnākarametya durmatirvihāya ratnānyasato maṇīn haret | [SaundĀ, 18 46.1]
apāsya saṃbodhisukhaṃ tathottamaṃ śramaṃ vrajet kāmasukhopalabdhaye | [SaundĀ, 18 46.2]
aho hi sattveṣvatimaitracetasas tathāgatasyānujighṛkṣutā parā | [SaundĀ, 18 47.1]
apāsya yaddhyānasukhaṃ mune paraṃ parasya duḥkhoparamāya khidyase | [SaundĀ, 18 47.2]
mayā nu śakyaṃ pratikartumadya kiṃ gurau hitaiṣiṇyanukampake tvayi | [SaundĀ, 18 48.1]
samuddhṛto yena bhavārṇavādahaṃ mahārṇavāccūrṇitanaurivormibhiḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 48.2]
tato munistasya niśamya hetumat prahīṇasarvāsravasūcakaṃ vacaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 49.1]
idaṃ babhāṣe vadatāmanuttamo yadarhati śrīghana eva bhāṣituṃ | [SaundĀ, 18 49.2]
idaṃ kṛtārthaḥ paramārthavit kṛtī tvameva dhīmannabhidhātumarhasi | [SaundĀ, 18 50.1]
atītya kāntāramavāptasādhanaḥ sudaiśikasyeva kṛtaṃ mahāvaṇik | [SaundĀ, 18 50.2]
avaiti buddhaṃ naradamyasārathiṃ kṛtī yathārhannupaśāntamānasaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 51.1]
na dṛṣṭasatyo 'pi tathāvabudhyate pṛthagjanaḥ kiṃ bata buddhimānapi | [SaundĀ, 18 51.2]
rajastamobhyāṃ parimuktacetasastavaiva ceyaṃ sadṛśī kṛtajñatā | [SaundĀ, 18 52.1]
rajaḥprakarṣeṇa jagatyavasthite kṛtajñabhāvo hi kṛtajña durlabhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 52.2]
sadharma dharmānvayato yataśca te mayi prasādo 'dhigame ca kauśalam | [SaundĀ, 18 53.1]
ato 'sti bhūyastvayi me vivakṣitaṃ nato hi bhaktaśca niyogamarhasi | [SaundĀ, 18 53.2]
avāptakāryo 'si parāṃ gatiṃ gato na te 'sti kiṃcit karaṇīyamaṇvapi | [SaundĀ, 18 54.1]
ataḥparaṃ saumya carānukampayā vimokṣayan kṛcchragatān parānapi | [SaundĀ, 18 54.2]
ihārthamevārabhate naro 'dhamo vimadhyamastūbhayalaukikīṃ kriyām | [SaundĀ, 18 55.1]
kriyāmamutraiva phalāya madhyamo viśiṣṭadharmā punarapravṛttaye | [SaundĀ, 18 55.2]
ihottamebhyo 'pi mataḥ sa tūttamo ya uttamaṃ dharmamavāpya naiṣṭhikam | [SaundĀ, 18 56.1]
acintayitvātmagataṃ pariśramaṃ śamaṃ parebhyo 'pyupadeṣṭumicchati | [SaundĀ, 18 56.2]
vihāya tasmādiha kāryamātmanaḥ kuru sthirātman parakāryamapyatho | [SaundĀ, 18 57.1]
bhramatsu sattveṣu tamāvṛtātmasu śrutapradīpo niśi dhāryatāmayam | [SaundĀ, 18 57.2]
bravītu tāvat puri vismito janastvayi sthite kurvati dharmadeśanāḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 58.1]
aho batāścaryamidaṃ vimuktaye karoti rāgī yadayaṃ kathāmiti | [SaundĀ, 18 58.2]
dhruvaṃ hi saṃśrutya tava sthiraṃ mano nivṛttanānāviṣayairmanorathaiḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 59.1]
vadhūrgṛhe sāpi tavānukurvatī kariṣyate strīṣu virāgiṇīḥ kathāḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 59.2]
tvayi paramadhṛtau niviṣṭatattve bhavanagatā na hi raṃsyate dhruvaṃ sā | [SaundĀ, 18 60.1]
manasi śamadamātmake vivikte matiriva kāmasukhaiḥ parīkṣakasya | [SaundĀ, 18 60.2]
ityarhataḥ paramakāruṇikasya śāsturmūrdhnā vacaśca caraṇau ca samaṃ gṛhītvā | [SaundĀ, 18 61.1]
svasthaḥ praśāntahṛdayo vinivṛttakāryaḥ pārśvānmuneḥ pratiyayau vimadaḥ karīva | [SaundĀ, 18 61.2]
bhikṣārthaṃ samaye viveśa sa puraṃ dṛṣṭīrjanasyākṣipan lābhālābhasukhāsukhādiṣu samaḥ svasthendriyo nispṛhaḥ | [SaundĀ, 18 62.1]
nirmokṣāya cakāra tatra ca kathāṃ kāle janāyārthine naivonmārgagatān parān paribhavannātmānamutkarṣayan | [SaundĀ, 18 62.2]
ityeṣā vyupaśāntaye na rataye mokṣārthagarbhā kṛtiḥ śrotṝṇāṃ grahaṇārthamanyamanasāṃ kāvyopacārāt kṛtā | [SaundĀ, 18 63.1]
yanmokṣāt kṛtamanyadatra hi mayā tatkāvyadharmāt kṛtaṃ pātuṃ tiktam ivauṣadhaṃ madhuyutaṃ hṛdyaṃ kathaṃ syāditi | [SaundĀ, 18 63.2]
prāyeṇālokya lokaṃ viṣayaratiparaṃ mokṣāt pratihataṃ kāvyavyājena tattvaṃ kathitamiha mayā mokṣaḥ paramiti | [SaundĀ, 18 64.1]
tadbuddhvā śāmikaṃ yattadavahitamito grāhyaṃ na lalitaṃ pāṃsubhyo dhātujebhyo niyatam upakaraṃ cāmīkaramiti | [SaundĀ, 18 64.2]
